  • Who Let Him Cultivate?!-Chapter 1074 - 1073 What’s the use of this broken box!

After breaking free from the torrent of time, Lu Yang found himself riding on the back of the Nian Beast Clan Leader, surrounded by fiery red clouds that matched the color of the Nian Beasts perfectly.

The Nian Beasts, wrapped in the fiery red clouds, shuttled and played around the world, invisible to all.

"Fairy, did you see the vision just now?" Lu Yang’s heart skipped a beat. In some time in the future, a box-world would open, meaning that the Dao Fruits of the Five Ancient Immortals had all been gathered, and the hidden enemy was vanquished— or could it be that the powers of Great Qian had gathered the Dao Fruits of the Five Ancient Immortals?

"Ah, what? What did you just say?" Fairy Eternity sounded as if she was still sleepy, her consciousness drifting.

"I was asking if you saw the vision just now?" Lu Yang didn’t think too much about it; the Fairy hadn’t been herself only since today.

"The vision just now was of me... wait, what did you see?" Fairy Eternity suddenly remembered what the Time Immortal had told her about observing the future; each person’s vision of the future might not be the same.

"It’s about the box-world opening up. Why, did we see something different?"

"The same, of course the same."

"Time Immortal once told me about this phenomenon, saying that if you’re caught in the torrent of time, you can see the past and the future. What has passed is certain, but the future is uncertain. The future we see is just one of many possibilities."

"So that’s how it is."

"So, did you see the future?" the Nian Beast Clan Leader carrying Lu Yang laughed.

"I’ve already told you, being able to see us Nian Beasts is a chance many can’t even beg for."

"So, what did you see, kid? Did you see yourself becoming a Great Cultivator, or did you envision a harem of wives?" The Nian Beast Clan Leader asked with a laugh, not out of curiosity, but merely finding the topic interesting. Lu Yang pondered for a moment; despite its fearsome appearance, the Clan Leader was a good beast. There was no need to hide this from the Nian Beast Clan Leader.

"I saw the box-world being opened."

No sooner had Lu Yang finished speaking than he felt the Nian Beast Clan Leader he was riding on abruptly stop, and he was flung forward by inertia, tumbling a couple of times before coming to rest in front of the Clan Leader.

"What did you say?!" The Nian Beast Clan Leader looked at Lu Yang in astonishment. Based on experience, the future seen by people who enter the torrent of time is always closely linked to themselves.

The other Nian Beasts also showed faces of disbelief at this news.

Although the future Lu Yang saw was only a possibility, even as a mere possibility, it was terrifying.

Could it be that the opening of the box-world was intertwined with this youngster’s fate?!

What did this youngster do in the future?

"The world was opened, is there a problem?" Lu Yang was utterly puzzled, not understanding why the Nian Beasts were reacting so strongly.

"Fairy, do you know the reason?"

"Not a clue." Fairy Eternity didn’t think there was anything to it. Little Yang had revived her first, then found the Yingtian Immortal, and who knows whom he might find next. Wasn’t it quite normal for Little Yang to share a causal connection with the opening of the box-world?

"Nothing, nothing at all." The Nian Beast Clan Leader, realizing his own overreaction, hastily reassured that everything was fine.

The Nian Beasts cherished their freedom above all else and dreaded nothing more than coming into contact with someone with significant causality like Lu Yang, lest they get entangled in that causality themselves.

"By the way, I forgot to ask earlier, are you from the Seek Dao Sect?"

"Yes."

"Then do you know Yun Zhi?"

"I do, she’s my Eldest Senior Sister."

"Hahaha, so that’s how it is, my apologies. It seems we’ve had a fateful encounter, we shall meet again!"

The Nian Beast Clan Leader no longer had the desire to carry Lu Yang around for fun. A person of great causality, and also the Junior Brother of a major demon—it was better to stay away from him!

The Nian Beasts, riding on the fiery clouds, swiftly fled, leaving Lu Yang alone where he stood.

```

"Wait, at least send me back first!" Lu Yang chased the fire-cloud riding Nian Beast as the Clan Leader flew with him for half a day. Where had he taken him?

However, even Yun Zhi couldn’t catch up with the time-traveling Nian Beast, how could Lu Yang possibly catch up?

Lu Yang pursued but shortly lost sight of the Nian Beast’s figure and had no choice but to give up.

"Speaking of which, where is this place?"

Lu Yang noticed a bustling city not far away, filled with fireworks bursting in the air in vibrant colors: swastika shapes, lotus shapes, and Buddha Beads shapes — all incredibly beautiful. From where Lu Yang stood, he could clearly hear the sounds of fireworks from the city.

The city was surrounded by boundless desert.

Lu Yang landed and approached the city, looking up to see two large characters engraved above the city gate.

Western Heaven.

...

"This is bad, the Second-in-command has been captured by the Nian Beast!" Yun Mengmeng saw the Second-in-command disappear before her eyes. Recalling that he had just boasted about fighting the Nian Beast, panic set in.

"Oh no, oh no, oh no... That’s right, seek help from Xiao Zhi."

With this thought, Yun Mengmeng flew out of Seek Dao Sect like the wind, leaving Li Haoran standing there, still clueless.

He hadn’t yet figured out why Lu Yang had brought him here.

"Senior Brother Lu has been captured by the Nian Beast, is that a New Year’s tradition or something?"

Worried about Lu Yangxin, Yun Mengmeng hurried away from Seek Dao Sect, heading straight for her old home, the Peach Blossom Secret Realm.

She flew over a lake and with a splash, she dived into the water, swimming straight to the bottom.

The Secret Realm sensed Yun Mengmeng’s arrival and a whirlpool appeared on the lake bottom, sucking her in.

Back home, Yun Mengmeng was greeted by the familiar scent of peach blossoms. The Peach Blossom Secret Realm was warm and welcoming, with peach trees blooming everywhere, fragrance hanging heavy in the air.

The rivers branched out like tree limbs, and the surface of the water emitted a dense fog of Spiritual Energy, maintaining the concentration. The entire Secret Realm’s concentration of Spiritual Energy was comparable to that of the Five Great Immortal Sects.

"Mengmeng." People of the Secret Realm smiled and waved at Yun Mengmeng, who were also celebrating New Year’s, frolicking and welcoming the new year.

"Senior Sister Nianger, where’s Xiao Zhi?" Yun Mengmeng asked urgently.

"Xiao Zhi? She should be with Granny. What’s the hurry, why do you need her?"

"It’s urgent, I’ll explain later."

When Yun Mengmeng found Yun Zhi, she was leisurely chatting with Granny, recounting tales of the outside world.

"Mengmeng is back? Come, sit by Granny," Granny beckoned with a smile.

Despite being called Granny, she looked remarkably young, around twenty-something, and was very composed in her actions.

"Hmm? Mengmeng, why are you here?" Yun Zhi asked as she set down her teacup, slightly puzzled.

"Happy New Year, Granny, I’ve got an emergency and can’t stay," Yun Mengmeng said.

"It’s serious, Xiao Zhi. The Second-in-command has been taken away by the Nian Beast!"

"Really? What happened?"

"Well, the Second-in-command and I were watching fireworks, and all of a sudden, he rolled on the ground with a ’clang’, then swiftly pinned something down, saying it was the Nian Beast. Afterwards, I don’t know how, but the Second-in-command jumped up and brought Li Haoran over, like he introduced him to someone. And then, ’whoosh’, as if something snatched him up, he just vanished."

Yun Zhi set down her teacup, ignoring the onomatopoeic words in Yun Mengmeng’s description, and thoughtfully said, "I see, so that’s what happened. No worries, it should be fine."

```

"Why am I in Western Heaven during Chinese New Year?"

Lu Yang had a strange expression. Although he practiced cultivation, he wasn’t superstitious. However, the implications of his current situation were not very auspicious.

Initially, Lu Yang was startled by the words "Western Heaven," but then he understood. Here lay Western Heaven City, managed by the Western Paradise Temple, which held a status equivalent to that of Great Xia Imperial City.

"Does the Nian Beast run so fast? It brought me to Western Heaven City in an instant?" Lu Yang felt that he hadn’t been riding on the back of the Nian Beast Clan Leader for long.

Since it was rare for him to visit Western Heaven City during Chinese New Year, and considering his treatment in Kaihuang City, Lu Yang thought it wouldn’t hurt to stroll around Western Paradise Temple.

"Hello, I’d like to enter the city."

Even on New Year’s Eve, the gates of Western Heaven City were wide open, with monks guarding the gates.

Lu Yang handed his identity proof to the gatekeeping monks.

"Lu Yang?"

The monk was startled by the name on the certificate and then, upon seeing Lu Yang’s familiar face, became even more surprised.

Could this be the legendary Lu Yang?

Lu Yang entered the city without any hindrances.

"Leaving Buddha Country is just a hassle; I’ll have to sneak across the border."

Lu Yang sighed. There was no other way; he didn’t have a departure record, only an entry record. How could he explain that?

Even if he told the Great Xia officials that he was forcibly taken out of the country by the Nian Beast, probably no one would believe him except for Jiang Pingan.

"Western Heaven City is quite lively."

Lu Yang walked leisurely, taking in the sights. The New Year atmosphere here was much stronger than at the Seek Dao Sect; at least the fireworks here wouldn’t kill anyone.

Children could be seen crouching on the ground lighting fireworks everywhere. Lu Yang, who hadn’t played with them for a long time, felt the itch in his hands and squatted down to join the children in lighting fireworks.

Sometimes Lu Yang would find unlit fireworks amongst the debris, picking them up one by one, clutching them in his palm, walking along while lighting them with the Three Flavored True Fire and tossing them aside, much amused.

The dull sound of the bell tolled, a myriad of fireworks ascending into the sky and exploding simultaneously, scattering golden sparks as cheers and Buddhist chants arose steadily throughout the city.

The New Year had arrived.

Lu Yang followed the sound of the bell toward Western Paradise Temple, from which the ringing emanated.

The Spiritual Space was equally bustling with activity—lively music, the booming of drums, the crackle of firecrackers—while Immortal Fairy Eternity cheerfully said Happy New Year amidst the hubbub.

"Also, Second-in-command, you’ve been exposed, it’s time to prepare to run," Immortal Fairy Eternity kindly added.

"Ah? Fairy, what did you say? I can’t hear you clearly!" Lu Yang shouted; the Spiritual Space was incredibly noisy.

He vaguely heard Immortal Fairy Eternity saying something intermittently about "every house’s head, to run."

In reality, suddenly a Buddha Light enveloped an area, and then it shrank, covering only Lu Yang.

A monk clad in a kasaya chanted Amitabha and then addressed the Buddha Light-covered Lu Yang, "Lu Yang Benefactor graces us with his presence. Western Paradise Temple regrets not having welcomed you from afar; would you care to join this humble monk as our guest at the temple?"

He had received a message from the guard monks that Lu Yang, the genius of the Seek Dao Sect, was visiting Western Heaven City, and as an Elder of Western Paradise Temple, it was only natural for him to personally welcome Lu Yang.

Suddenly another monk flew in with an unfriendly expression: "Elder Kong Chan, you arrived quite fast."

"Junior Brother Kong Xing flatters me."

Elder Kong Xing sneered: "Hmph, don’t think I don’t know you’re trying to use Lu Yang to find out Ye Zijin’s whereabouts."

Elder Kong Chan replied unhurriedly, "Do you share the same thought, Junior Brother?"

"Elders Kong Chan, Kong Xing, what brings you here?" Another Elder of Western Paradise Temple flew in. While addressing them, his gaze kept drifting towards Lu Yang.

More and more Elders flew over from Western Paradise Temple, causing Lu Yang’s eyes to twitch.

"So, what if I said I don’t know where my Second Senior Brother is, would you believe me?"

"Hehe, since Lu Yang Benefactor has visited our Western Paradise Temple, we shall believe him."

Hearing this, Lu Yang took to his heels and ran. This group of Elders had clearly set their sights on the relationship between him and his Second Senior Brother, determined to acquire something from him.

Handling one Elder was manageable, but who could withstand a whole group of Elders? If he didn’t run now, it would be too late!

"Chase!"

As soon as the many Elders saw Lu Yang trying to flee, they couldn’t let that happen. Displaying their Divine Abilities, Buddha Light soared to the sky, Arhats chanted scriptures, Guanyin saved souls, Worldly Venerables enlightened... Miracles abounded, instantly illuminating Western Heaven City as bright as day, and even the King of Ghosts would be purified here.

The clueless citizens, witnessing this spectacle, all came out to worship, creating a commotion that was even livelier than the New Year celebrations with bell-ringing and fireworks.

Lu Yang used Earth Shrinking to burrow into the ground, fleeing in all directions, occasionally having to change his course to evade the encircling pursuit.

"Isn’t this New Year’s Eve a bit too eventful?"

He had simply wanted to live in peace and enjoy the New Year, but who would have thought he’d encounter the Nian Beast, get swept into the currents of time, and then bewilderingly arrive at Western Paradise Temple to be warmly entertained by a group of Elders?

In terms of speed among his peers, Lu Yang was unquestionably unmatched, even the Kunpeng Clan might not meet his pace.

But this was the Western Paradise Temple, where the skies were filled with Combined Great Abilities; even with the power of three heads and six arms, he couldn’t escape.

"This won’t do, I need to think of a plan."

Lu Yang had a flash of inspiration, flipped over the high wall, created a Bodhi Wood avatar to attract attention, while his true form hid in the Green Blade Sword Small World, dropping to the ground, camouflaging as an ordinary sword.

The design of the Green Peak Sword wasn’t particularly lavish, and no one would recognize the grade of the sword.

As Lu Yang expected, the Spiritual Sense of the Western Paradise Temple Elders swept over the area several times, yet no one took notice of the ordinary longsword lying on the ground, stained with soil.

"Hmm, why is there a sword here?" The Young Monk, after finishing in the restroom, accidentally noticed an ordinary longsword lying in the bushes.

"There’s no name on the sword, did a layperson drop it here?"

"But were there any laypeople at our Temple of Miscellaneous Affairs today?"

The Young Monk was puzzled; he didn’t know much about swords but knew that the owner would be anxious about losing their possession.

"I should hand it over to the Manager."

Upon hearing this, Lu Yang realized that in his haste to hide, he had not paid attention to his surroundings and had vaulted over the wall to hide within the sword—turns out he was at the Western Paradise Temple.

However, he couldn’t let the little monk hand him over to the Manager.

"Hehe, you have a kind heart for a little monk."

"Who’s there!" The Young Monk jumped with fright, apprehensive.

"Stop looking around; it is I who am speaking."

The Young Monk’s pupils shrank immediately, almost throwing the sword away in fear.

The sword was speaking!

"Who, who are you? I must tell you, this is Western Paradise Temple!"

"Hehe, how does that matter to me—can Western Paradise Temple do anything to me?"

"Who, who exactly are you?"

"I am Tofu Heavenly Venerable, have you, little monk, heard of my name?"

The Young Monk showed a puzzled expression.

Noticing the Young Monk’s expression, the consciousness within the sword felt somewhat desolate.

"Countless ages in the blink of an eye, the mortal world’s past turns to smoke. Did I, who once reigned supreme over the heavens, joyously soaring through the skies, befriending heaven and earth, shining alongside the sun and the moon, witness the eons, to now awaken and find that the people of later generations no longer know of me?"

"Tofu Heavenly Venerable?"

Upon hearing the entity within the sword recount its past, the young monk had quite a shock; this was indeed an extraordinary existence.

He racked his brains for a long time, but still could not think of any great power from ancient times who bore the name "Tofu."

"Ah, let it be, let it be, it seems even I cannot escape the fate of being nameless through the ages."

With a long sigh, Tofu Heavenly Venerable expressed either his lament for the heartlessness of time or his reminiscence of that carefree era.

"It’s just unfortunate that my involvement with causality is too profound. Should it surface today, I fear it might trigger a cataclysmic immortal battle, and this little Western Paradise Temple would be reduced to ruins."

"Then, what should we do?" The young monk had not expected that the sword he picked up at random would involve so many issues. He trembled, deeply afraid of triggering some significant causality.

"I currently dwell within this immortal sword to neutralize causality. As long as you, young monk, do not disclose anything about me, no trouble will occur."

"That’s good, that’s good. My lips are sealed; I definitely won’t speak of the senior’s matters," the young monk hurriedly said.

"That would be best."

After this, no more sounds came from the sword; whether Tofu Heavenly Venerable was too lazy to speak or had fallen asleep was unknown.

Knowing the origins of Tofu Heavenly Venerable, the young monk dared not neglect his duty nor entertain the thought of discarding the immortal sword. He carefully held the sword and tiptoed back to his meditation chamber.

The chamber was a large communal sleeping area for six or seven individuals. The young monk quietly found a clean, long piece of cloth, wrapped up the Green Peak Sword, placed it next to his pillow in his designated spot, and then went to sleep.

...

"Xin Ding, why did you take so long to go to the restroom last night?" Upon waking up in the morning, while the young monk was getting dressed, his companion inquired.

He had slept vaguely last night, could not remember how long the young monk had been gone to the restroom, but felt it was quite a while.

"Amitabha, monks don’t lie."

"So?"

"So I cannot tell." The young monk earnestly responded, knowing he couldn’t disclose the matters regarding Tofu Heavenly Venerable, as that could lead to the destruction of the Western Paradise Temple; he now bore the responsibility of saving it.

"Ah?"

Having woken up, put on his clothes, and eaten a light breakfast, the young monk attended morning classes to chant scriptures. Along with the other servant monks, he fetched water, chopped wood, and cleaned the grounds. After all that, he sat down to meditate.

"Young monk, are you engaged in visualization?" An ancient and muffled voice came from the immortal sword; Tofu Heavenly Venerable noticed that the young monk had a foundation in cultivation, roughly at the fifth level of Qi Refinement.

Before the young monk, there lay a yellowed Arhat Demon Suppression Map, which he was using for his visualization to stimulate his spiritual sense.

In the Cultivation World, the visualization method is commonly used to grow spiritual sense. Meng Jingzhou’s method of constantly suppressing his instincts to enhance spiritual sense was one used by very few.

The young monk was startled, looking around and realizing that whether it was Senior Brothers and Junior Brothers meditating, or the Deacon Master, none could hear the Venerate’s voice.

"Stop looking; this is a spiritual sense transmission, others can’t hear it."

Only then did the young monk reply, "Yes, Heavenly Venerate."

"This is the most basic visualization map. To obtain a better one, you need to contribute to the temple and exchange Merit Points to get it."

The young monk shyly smiled, "But this Arhat Demon Suppression Map is already very good, said to be handed down from Ancient Times."

Naturally, what the young monk held was not an original, but merely a copy of an ancient visualization map.

"These things are also worthy of being called visualization maps." Tofu Heavenly Venerable shook his head, clearly unimpressed by the young monk’s method.

"Since you’ve met me, it means you’re destined to be associated with me. I will impart to you a genuine ancient visualization map, lest in the future people say I’ve lost face."

Tofu Heavenly Venerable used his Spiritual Sense as a seal, imprinting an image within the young monk’s mind.

"What is this?!"

The young monk closed his eyes, and the imprint of Tofu Heavenly Venerable’s Spiritual Sense appeared in his mind.

It was a golden divine Dragon soaring between heaven and earth, a naturally supreme being, far more imposing than any depiction of a True Dragon the young monk had ever seen in books. With a furrow of its eyebrows, the divine Dragon summoned a sky full of Immortal Thunder, as if heaven and earth were altered by its will.

"This is one of the five founders of Buddhism, whom I had the fortune to meet several times. This visualization can be called the Yinglong Visualization."

One of the five founders of Buddhism!

The young monk heard these five significant words and was greatly shocked inside his heart. Weren’t the founders of Buddhism the Worldly Venerable? How did it become five people in the words of the Heavenly Venerable?!

The young monk contemplated Venerable Ying Long and found that the effect on the Spiritual Sense was far superior to the Arhat Demon Suppression Map!

Generally speaking, the more powerful the figure in the visualization and the greater their impact on the world, the better the effect of the visualization if it is related to the viewer’s Cultivation Technique.

Such good effects indicated that the True Dragon in the visualization was connected to Buddhist teaching, and its status within Buddhism was absolutely exalted!

Indeed one of the founders of Buddhism!

The young monk increasingly felt that Tofu Heavenly Venerable was profoundly enigmatic, as this casually given item had overturned his understanding.

"May I ask, Heavenly Venerable, what exactly is the matter with the five founders of Buddhism?"

"Your Cultivation Level is too low; it is not yet time for you to know the secrets of Ancient Times."

"Yes."

From the perspective of visualization methods, actually, Lu Yang was also engaging in visualization, except his object was the Immortal Fairy rather than any pictorial image.

It was akin to Lu Yang being in constant contemplation; naturally, his Spiritual Sense far surpassed his peers.

"Speaking of which, I still don’t know what this little monk is called."

"This humble monk is Xin Ding, a servant monk in the Servant Monks Institute."

"Subduing the mind and stabilizing the world, a fine dharma name."

With the mysterious Tofu Heavenly Venerable presenting an ancient visualization, the young monk Xin Ding felt his Spiritual Sense Cultivation advancing at an unprecedented rate, experiencing an exhilarating feeling like never before.

Several days passed, and Xin Ding’s Spiritual Sense grew increasingly powerful, transforming his essence, Qi, and spirit, although the other servant monks who interacted with him daily failed to notice this subtle change.

One day, as Xin Ding finished his contemplation and walked out of his Zen room, suddenly a stone flew at him, aiming directly at his forehead.

Xin Ding, sensing something, tilted his head and dodged the blow.

"Xin Ding Junior Brother, your skills seem quite impressive these days," several servant monks said tauntingly, with the leader still clutching several stones in his hand.

"So it is Xin Cheng Senior Brother." Xin Ding responded nonchalantly, as if unaware that Xin Cheng had intentionally thrown the stone at him, causing Xin Cheng to feel as if his punch had landed on cotton, unable to exert any force.

"It’s Xin Cheng, what is he doing here?"

"Don’t you know? The selection at the Martial Monk Institute is soon, and he is all over the place snatching Merit Points to exchange for items to prepare for the selection!"

"I also heard that he is acquainted with a Senior Brother from the Martial Monk Institute, who gifted him a Fragmented Map of ’Elephants Crossing the River’."

"What, it’s actually the Fragmented Map of ’Elephants Crossing the River’? That’s a visualization that we servant monks couldn’t afford in half a lifetime!"

"Yes, it seems Junior Brother Xin Ding might be in trouble."

"Xin Ding, Junior Brother, I see that your movements are nimble, surely you’ve made some breakthroughs recently," Xin Cheng said with a cold smirk. "Why don’t we have a match? It’s the customary rule here in the Servant Monk Institute; the loser must give the winner ten Merit Points."

If Xin Ding refused, he would keep harassing Xin Ding, making it impossible for him to accomplish anything!

"Very well, Senior Brother has invited me, how could I possibly refuse?"

Xin Cheng was stunned, not expecting Xin Ding to agree so readily.

But that was also good, it saved time, and with the Martial Monk Institute selection coming soon, it was best to save time.

Seeing that the two were about to start fighting, some astute students quickly ran out to find the Deacon Master to intervene.

"Please, Xin Ding Junior Brother," Xin Cheng said insincerely, but Xin Ding was not one to exchange courtesies, he struck as soon as he said the word.

Both disciples from the Servant Monk Institute practiced Bodhi Fist, which was the most basic form of boxing, and Xin Ding and Xin Cheng were no exceptions.

Xin Ding attacked first; his Spiritual Sense had greatly improved, allowing for better control over his body, making his execution of the Bodhi Fist techniques more precise.

Xin Cheng was shocked. The punch was both swift and fierce. When had Xin Ding’s boxing become so powerful?

"Look, isn’t Junior Brother Xin Ding dominating Senior Brother Xin Cheng?"

"That shouldn’t be, doesn’t Senior Brother Xin Cheng possess the Fragmented Map of ’Fragrant Elephant Crossing the River’?"

"Could it be that Senior Brother Xin Cheng hasn’t seriously contemplated the Enlightenment Vision Diagram since he obtained it?"

Hearing the surrounding discussions, Xin Cheng felt so frustrated he wanted to spit blood. He had been contemplating since he obtained the vision diagram; logically, no one at the fifth level of Qi Refinement in the Servant Monk Institute should have been able to defeat him, so how could the inconspicuous Xin Ding come out on top?

Xin Cheng became disoriented, and his moves, both fists and kicks, were sloppy, even worse than before he owned the ’Fragrant Elephant Crossing the River’ Fragmented Map.

Seizing the opportunity, Xin Ding widened his stance and landed an Exploding Punch that sent Xin Cheng flying.

The crowd was in uproar as Xin Cheng, who had high hopes of entering the Martial Monk Institute, lost the match!

"Stop it all, what are you doing, Xin Cheng!" a voice from the outskirts of the crowd called out—it was the Deacon Master’s voice. Everyone quickly stepped aside to make way.

The spiritual essence in the Small World was completely frozen, unable to be refined; this was the End of Dharma Era mentioned in the Buddhist scriptures, a struggle at the world’s end. During the End of Dharma Era, spiritual essence could not be harnessed, cultivators could no longer cultivate, and they were thoroughly reduced to mortals.

"Five Ghosts Moving Mountains, Six Generals Supporting Heaven!"

Venerable Qing Yan summoned eleven giant figures, taller even than when Meng Jingzhou displayed his full Dharma Aspect.

The middle-aged man’s face showed despair. Was this the legendary ultimate move of Venerable Qing Yan, that supposedly left everyone who saw it with a slim chance of survival?

The mountains moved by the Five Ghosts and the heavens supported by the Six Generals weren’t truly existent. They were formed of humanity’s evil thoughts - noisy, angry, sorrowful... frёewebnoѵēl.com

Bathed in humanity’s malevolence, even one who survived by luck would turn utterly insane.

Fairy Eternity pouted, somewhat impatiently: "What a complete mess, Arhat Fruit Fist."

Fairy Eternity launched an Immortal Fist Technique, and with the Arhat Fruit Fist—carrying a purifying intent—with just one punch, the entire Small World was instantly rejuvenated, as if spring had returned to the earth, warm and blooming.

What End of Dharma Era, with its miles of frozen evil and turbidity—all vanished without a trace, replaced by a new world teeming with life.

"Bodhi Leaf Fist."

Fairy Eternity’s fist technique changed, and the Bodhi Leaf Fist, aiding restful sleep and equally potent in purification, washed away the maliciously condensed mountains and skies with an immense tide of purifying intent, erasing the negative emotions completely.

"What kind of fist technique is this?!"

Venerable Qing Yan was astounded, Arhat Fruit Fist, Bodhi Leaf Fist, they sounded nonsensical, how could they possibly possess such power?!

"Qing Yan Dissolves into the Clear Sky!"

Seeing he was no match, Venerable Qing Yan made a snap decision and resorted to his Escape Skill. This top-notch skill had once allowed him to slip away from Master Ming Yu, capable of creating a illusory clone to deceive his opponent, while his true form transformed into a wisp of Qing Yan, disappearing without a trace, eluding anyone’s search!

"What’s that, you call this an escape skill? Time Immortal’s and Yingtian Immortal’s escape skills are much better than yours."

Fairy Eternity clasped her hands together, interlocking her fingers. Venerable Qing Yan, who thought he had vanished like smoke in thin air, was pinched into form, forced back to his original appearance.

"What kind of technique is this, who exactly are you?!"

Desperation filled the eyes of Venerable Qing Yan. This was an opponent on an entirely different level compared to Master Ming Yu. He could understand the moves of Ming Yu, but every technique Fairy Eternity used was beyond his comprehension!

"You are not worthy of knowing who this Immortal is, fix."

Fairy Eternity uttered the word "fix," and Venerable Qing Yan was struck with alarm; could this be the legendary Fixation Technique?

But he tried to struggle and found he was not fixed in place.

Fairy Eternity’s expression darkened: "If you dare move a bit, you’re as good as dead."

Venerable Qing Yan immediately was so scared that he did not dare to move an inch.

"And that goes for you two as well." Fairy Eternity used the Fixation Technique on Mo Xiaochou and the middle-aged man too, with outstanding results.

"All done."

Lu Yang hurried forward to welcome Fairy Eternity’s triumphant return: "With His Majesty in action, how could such petty figures possibly stand a chance of victory?"

"His Majesty’s martial prowess is unparalleled throughout history, indeed a naturally brilliant, supremely strategic, world-shaking figure, surpassing all predecessors, and illuminating for posterity!" Lu Yang clapped enthusiastically, genuinely full of praise.

"Right, right, this Immortal is awesome," Fairy Eternity stood with hands on her hips, brimming with pride, as if she had vanquished a formidable foe.

"Let’s hear it, what’s your situation, and why are you hiding in the Servant Monk Institute?"

With his hands behind his back, Lu Yang paced before the three soul bodies. Even though Lu Yang was only at the mid-stage of Transforming Spirit and not of high seniority, the three soul bodies were still trembling in fear, not daring to hide anything from him. freewēbnovel.com

"Speak the truth."

Immortal Fairy, standing behind Lu Yang, said fiercely.

"I am here to learn the Arhat Fist," Mo Xiaochou confessed first.

"Tell the truth."

"I am here to steal the technique of the Arhat Fist."

"The discipline towards the Servant Monks in Western Heaven Temple is lax, providing the simplest way to infiltrate. I planned on possessing one of the Servant Monks and gradually climb the ranks. Eventually, there’d be a chance to come into contact with the Arhat Fist."

"My name is Duan Qingshui." The middle-aged man at the early Integration Stage said. His purpose for infiltrating Western Heaven Temple was the same as Mo Xiaochou’s—to steal techniques. Except, he aimed to steal one of the three great scriptures of Western Heaven Temple, the "Great Collection Sutra."

"Where are your physical bodies?"

"Hidden away outside."

"Why separate?" Lu Yang wondered. Separating the spirit from the body was dangerous, as it halved one’s combat power.

"We don’t have magic artifacts capable of carrying our physical bodies without being detected," Duan Qingshui explained helplessly. They didn’t want it this way; they had no choice. Such magic artifacts were extremely rare; they couldn’t buy them even if they wanted to.

Qing Yan Venerate had fought a fierce battle with Master Mingyu, one that left only his soul remaining. After employing the Escape Skill "Qing Smoke Transforming the Blue Sky," his soul was still gravely injured. Left with no choice, he had to possess the body of Xin Ping from the northern Servant Monk Institute.

In order to help Xin Ping advance to a higher institute, allowing Qing Yan Venerate to recover his strength and look for a chance to make a scene in Western Heaven Temple as revenge against Master Mingyu, he cultivated Xin Ping into possessing the Formless Physique using a secret method, ensuring it would go undetected by anyone.

"You’ve saved Western Heaven Temple a big trouble," Lu Yang could imagine that if Qing Yan Venerate really managed to stay hidden, he could indeed stir up significant trouble in Western Heaven Temple.

However, he acted righteously without seeking reward; there was no need to report such a minor matter to Western Heaven Temple.

"Leave these three in the Small World for now, and when we return to the Sect, lock them up in Captive Peak."

All three had seen Immortal Fairy, so there was no choice but to silence them or confine them to Captive Peak.

Lu Yang hadn’t expected that in just over half a month since his arrival at Western Heaven Temple, he’d helped Captive Peak capture three more individuals. The only issue was that Mo Xiaochou and Duan Qingshui were of too low a Cultivation Level, especially Mo Xiaochou, who would be bottom-ranked at Captive Peak.

"Never mind, a mosquito is still meat no matter how small," Lu Yang believed that doing good deeds didn’t discriminate by size.

Having dealt with these three, Lu Yang finally had time to continue watching Xin Ding’s match.

"What, Xin Ding at the sixth level of Qi Refinement actually defeated Xin’an at the seventh level!"

"This is a challenge beyond his level!"

The battle in the Green Blade Sword Small World had concluded, and the Martial Monk Institute selection competition was also nearing its end. Xin Ding, who no one had faith in, defeated the most likely candidate, Xin’an.

Defeating someone from the seventh level of Qi Refinement while at the sixth level was no small feat. It signified a mid-stage practitioner overcoming a late-stage one. How could the Servant Monks not cheer ecstatically at this scene?

Especially the Servant Monks from the eastern Servant Monk Institute, who were the most excited. How many years had it been since they last claimed victory? Now, finally, they could hold their heads high in front of the other three institutes.

Lu Yang rubbed his temples in pain. The disparity between the fights inside and outside the Small World was substantial, and sudden exposure was somewhat overwhelming.

"Zhi Yuan Senior Brother, you’ve taught a good disciple," a monk from the Martial Monk Institute remarked meaningfully to Zhi Yuan. He definitely didn’t believe that Zhi Yuan hadn’t taught Xin Ding.

It seems that these years of seclusion by Zhi Yuan were a facade. In reality, he had been secretly grooming a successor all along, and Xin Ding was the prime example.

Given Xin Ding’s display of talent today, there was a chance he could enter the Heaven-Earth-Man rankings and become a famed expert listed there.

Zhi Yuan couldn’t be bothered to reply; after all, even if he denied teaching Xin Ding, the other person wouldn’t believe it.

"However, once he joins the Martial Monk Institute, he might face targeting—after all, Senior Brother, you made quite a few enemies there back in the day," the monk from the Martial Monk Institute warned, having a relatively good relationship with Zhi Yuan. But as for others, that was less certain.

Zhi Yuan glared, "How dare they! Do they really think I’m dead?"

"In any case, I will do my best to take care of him, but I can’t guarantee anything beyond that," said the monk from the Martial Monk Institute.

Zhi Yuan calmed down, pressed his palms together in gratitude, "Then I’ll have to trouble Junior Brother."

"This Master Uncle..."

"You may call me Master Uncle Zhi Kong."

Zhi Kong said, leading Xin Ding towards the medicine warehouse.

"Come in, just remember not to trample the seedlings at the doorway."

The great doors of the medicine warehouse opened automatically, revealing a field of herbs, with a little old man going about sprinkling water from his watering can.

The little old man flew in front of Xin Ding with his hands clasped behind his back. Facing the little man, Xin Ding felt utterly naked, with no secrets to hide.

He was definitely a great master!

"He’s just at the early stage of Spirit Transformation," came the lazy voice of Tofu Heavenly Venerable beside Xin Ding. A random person from the Green Blade Sword Small World would be stronger than this little old man.

Knowing the little old man’s cultivation level, Xin Ding still thought he was very impressive. Being at the initial stage of Spirit Transformation was already an unattainable level for him.

He feared he might never reach the stage of Spirit Transformation in his lifetime.

"What herb do you want?" asked the little old man.

"Hundred-year Spirit Core Grass."

"So it is Spirit Core Grass," the little old man surmised upon seeing the Buddha beads Xin Ding wore, guessing that he would want the Spirit Core Grass.

Spirit Core Grass was rare, and not many knew about it.

"Zhi Yuan was the most gifted and virtuous student I had ever taken, who would have thought that he, so devoted to Buddhism, would meet the Red Lotus Demoness on a mission, become entangled with her several times, and develop worldly affections, breaking the monastic precepts? If I hadn’t separated them, who would take the monastic precepts seriously?"

The little old man rambled on for quite a while, and Xin Ding managed to roughly understand Master Uncle Zhi Yuan’s story.

"I’m puzzled about something and would like to ask Master Uncle to clear my confusion."

"If Buddhism is a sanctuary far from worldly affairs, and marrying a person from the secular world means developing worldly affections, then why not let the Red Lotus Demoness also join our Western Paradise Temple? In that way, Master Uncle Zhi Yuan marrying her wouldn’t be a problem, right?"

The little old man began to doubt his own judgment.

Did Zhi Yuan truly teach this disciple?

Zhi Kong looked at Xin Ding with astonishment, a good question indeed. How had he never thought of this before?

"Certainly not," the little old man replied. He had cultivated for several hundred years, guarded the garden, and his Zen skills were exceptional. He spoke slowly and deliberately, smiling as he answered Xin Ding’s question.

"Marriage is a matter of the secular world. Our Buddhism is a pure land of cultivation. If the Red Lotus Demoness converts to Buddhism and marries Zhi Yuan, wouldn’t that be introducing worldly affairs into the pure land, breaking its rules?"

Zhi Kong suddenly realized the truth of the matter, worthy of being Uncle Wu Nian, resolving his confusion in a few words.

However, Xin Ding was still puzzled, his clear eyes fixed on the little old man: "But I see that gambling and fighting are rampant in our menial work division. Uncle Zhi Xing from the Western menial work division provoked Uncle Zhi Yuan, the four menial divisions competed against each other, and the Martial Monk Institute selected the top four to compete for first place.

Aren’t these all worldly matters too?"

"I..."

The little old man was at a loss for words, unable to reply to Xin Ding immediately.

Primarily because everything Xin Ding said was true, he found himself unable to retort.

Xin Ding came to a sudden realization, finally understanding the matter: "I get it, there’s only one Uncle Zhi Yuan, easy to manage. The rest involves too many people, and if our Buddhism cannot manage, we just let it be."

"I..."

The little old man was rendered speechless again. How could this seemingly simple-minded youngster speak nothing but the truth?

This youngster could not have been taught by Zhi Yuan. If Zhi Yuan had such a mind, he wouldn’t have been trapped by emotions and failed his breakthrough!

Lu Yang laughed so hard in the Green Blade Sword Small World that his stomach hurt. Xin Ding’s single-minded nature indeed made him an excellent seedling for Buddhism.

The little old man took a deep breath and spoke earnestly, "Xin Ding, you must understand that everything undergoes a process of change. Our Western Paradise Temple indeed has many impurities, but you should also see that we are cleansing these matters. It is just that such things take time."

"How much time does it need?"

"A very long time."

Xin Ding thought about it and felt like his great-uncle had said something but also as if he hadn’t said anything at all.

"He said that our Western Paradise Temple has too many impurities to manage. Uncle, your desire to marry the Red Lotus Demoness is too conspicuous, and the Western Paradise Temple cannot overlook it."

The master was indeed on his side!

He couldn’t ignore this.

Having a Great Uncle Master at the Divinity Transformation Stage as a backer, who in the Martial Monk Institute would dare bring up the matter of new Martial Monks sparring with the older ones?

...

Except Xin Ding himself.

Zhi Yuan, using the power of Spirit Core Grass, returned to the pinnacle of the Golden Core, roamed around the Martial Monk Institute, and was astounded to find no one was bullying Xin Ding.

Seeing the inexplicably good attitude of everyone in the Martial Monk Institute towards him, Xin Ding didn’t think much of it, and just assumed it was the reward for steadfastly guarding the secret of Tofu Heavenly Venerable and saving Western Paradise Temple, the good deed had brought good karma.

Once they knew of Xin Ding’s identity, the Martial Monk Institute would not treat him as they did the other newcomers; resources were allocated in his favor.
