Xin Ding was searching for books on the second floor of the Scripture Pavilion; according to the rules, he could only take one book with him.

The books here were dazzlingly varied, and he was confused about what to choose.

"Fairy, are there hidden opportunities on the second floor?" Tofu Heavenly Venerate asked Heavenly Venerate Dou.

Heavenly Venerate Dou opened his Immortal Sense and scanned around, then shook his head, "Like the first floor, those opportunities are gone, but there are other opportunities."

"What opportunities?"

"See that monk sweeping the floor? He is actually at the Late Tribulation Stage."

"To think such a master was hidden here." Lu Yang was immensely surprised, thankful that he hadn’t rashly used his Spiritual Sense to probe, as he would certainly have been detected by the other.

"Heavenly Venerate, which book should I choose?"

"Fairy, which book should he choose?"

"That one called Qing Yan, come here, are there any good cultivation techniques on this second floor?"

Qing Yan, an honest and straightforward figure, came over. Having lived for over a thousand years in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage and possessing multiple identities, he had visited the Scripture Pavilion in the Western Paradise Temple several times. He was the most familiar with the Western Paradise Temple within the Green Peak Sword Small World.

"How about the ’Six-character Mantra Scripture’? If you memorize this scripture, it has the effect of blessing and exorcising evil."

"No, it’s too difficult to learn."

"How about the ’Great Compassionate Mantra’? It can purify the soul."

"No need, this little monk’s soul is pure enough."

"How about the ’Great Brightness Spell’? It’s effective against soul attacks."

"Sounds pretty average."

"What about ’Lion Roar’? It’s a sonic attack that imitates the roar of a lion and can deter enemies. Although the second floor only has the first part, it should be enough for this little monk."

"That will do. Little Yang, let him choose ’Lion Roar’."

"Little monk, you choose ’Lion Roar’."

"Okay." Xin Ding trusted Tofu Heavenly Venerate greatly and took the first part of Lion Roar.

...

The treatment of martial monks and servant monks was not comparable; each martial monk owned their private monastery, and Xin Ding, unable to wait, started flipping through ’Lion Roar’ upon his return to the monastery.

After glancing through it twice, Xin Ding felt dizzy and couldn’t quite understand the technique.

"Heavenly Venerate, do you know Lion Roar? Could you teach me?"

From the Green Peak Sword, the eternal raspy voice of Tofu Heavenly Venerate replied, "Hehe, this seat has traversed through the heavens, mastered countless techniques; what is there I do not know? But if I were to teach you directly, it would only harm you, you should first read it a few times, get a superficial understanding of this technique, then I will teach you."

"Yes!"

Tofu Heavenly Venerate then turned and sought help from the Golden Finger, "Fairy, do you know how to perform Lion Roar?"

"What’s there not to know? The so-called Lion Roar is nothing but imitating the roar of lion-like Demon Beasts, bringing out the true essence of the roar to stun the opponent, just an ordinary technique."

"Can you teach me?" Lu Yang, clutching at straws, looked expectantly at Immortal Fairy Eternity.

"Lion-like Demon Beasts have never produced any notable characters, except for the Suan Ni of the Qiongqi Clan who are a bit capable; still, they haven’t even produced a Semi-Immortal."

Lu Yang had a request, and naturally, Immortal Fairy Eternity had to agree; however, since Lu Yang was a loyal officer of the Great Bean Dynasty, teaching him just an ordinary technique like Lion Roar wouldn’t do.

If he was to learn, he should learn the best!

"Look at Little Ling Lianyi and Xiao Baihu, their shouts are much stronger than Lion Roar."

"Dragon chants, phoenix calls, and tiger roars, huh?" Lu Yang nodded. It was indeed true, especially for the Qiongqi Clan. Despite being named ’poor,’ they had produced two Semi-Immortals, more than both the Dragon and Phoenix Tribes, truly powerful.

Whereas the Suan Ni among the lion-like Demon Beasts, was merely a branch of the Dragon Clan and truly not worth emulating.

"So, should I learn their calls?" Lu Yang asked, as dragon chants, phoenix calls, and tiger roars also sounded quite impressive.

Fairy Eternity shook her head, "Of course not, didn’t I just say that? The principle of the Lion Roar is to express the true essence of a lion’s roar. The stronger the lion you imitate, the more powerful the roar."

"So?" Lu Yang had a faint feeling of foreboding.

Fairy Eternity smiled without showing her teeth, revealing a clean smile, "Little Ling and the others are indeed strong, but none are as strong as I am. Little Yang, you just need to learn my voice!"

"Let me think, since they call it ’Lion Roar,’ then I’ll name this magic skill ’Fairy Shout.’

Fairy Eternity had never taught anyone before, so she could only think of a technique name on the spot.

Lu Yang: "..."

This technique’s name sounds like something I really don’t want to learn.

However, Lu Yang also admitted that Fairy’s analysis made sense. The more the subject of imitation resembled the original, the more powerful the roar would be.

He gritted his teeth, to become stronger, he decided to learn it!

As soon as Fairy Eternity heard that Lu Yang wanted to learn, she immediately beamed with joy and shooed away the unrelated people, "Go, go, go, all three of you, stay far away."

Qing Yan Venerable and the other two were chased to the edges of the Small World.

"Fairy, how should I learn?" Since he decided to learn, Lu Yang focused intensely on learning.

"Follow me, ha—" Fairy Eternity tried to open her mouth wide, like a kitten, pressing down her voice as she said "ha."

"Ha—" Lu Yang mimicked studiously.

"No, no, you need to imitate my voice, ha—"

"Like this? Ha—"

"Still not right." Fairy Eternity corrected him, pointing to her own mouth to demonstrate, "Pay attention to my mouth shape."

Lu Yang stared hard at Fairy Eternity’s mouth, trying to grasp every movement. The fairy’s mouth was very attractive, with red lips and white teeth, and her little tongue looked pink and tender.

"Stop staring at me all the time." Fairy Eternity pushed Lu Yang’s face away, her cheeks blushing, feeling somewhat odd.

Lu Yang wore a perplexed expression, wasn’t it you who asked me to watch?

Oh well, at His Majesty’s command, whatever he says, goes.

In just half a day, Lu Yang had learned ’Fairy Shout’. After all, spending his days with Fairy Eternity, learning her shouting voice wasn’t difficult.

"Ha—" Lu Yang emitted the voice of the Fairy, astonishingly powerful, the sound waves materialized, directly demolishing a mountaintop!

Then Lu Yang used his hands to form a horn shape, and deployed ’Fairy Shout’ again, the power increased a notch, even shaking the space!

Lu Yang was delighted, truly much more powerful than Buddhism’s ’Lion Roar’!

The only problem was that the voice wasn’t very intimidating.

"I didn’t lie to you, did I? This move is very powerful, it can immobilize the enemy and even has a suppressive effect on Demon Beasts. When the Demon Beasts hear my voice, I guarantee they all get scared and lie down!" Fairy Eternity said proudly, reminiscing how in the Ancient Times, any Demon Beast that heard her voice would immediately flee.

"Heavenly Venerate, I have reviewed it several times now, I think I understand the essence of the Lion Roar, can you teach it now?" Xin Ding closed the book with a sigh of relief, rubbing his temples, having finally understood the book after half a day’s effort.

Lu Yang muttered to himself worriedly, absorbed in learning ’Fairy Shout’, he had forgotten that Xin Ding was outside waiting for him.

Soon, from within the Green Peak Sword, the calm voice of Tofu Heavenly Venerable came, "Good comprehension, I’ll teach you the Transformation Technique first."

"Transformation Technique?"

"Indeed, if one wants to learn Lion Roar, one must first imitate a lion and comprehend the true essence of a lion."

"So that’s how it is." Xin Ding suddenly understood, finding Tofu Heavenly Venerable’s words made a lot of sense.

Lu Yang released a Spiritual Sense imprint, which conjured a lively and vivid Suan Ni.

When Lu Yang had been in the Demon Territory, he had interacted with the Suan Ni species and remembered their ways of moving.

The conjured Suan Ni was awe-inspiring, leaping between mountains, roaring at heaven and earth as if it could swallow the sky with its wide-open mouth!

Xin Ding’s expression was in a trance, having never seen such a ferocious Demon Beast before!

"Observe this Suan Ni carefully!" came Tofu Heavenly Venerable’s voice beside his ear.

Tofu Heavenly Venerable’s voice carried a kind of unbelievable magic, which snapped Xin Ding back to reality, focusing solely on observing the Suan Ni.

Seizing the moment when Xin Ding was distracted, Lu Yang quickly used his Spiritual Sense to scan and study "Lion Roar."

The fairy was right; this was indeed a very simple magic skill, with principles not much different from "Fairy Shout." The only difference was the learning difficulty, which was much easier compared to "Fairy Shout."

Following the method written in "Lion Roar," Lu Yang formed hand seals and let out the most orthodox lion’s roar: "Roar—"

In passing, he lay down on the ground and transformed into a lion.

"..."

Lu Yang cradled his forehead with his lion’s paw, knowing something would go wrong.

Lu Yang reverted to human form and pondered, Xin Ding’s cultivation level was too low, learning Lion Roar directly was too difficult; was it really necessary to stick to the initial idea?

"Heavenly Venerable, I have finished observing."

"Good, then I shall teach you Lion Fist."

"Lion Fist?" Xin Ding had never heard of such a boxing technique.

"This boxing technique is of my own creation. When cultivated to perfection, one can transform into a real lion."

"Perfection?"

"You are still inexperienced in learning, and perfection is far from your reach. Do not aim too high; focus on mastering the basics before thinking of perfection."

"Yes."

Then, a figure as immaculate and white as tofu appeared before Xin Ding. The tofu-like figure posed, and in its punches and kicks were echoes of Suan Ni movements.

Lu Yang conjured a figure demonstrating Lion Form Boxing.

"Is this Lion Fist? It’s so powerful. If the boxing technique is perfected and I transform into a true lion, what a sight that will be!"

As the tofu figure’s movements became faster, it suddenly transformed into a Suan Ni, leaving Xin Ding lost in awe!

This was the perfection of Lion Fist!

Xin Ding earnestly began to learn, with Lu Yang, the founder, as his guide, and quickly got the hang of Lion Fist.

The fact proved Lu Yang was right. Imitating the lion’s movements before learning Lion Roar was much simpler.

It wasn’t long before Xin Ding could execute Lion Roar, and though it was nowhere near as effective as Lu Yang’s, it was sufficient for someone at the Qi Cultivation Stage.

...

"Xin Ding Senior Brother, have you heard? The Chi Xiao Ancient Realm is going to open, and we all can enter!" Xin Chen from the Southern Servant Institute, upon receiving the news, immediately came to tell Xin Ding.

"What is the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm?"

"The Chi Xiao Ancient Realm is a secret realm passed down from Ancient Times that only cultivators below the Foundation Establishment Stage are eligible to enter. For the sake of safety, the various powers usually require cultivators to be at least at the Seventh Layer of Qi Refinement and below Consummation of Qi Refinement. We can all enter the Ancient Realm!"

"Are there any benefits to entering the Ancient Realm?"

"Of course, there are benefits. Although the institute will issue a Foundation Establishment Pill when we reach Foundation Establishment, they only provide one. If you want to get more, you have to buy them with Merit Points."

"The Chi Xiao Ancient Realm is full of ancient Foundation Establishment Grass, which is the main ingredient for concocting ancient Foundation Establishment Pills. With the main ingredients, do you still need to worry about the quantity of Foundation Establishment Pills?"

"Besides the ancient Foundation Establishment Grass, at the deepest part of the Ancient Realm, there are various inheritances. If you can obtain any one of them, you will have no worries for your future cultivation!"

Xin Chen grew more excited as he spoke. If he were still in the Servants’ Institute, he definitely would not have had the chance to go to the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm. Now that he had come to the Martial Monk Institute, the benefits were apparent.

"It does sound like a good place." Xin Ding nodded. According to what Xin Chen had said, all the Qi Cultivation Stage Martial Monks from the institute would go, so he didn’t really have another option.

After Xin Chen left, Xin Ding asked, "Heavenly Venerate, do you know about the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm?"

"This Venerable has not heard of this secret realm. Since it originated from Ancient Times, it seems that its original name was lost over the long years, and it was given a new name by later generations."

"With this Venerable here, there is no harm in going."

These were the words Lu Yang conveyed from Immortal Fairy.

"Alright."

...

The day to enter the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm soon arrived.

The Chi Xiao Ancient Realm was a famous secret realm in Buddha Country. Apart from the Western Paradise Temple, many other major powers also sent their Qi Cultivation Stage disciples. Among them, Xin Ding’s seventh layer Qi Cultivation Realm was inconspicuous and went unnoticed.

"The people from Dujiang Temple have arrived!"

"It’s the Nianci Temple contingent!"

"Look, the Heavenly Vault Holy Land has come too!" someone shouted as a group of ethereal, fairy-like women in white robes flew in on a boat, attracting everyone’s attention upon their arrival.

"Isn’t that Yu Youlan from the Heavenly Vault Holy Land? I’ve heard she has an Immortal body and cultivates at an astonishing speed, unrivaled among her peers, deeply favored by the Holy Land’s patriarch. She’s bound to be on the three lists of heaven, earth, and men in the future!"

Yu Youlan’s face was veiled, revealing a pair of charming peach blossom eyes. Although she was young, it was evident that she would grow up to be a beauty and had many admirers.

Even the Martial Monks who had come with Xin Ding could not help showing a slightly infatuated look upon seeing Yu Youlan, but Xin Ding alone recited scriptures silently, unaffected by her beauty.

Yu Youlan showed no expression; she was all too familiar with her own allure. She inadvertently noticed Xin Ding, who was lowering his head reciting scriptures, and a trace of interest appeared on the corner of her mouth.

"Hmm, a little monk that’s quite interesting."

"Heavenly Vault Holy Land? Immortal recalls that there was a Holy Land with this name during Ancient Times," Immortal Fairy said, remembering that the Heavenly Vault Holy Land was quite a force back in the Ancient Times, with two Pass Tribulation Cultivators who were eligible to attend lectures given by the Five Immortals.

"Qing Yan, come over and tell me about it?"

"Reporting to the Immortal, it is said that the Heavenly Vault Holy Land’s patriarch came into possession of half an ancient inheritance, which allowed them to rise from obscurity and establish the Holy Land. Moreover, this ancient inheritance originated from a place known as the Heavenly Vault Holy Land."

"No wonder it sounded familiar; it turns out there is an inheritance from that Heavenly Vault Holy Land."

"It’s rumored that there’s another part of the Heavenly Vault Holy Land’s inheritance within the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm. Every time the Ancient Realm opens, the Holy Land sends people to try to obtain the inheritance, but they’ve never succeeded."

With Elder Qing Yan, who knew everything in Buddha Country, many things were convenient to understand.

As the Ancient Realm opened, Xin Ding entered with the Green Peak Sword.

The Green Peak Sword Small World could shield causality, and naturally, it could also shield the Ancient Realm’s probes, easily deceiving the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm.

"So this is the place," realized Immortal Fairy upon entering the Ancient Realm.

"Fairy, where is this place?"

"Hasn’t Immortal already told you? In the Heavenly Vault Holy Land, only two at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage are qualified to listen to Yingtian Immortal’s lectures. Besides sharing his cultivation experience, Yingtian Immortal mainly talks about how to maintain composure and style," the Fairy explained.

"After the lecture, one must complete the assignment. People from a few other Holy Lands in the Heavenly Vault Holy Land have teamed up to create this Secret Realm, which only Cultivators below the Foundation Establishment Stage can enter."

"They pretend to be Cultivators at the Qi Cultivation Stage and enter the Secret Realm as well, but once inside, they do not use their own power but rather rely on the Realm’s power to pass through."

"Then, what was the original name of this Secret Realm?" Lu Yang asked.

"Assignment One."

.....

"Just as I thought, I’ve been separated from them." Xin Ding appeared all alone in the dense forest of the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm, unable to even discern directions.

"According to Junior Brother Xin Chen’s words, the locations after entering the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm are random. If lucky, some acquaintances might be transported to the same place. It seems my luck wasn’t good."

"The Chi Xiao Ancient Realm is divided into an outer layer and an inner layer. The outer layer has some ordinary opportunities, while the inner layer has a higher chance of encountering special opportunities. However, the inner layer is also more dangerous."

"There are two methods of departure: automatic departure after three days, or choose to leave after obtaining an opportunity... Who’s there!"

Xin Ding, sensing something, turned and demanded loudly. After cultivating Lion Roar, his voice naturally carried a commanding presence.

"This little monk has quite the sensitive perception. Is it that you have specially cultivated your Spiritual Sense?"

Accompanied by the rustling of the bushes, a young girl in white appeared, like a Youlan orchid in a secluded valley, completely out of sync with the surrounding atmosphere.

Yu Youlan looked at Xin Ding with a smile that was not quite a smile, finding the coincidence quite amusing.

"So it’s the Benefactor Yu Youlan from the Heavenly Vault Holy Land," Xin Ding greeted with palms together, feeling relieved. He had heard that this Holy Daughter was whimsical and quirky but had no bad intentions; she was someone he could associate with.

Yu Youlan quietly observed Xin Ding’s reaction to her presence and discovered that the little monk’s gaze was clear, and when looking at her, there was no trace of impure thoughts—a rarity indeed.

"Alright, little monk, I have something to do, so take care of yourself."

Yu Youlan hadn’t forgotten her mission; she came to the Ancient Realm fully prepared, with a thirty percent chance of entering the inner layer to find the other half of the Holy Land’s heritage.

"Amitābha."

Yu Youlan smiled sweetly at Xin Ding and then went on her way.

As she weaved through the jungle, running for a while, she couldn’t shake the feeling that someone was following her. She stopped and hid in a treetop, on guard for the newcomer.

Before long, Xin Ding passed by.

"Little monk, are you following me?"

Yu Youlan was surprised, having thought this monk was virtuous; why would he resort to tailing her?

"Benefactor, you misunderstand. I’m merely heading toward the inner layer, and it only happens that our paths coincide," said Xin Ding.

"Coincide?" Yu Youlan eyed him skeptically, not believing his words. The shortest and safest route from the outer to the inner layer was a secret their Holy Land had only recently unraveled. How could Western Paradise Temple possibly have figured it out?

"You go ahead."

Without any hesitation, Xin Ding continued onward, and Yu Youlan followed him.

Could it really be the same route I intend to take?!

After following for a while, Yu Youlan began to believe what Xin Ding had said.

"Little monk, how did you know to take this route?"

"The Buddha said, ’Not to be spoken of,’" replied Xin Ding, who dared not reveal anything about Tofu Heavenly Venerable, as it involved matters of great causality and the potential destruction of Western Paradise Temple.

"Tell me," pressed Yu Youlan with a sweet, coaxing voice that could easily make any weak-willed cultivator bow to her demands.

"Not to be spoken of."

"An interesting little monk," Yu Youlan commented, her interest in Xin Ding increasing. She had been born with a silver spoon and chosen by the Patriarch to be the Holy Daughter, unmatched in talent and background. She had never failed to get what she wanted.

She was eager to see what other abilities this little monk had!

The two shared the same route, chatting and laughing along the way.

Mainly, it was Yu Youlan who talked and laughed on her own, while Xin Ding rarely responded.

The more Yu Youlan interacted with him, the more she felt that this little monk was quite extraordinary. No matter how she tried to probe and hint, he remained tight-lipped about the accurate insights he held about Lu Yang.

"Youlan, I didn’t expect you to be here as well," said the newcomer.

As the two were chatting, a group of people emerged from the forest. The leader was dignified and majestic-looking. The only imperfection was that the hem of his clothes was slightly torn as if he had been through a fierce battle recently.

The situation outside was not entirely peaceful. The presence of demon beasts and malevolent spirits would cause disturbances. The reason Xin Ding and his companion had not run into any so far was that they had been following the safest route.

Xin Ding recognized the leader; it was Gao Tianxiu, the Holy Son of Tuo Luo Holy Land. The others must be his followers.

"Greetings to Benefactor Gao."

Gao Tianxiu frowned slightly. He hadn’t expected Yu Youlan to be accompanied by someone. While Yu Youlan appeared affable and approachable to outsiders, upon interaction, one would discover that she kept everyone at a great distance, allowing no one to come close to her.

Why was this ordinary-looking, averagely-cultivated little monk so close to Yu Youlan?

"Who among you knows this little monk?" he asked one of his followers.

"Holy Son, this monk should be Xin Ding from the Western Paradise Temple. I heard he was originally a Servant Monk who fortuitously entered the Martial Monk Institute."

"So he is just a Servant Monk." Gao Tianxiu sneered, having thought the monk had some impressive background.

"Gao Tianxiu, I’ve told you many times before, we aren’t that close, and you shouldn’t address me by name!" Yu Youlan said, somewhat annoyed. Gao Tianxiu was like a clingy plaster that she couldn’t shake off.

"Youlan, I’m just worried about you. This Ancient Realm is fraught with dangers. We’ve already encountered more than one batch of demon beasts and malevolent spirits. It wouldn’t be good if someone alone like you got deceived or ran into some danger," he said.

As he spoke, Gao Tianxiu’s gaze drifted towards Xin Ding, his implication clear.

"The concern of Holy Son Gao is appreciated, but my affairs are really none of your business!"

"It seems Benefactor Gao has some misunderstandings about me."

"Little monk, beat it. You have no place here!"

"Benefactor Gao, I’m afraid that would be asking too much of me."

"It seems you prefer punishment over a toast!"

Gao Tianxiu let out a sinister chuckle as the full aura of his Consummation of Qi Refinement erupted. The group of followers behind him also released their auras, revealing themselves to be on the eighth or ninth levels of Qi Refinement. Any of them alone was more highly-cultivated than Xin Ding!

"What are you all trying to do!" Yu Youlan exclaimed angrily, stepping forward to protect Xin Ding. She was no match if all these people were to rush them at once.

"Youlan, this is a battle between men. You shouldn’t interfere!"

Gao Tianxiu, confident of victory, pressed forward towards Xin Ding. With more than a dozen people at the Qi Cultivation Stage, he believed it impossible for Xin Ding to escape!

"Benefactor Gao, neither toasts nor penalties are for me to consume."

"Brave kid, let’s all go at him together!"

As the crowd moved to surround him and there was no escape, Xin Ding clasped his hands together and sighed. Spiritual Energy surged, the space around twisted, and the trees seemed to come to life, roots drilling out and branches growing wildly, entangling Gao Tianxiu and his men like a demonic dance.

"What sorcery is this!" the crowd exclaimed in shock. How could the trees transform? Since the discovery of Chi Xiao Ancient Realm, they had never heard of such a thing!

To them, with their cultivation levels and their numbers, the suddenly animated ancient trees were meaningless.

Xin Ding placed one hand on his chest and gently pressed down with the other. Space obeyed his command as an invisible giant hand pressed down, pinning Gao Tianxiu and the others wrapped by the trees to the ground with a thud!

Xin Ding remained calm and unruffled, approaching Gao Tianxiu.

Gao Tianxiu struggled to lift his head, his eyes filled with immense fear. The light shining on Xin Ding’s head obscured his features, making him appear both divine and demonic.

"Benefactor Gao, I am a monk; I do not drink alcohol."

"Benefactor Yu, let us continue on our way."

"Ah, oh." Yu Youlan snapped out of her daze. She hadn’t expected such a turn of events either.

Xin Ding’s performance just now was akin to him being the master of the Ancient Realm!

Within the Green Blade Sword Small World, the Tofu Heavenly Venerable was half delighted and half vexed.

He was pleased with Xin Ding’s performance.

"The problem is, when I went to the Ancient Realm before, why didn’t I encounter such opportunities?"

Yu Youlan closely followed Xin Ding, her interest in the little monk growing ever more intense.

"We’re here."

Standing in front of a stone gate tens of meters high, Xin Ding was surrounded by the incredibly precious Foundation Establishment Grass from ancient times. This was precisely Xin Ding’s secret for coming to the Ancient Realm. He bent down and picked ten plants, enough to refine ten Foundation Establishment Pills.

With them, even those with the poorest aptitude could reach the Foundation Establishment Stage.

Outside the dense, primordial forests of the Ancient Times, Chi Xiao Ancient Realm’s inner layer held a majestic hall carved from a single small planet—a feat only possible during the Ancient Times. The modern Cultivation World no longer had the means to create such wonders.

"So this is the Ancient Stone Hall inside," Yu Youlan exclaimed. It was her first visit to the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm, and she hadn’t expected the Ancient Stone Hall to be so grand. Even the palace of the elder patriarch at her Holy Land was not as imposing.

"However, such a vast Ancient Stone Hall is just for testing those at the Qi Cultivation Stage?" A question surfaced in Yu Youlan’s mind. Were cultivators at the Qi Cultivation Stage worthy of such a Secret Realm?

Xin Ding shared her doubts and decided to consult the Tofu Heavenly Venerable. He knew how to enter the inner circle and how to harness the hidden powers of the Ancient Realm, all thanks to the Tofu Heavenly Venerable’s guidance.

"Heavenly Venerable, do you know why this Ancient Realm was built in the first place?"

In the world, what secrets were unknown to the Tofu Heavenly Venerable? "Heh, the origin of this Secret Realm is hardly worth mentioning; it was simply constructed by a few juniors at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage in order to pass the tests set by Immortals."

Juniors at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, tests by Immortals!

Xin Ding was astonished; the Heavenly Venerable could always reveal his glorious past with just a few words.

Lu Yang wasn’t lying. As the Immortal Lineage Second Boss, his stature was immensely respected. By the hierarchy, the two at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage from the Heavenly Vault Holy Land were juniors in front of him.

The sealed stone gate opened, and the two entered the Ancient Stone Hall.

Each time the Ancient Realm was accessed, only ten percent of those at the Qi Cultivation Stage could enter the Ancient Stone Hall. On average, entry happened on the third day, so the progress of the two was already far beyond everyone else’s.

Yu Youlan blinked at Xin Ding, "Inside this Ancient Stone Hall, there are eight Sub-Halls, each with its own challenges. Only by passing all the challenges can one enter the Inner Hall and obtain the inheritance!"

"It’s difficult for you to overcome all the challenges alone. Why don’t we cooperate?" she suggested.

Xin Ding calmly shook his head, "Benefactor Yu is mistaken."

"Mistaken?" Yu Youlan found that hard to believe. This was the pattern that generations of Qi Cultivation Stage cultivators from her Holy Land had summarized through trials; how could it be wrong?

"The eight Sub-Halls of this Ancient Stone Hall are arranged according to the scene of the Innate Eight Diagrams. One only needs to pass through the Kan, Li, and Gen directional Sub-Halls in order to enter the Inner Hall."

"Is that really so?" Yu Youlan instinctively doubted this, but considering Xin Ding’s confident assertion together with his previous actions, she thought what he said must be true.

Xin Ding didn’t insist on Yu Youlan believing him; it was enough for him to believe in himself.

Without paying further attention to Yu Youlan, Xin Ding resolutely headed towards the Kanfen Hall.

"Hey, little monk, wait for me. Let’s go together," Yu Youlan decided to trust the little monk.

The two arrived at Kanfen Hall, where various magic artifacts were wrapped in bubbles, floating in the air. Each one was precious to those at the Golden Core Stage and extremely tempting for those at the Qi Cultivation Stage.

Seeing Xin Ding approaching a bubble, Yu Youlan hastily warned, "Don’t touch it. Only by resisting the temptation and not touching any magic artifact can you safely pass this challenge!"

As if not hearing Yu Youlan’s words, Xin Ding popped a bubble and took out a gourd-shaped magic artifact.

Yet nothing happened.

"What’s going on?" Yu Youlan was bewildered; this was not consistent with the experience accumulated by her Holy Land.

Xin Ding stowed the gourd and explained lightly, "Indeed, this challenge tests one’s resolution, and touching any bubble will trigger a penalty. However, among the many traps, one artifact is not trapped, and that is this very gourd."

After passing through the Kanfen Hall, they came to the Separation Hall.

Upon entering the Separation Hall, countless ghosts emerged from the walls, emitting eerie wails and filling the space with overwhelming Yin Energy.

"Be careful, innumerable stronger ghosts than those outside will appear in this hall. They can only be restrained by Pure Yang Techniques!"

"I have a Pure Yang Treasure. Little monk, you come from the Western Paradise Temple and must know some transcendent scriptures. If you know the Lion Roar, it would be ideal since it has a remarkable effect on souls. But the Lion Roar is very difficult to learn, so I doubt you know it.

I’ll use the treasure and you can chant the scripture, and together we’ll break through..." Yu Youlan quickly assessed the situation and assigned tasks to them.

Xin Ding placed his palms together and uttered an obscure phrase, seemingly an ancient language. Suddenly, the countless ghosts automatically retreated to either side, forming a queue and revealing a clear path!

"This..."

Yu Youlan watched incredulously. How had Xin Ding achieved this?

"Benefactor Yu, let us proceed."

They smoothly made it to the Gen Sub-Hall.

"Be careful, no one has ever breached this Sub-Hall!" Yu Youlan warned, wielding her treasure, ready for any imminent attacks.

Yu Youlan’s face turned pale as soon as they entered the Gen Sub-Hall, which was encircled by a puppet serpent exuding the aura of a Foundation Establishment Middle stage!

With their current strength, their chances of survival were slim, perhaps one in ten!

"Since it’s a puppet, there must be some kind of switch on this snake’s body. If we both engage it, with a bit of luck, we should be able to find the switch," Lu Yang calculated.

The puppet serpent, sensing intruders, opened its jaws wide and lunged at them!

"This is a poisonous snake!"

Yu Youlan noticed the puppet serpent’s exposed fangs; it was indeed a venomous snake. However, this snake belonged to an ancient and exotic species, and its degree of toxicity was unknown!

In the face of the charging poisonous snake, Xin Ding calmly extended a finger and touched a particular scale on the snake, causing it to clang to the ground, paralyzed.

"How come you know everything... Fine, I know ’the Buddha says some things must not be told,’ so don’t bother explaining," Yu Youlan interrupted Xin Ding prematurely and excitedly ran toward the puppet serpent.

This was a rare artifact of ancient puppetry techniques. If she could take it back for study, she might be able to decipher a corner of the ancient puppetry techniques.

"Benefactor Yu, you’d better stay away from this snake. In the time it takes to brew a cup of tea, the snake’s poison sack will self-detonate. The poison sack has aphrodisiac properties, and I believe you wouldn’t want to be afflicted by this kind of poison."

"What?" Yu Youlan, scared, quickly stayed as far away as possible.

"Let’s go."

Xin Ding led Yu Youlan to the Inner Hall. The Inner Hall was splendidly decorated, also reflecting the rough and bold style of Ancient Times, with extreme artistic value.

"Is this the Inner Hall?" Yu Youlan was very excited. She had thought they would have to go through numerous perilous battles and face schemes from fellow travelers, after all the cutthroat fighting for survival, just to reach the Inner Hall.

She didn’t expect it would be so easy to get to this previously unexplored Inner Hall.

Yu Youlan glanced at Xin Ding secretly. She owed a lot to this little monk.

From their interactions along the way, she grew more and more curious about the secrets Xin Ding was hiding.

After entering the Inner Hall, the rules of the Inner Hall automatically entered their minds.

Inside, there were about eight clumps of items enveloped in Chaos Qi, looking mysterious and inscrutable, each containing a Taoist lineage inheritance.

"So, you’re saying we each can choose one clump of Chaos Qi, but have no idea what kind of lineage inheritance is inside?" Yu Youlan faced a dilemma, the inheritance of the Holy Land was within reach, yet it all came down to luck.

Pointing at one of the clumps, Xin Ding said, "Benefactor Yu, this wooden box is the inheritance your Heavenly Vault Holy Land seeks."

"Really?"

Knowing the character of Xin Ding, Yu Youlan didn’t hesitate to pick that clump of Chaos Qi. Within the Chaos Qi was a wooden box, and inside was indeed the inheritance of the Heavenly Vault Holy Land!

"Little monk, you’re so kind!"

Yu Youlan, elated, hugged Xin Ding and then quickly let go, moving so fast that Xin Ding couldn’t react in time.

Xin Ding looked at Yu Youlan with a puzzled expression.

Yu Youlan’s Little Face flushed red, and she turned her back, not wanting Xin Ding to see her expression.

She remembered the vow she had made: whoever could help her find the Holy Land inheritance, she would become that person’s wife!

Since Xin Ding helped her find the inheritance, according to her promise, she was supposed to become Xin Ding’s wife!

But this wooden block didn’t seem to have any interest in her; was it her lack of charm?

"By the way, little monk, do you know what’s inside the other clumps of Chaos Qi?"

"I know. This one contains the Green Bamboo Holy Land inheritance, this one has the Dragon Han Holy Land inheritance..."

Xin Ding methodically described the contents enshrined within each clump of Chaos Qi, repeating whatever Tofu Heavenly Venerable had said until the last one.

"The clump of Chaos Qi here is a coffin, and inside the coffin lies the lord of the Heavenly Vault Holy Land."

"What?"

After speaking, Xin Ding was struck with disbelief and quickly sought assistance from Tofu Heavenly Venerable.

"Heavenly Venerable, is the lord of the Heavenly Vault Holy Land really inside here?"

"Fairy, is the lord of the Heavenly Vault Holy Land really inside here?"

"Right."

As they spoke, the Chaos Qi containing the lord of the Heavenly Vault began to tremble, with Transcendence Tribulation energy spilling out, affecting the entire Ancient Stone Hall!

"What’s going on?" the outer layer of Qi Refinement Cultivators looked dumbfounded as the earth shook and the mountains quaked.

"What happened?"

"I don’t know, it’s been over two hundred thousand years since the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm was discovered, and I’ve never heard of such a thing."

It was not just the Ancient Stone Hall; the entire ancient realm was shaking, causing alarm and panic among everyone, unsure whether this incident was a blessing or a curse. They all stopped what they were doing, no longer caring about competing for the Ancient Foundation Establishment Grass.

The two at the center of the incident didn’t know what had happened either.

The last wisp of Chaos Qi dispersed, revealing an ancient coffin that continued to shake, emitting strands of terrifying aura.

"Is it, is it reviving the dead?" Yu Youlan shivered as she looked at the ancient coffin.

In the Green Blade Sword Small World, Lu Yang was full of question marks, thinking, who rewards with their own self?

As Xin Ding and Yu Youlan’s heartbeats quickened, a bony hand suddenly shot out from the coffin, clinging to the edge of the coffin.

With a lift of the bone hand, the coffin lid burst open, swirling in the air twice before crashing to the ground, creating a large pit!

"After a long dream, emotionally unattached, who would have thought I would have a day to reappear in the world," the corpse muttered.

The skeleton stood up, its gaze empty except for two flickering green ghostly fires.

As the skeleton rose, the Tribulation aura was controlled, and the ancient realm stabilized.

Looking at Xin Ding and Yu Youlan indifferently, the skeleton asked, "Which year is it now, and which fellow Cultivator rules the world?"

Xin Ding and Yu Youlan looked at each other, unable to understand as the skeleton spoke in the language of Ancient Times.

The language of Ancient Times that Xin Ding spoke while controlling the ghosts in the Separation Hall was actually taught on the spot by Lu Yang.

The Heavenly Venerate slightly frowned, puzzled as to why the two had no reaction. Had they been frightened into stupidity?

Just then, Xin Ding lowered his head, then looked up again, appearing like a completely different person in an instant, his eyes deep as if he had seen through the vicissitudes of life, to whom all worldly matters were but fleeting clouds.

"Haha, Xuan Tianzi, I didn’t expect to find you here."

"What went wrong with your hiding technique that your flesh could not withstand the wear of three hundred thousand years, leaving only this skeleton behind?"

Xin Ding also spoke in the language of Ancient Times!

The Heavenly Venerate was stunned, not expecting that even in his skeletal state, the other could recognize him and know his name. He politely asked, "Who are you, fellow?"

He must indeed be a fellow Cultivator from the Ancient Times.

"Who am I?" Xin Ding laughed twice as if finding the question absurd, as well as mocking the Heavenly Venerate for his ignorance in not recognizing a True Immortal.

"Zhu Tian holds me in high regard, Xiao Ling and Lianyi call me Senior Brother, Yingtian Immortal calls me friend. Who do you think I am?"

The Heavenly Venerate’s heart churned with shock. How could this be possible, and who exactly was this great figure?

If what the other said was true, he wasn’t even qualified to call him "fellow."

"Don’t believe it?"

"Fair enough, words alone are no proof, how about this then?"

The Tofu Heavenly Venerate chuckled lightly as a terrifying aura rose behind Xin Ding—only the Heavenly Venerate could feel it!

Immortal!

Sensing this aura, the Heavenly Venerate showed a look of horror and took several steps back!

Identities can be faked, but this aura is absolutely undeniable!

It was then that the Heavenly Venerate noticed the Green Peak Sword wrapped in coarse cloth that Xin Ding carried on his back.

Though he did not recognize the Green Peak Sword, being a being from Ancient Times who often heard Yingtian Immortal lecture, he recognized it at a glance as a true Immortal Artifact!

"This esteemed predecessor..."

The Heavenly Venerate of the Firmament approached with genuine trepidation, not daring to show the slightest hint of negligence.

"I am Tofu Heavenly Venerable."

The Heavenly Venerate of the Firmament racked his brains, trying to recall which of the Four Ancient Immortals might have used the title ’Tofu Heavenly Venerable,’ but he couldn’t think of anyone.

This naming style did not seem like it belonged to any of the Four Ancient Immortals.

Even though he didn’t know the identity of Tofu Heavenly Venerable, he didn’t neglect the courtesies, "Xuan Tianzi pays respect to Tofu Heavenly Venerable!"

"Let’s talk about you. Why have you remained asleep until now?"

"To reply to the predecessor, I actually had not intended to preserve my physical body; my soul resides in this skeleton, which was indeed my intention."

"Oh?"

The Heavenly Venerate of the Firmament sighed bitterly, "With a cultivation level such as the predecessor’s, it’s probably hard to comprehend the troubles of the younger generation. I am merely at the Late Tribulation Stage, my cultivation level is insignificant. In ancient times, it was hard to ascend, and even concealing my identity could lead me to encounter others doing the same.

It was always awkward, and should I encounter a Semi-Immortal, it would be even more embarrassing."

"I am ashamed that I could not completely follow the teachings of Yingtian Immortal Venerate."

"I came up with a brilliant plan, to sleep for hundreds of thousands of years, reviving within the body of a junior cultivator just starting out, and guide his cultivation, making his future bright."

"Considering my limited lifespan of less than two thousand years left, and having nothing to hold onto, I chose to sleep in this secret realm, waiting for a fated junior cultivator to arrive in the Inner Hall."

"I did not expect to encounter a predecessor here."

Lu Yang: "..."

Can’t you ancient cultivators focus on something serious, like learning from someone...?

Lu Yang was stumped, it seemed like there was no one worth learning from in the ancient times, even the Five Ancient Immortals led in frivolity.

"Carrying a multitude of causality, I need to possess this junior to dissolve these karmic ties. Although this junior’s aptitude is mediocre, his nature is excellent, and he will surely achieve great things. After I leave, you can continue to possess this junior."

Lu Yang had inquired about the character of the Heavenly Venerate of the Firmament from Fairy Eternity, who had given a good account, calling him a genuinely good person.

Lu Yang indeed believed that Xin Ding had the potential to become great; the Western Paradise Temple was blind not to see it. He was a talent worth nurturing and would surely accomplish much.

By helping the Western Paradise Temple nurture talent, they should be thanking him.

"Thank you, predecessor!"

The Heavenly Venerate of the Firmament was thrilled; he needed someone like Xin Ding, whose outstanding qualities made his own life more interesting.

And being so highly praised by Tofu Heavenly Venerable, he surely couldn’t be wrong.

"For now, wait in the secret realm."

"Yes!"

With the matter concluded, Lu Yang retreated back to the Green Peak Sword Small World and returned control to Xin Ding.

Yu Youlan stood there stunned, unable to calm her emotions for a long time.

What had just happened? Facing the Heavenly Venerate of the Firmament, Xin Ding showed no fear and conversed using ancient languages; although she didn’t understand what they discussed, from the Heavenly Venerate’s respectful bow toward Xin Ding, his identity must be more terrifying than she had imagined!

He is indeed the man I fancied.

Coming back to his senses, Xin Ding did not understand what Tofu Heavenly Venerable had said, but seeing the respectful attitude of the Heavenly Venerate of the Firmament towards him, he knew that what Tofu Heavenly Venerable had mentioned before was true, making him nothing but a junior in comparison to Transcendence Tribulation Stage.

This convinced him further not to disclose the matters regarding Tofu Heavenly Venerable, to avoid bringing disaster to the Western Heaven.

"Benefactor Yu, let us go."

Lu Yang did not allow Xin Ding to choose any inheritance. After all, with the Heavenly Venerate of the Firmament staying, the inheritance of the secret realm would eventually belong to Xin Ding.

Although there were people in the Ancient Realm who devoured the Ancient Foundation Establishment Grass raw, becoming Foundation Establishment Stage Cultivators, commanding the winds and summoning the rains within the Ancient Realm, rallying troops and hastily forming small forces to snatch resources.

There emerged Qi Refinement Consummation cultivators who defied expectations by defeating Foundation Establishment Stage Cultivators, creating a sensation for a time.

There was the incident of a female cultivator being drugged by a Holy Land cultivator, and a male cultivator acting heroically to defeat the Holy Land cultivator; afterward, he shared a night of passion with the female cultivator. Filled with guilt afterwards, the male cultivator saw it as an accident while the female cultivator, in fact, harbored a budding affection.

There emerged a series of situations such as Holy Land cultivators secretly struggling amongst themselves for the position of successor.

But none of these had anything to do with Xin Ding and Yu Youlan.

In order not to leave the Ancient Realm prematurely and attract attention, the two stayed in the Inner Hall for three days without going anywhere.

Actually, it was mainly Xin Ding who feared attracting attention. As the Holy Daughter, Yu Youlan had nothing to fear from covetous stares; she stayed in the Inner Hall to keep Xin Ding company.

When the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm closed, everyone automatically left the Ancient Realm.

"How was your harvest?" Zhi Kong asked, curious about their gains upon seeing everyone emerge.

"I only found one Ancient Foundation Establishment Grass," Xin Chen took out a Foundation Establishment Grass, which he had found only on the last day as it was about to end.

He took out a handful of Ancient Foundation Establishment Grass from his bosom, speaking deliberately.

"I found ten."

"Ten?!"

The crowd was astounded, even Zhi Kong somewhat shocked. Finding Foundation Establishment Grass was not simply a matter of luck; it certainly involved competition. Xin Ding was only at the seventh level of Qi Refinement, so how could he outcompete those at the ninth level or Consummation of Qi Refinement?

Just as the crowd was filled with surprise and envy, the people not far away started to stir – it was Yu Youlan running towards them.

Not only the Martial Monk Institute but all cultivators who had come to participate in the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm were surprised – Yu Youlan had never shown such an affectionate demeanor to anyone before!

What had happened between these two in the Chi Xiao Ancient Realm?!

Xin Ding chanted an Amitabha Buddha silently, not understanding why everyone reacted so strongly. Weren’t they all monks who should regard female beauty as skeletal illusions?

Western Paradise Temple, Abbot’s quarters.

On the chessboard, the black and white pieces were clearly demarcated. A tall elder, draped in a lavish kasaya, held a black piece without expression, while an elder in coarse linen garments held a white piece with a smile.

As if frozen in place, the elder in the lavish kasaya was unable to set down his black piece for the longest time. In the end, he sighed softly, no longer persisting, "Junior Brother, you have won."

The coarse-clothed elder was not surprised by the outcome of the chess game, "Master Mingyu, you play chess too hastily." freēnovelkiss.com

The gorgeously robed elder was none other than the abbot of the Western Paradise Temple, Master Mingyu, and the other was the temple’s hidden master, Master Ming Huai, the sweeper of the Scripture Pavilion.

"You’re right, I have been feeling restless lately, sensing that something big is going to happen." Master Mingyu sighed, a sentiment he could only share with his junior brother, Ming Huai.

"A big event?" Master Ming Huai was puzzled, wondering what kind of significant event could possibly befall their Western Paradise Temple.

"I can’t put my finger on it, just a feeling." Master Mingyu shook his head; he had practiced Zen meditation his entire life and often had a certain premonition about things in the unseen world, especially concerning the Western Paradise Temple.

"Then again, it may be that I have been too impatient with my cultivation lately, and my mind state is somewhat unstable," Master Mingyu said with a self-deprecating smile.

"Speaking of issues with the mind state, it’s not just me. Have you heard of Ye Zijin?" Master Mingyu brought up another matter.

"I have heard of him. Isn’t he the one who has been causing trouble across the Buddha Country, building temples, forging Buddha statues, and promoting false Buddhist teachings?" Master Ming Huai didn’t pay much attention to External affairs.

"That’s about right, but the most important thing is that he talks in a very irritating manner, and the elders all have grievances against him, eager to catch him."

Master Ming Huai smiled nonchalantly, seeing it as a minor issue, "How can words be irritating? It seems the younger generation’s cultivation still falls short."

Master Mingyu nodded, "That’s what I think, too, which is why I’ve left Ye Zijin alone, hoping the elders would realize their shortcomings and cultivate their mind state through this."

Master Ming Huai picked up the broom and stood up to take his leave, "Enough chat for now, there’s an intruder in the Scripture Pavilion. I’ll go back and check."

In the first level of the Scripture Pavilion, a shifty figure was skulking about, searching for something.

"Ha, such a daring youth, coming to steal from the Scripture Pavilion."

The figure jumped in fright, not expecting to be discovered.

Turning around, he saw an elderly sweeper at the end of the hallway, who had appeared there without notice.

"I take my leave!"

The figure turned and ran.

"Young man, don’t rush off. Why not keep this old man company for a game of chess?"

The figure’s expression flickered, only to find a chessboard set up before him, with the elderly sweeper sitting opposite him.

"Are you Ye Zijin?" The sweeper’s eyes were cloudy, yet he saw through the identity of the shadowy figure at a glance.

"Yes." Ye Zijin knew he could not escape, so he resigned himself to playing chess.

The two chatted while they played chess.

"To reach the mid-stage of Unification at such a young age, with so many unable to catch you – you’re quite capable."

"I’m old, so I tend to ramble on."

"Not many young ones are willing to listen to an old man like me. In Go, the initial setup dictates the game; in life, planning determines the future. You’ve strayed off the path and joined the Seek Dao Sect; life is an endless sea of suffering, but it’s not too late to turn back..."

The sweeper seeing that Ye Zijin was polite and not as annoying as the rumors suggested, wanted to persuade him a bit more.

Ye Zijin placed the last white stone, looking somewhat embarrassed, "Uh, elder, I’ve won."

The sweeper was taken aback; he loved chess and had never lost before, but today, he had unexpectedly been defeated by a junior.

It was only a game of chess, after all, and the sweeper did not take it to heart; he stroked his beard and laughed heartily, "Old and no longer useful."

Ye Zijin hurriedly offered a smile, "You’re still spry."

As soon as Ye Zijin spoke, he inwardly cursed his misfortune. Ever since he had formed the Yin Yang Golden Core, he had been plagued by this issue, which persisted even after his core had broken to reach Nascent, transformed into a primordial spirit, and unified in the Body Integration Realm.

Of course, this also had to do with his personality, but not significantly.

Because of his knack for shocking statements, he had drawn much envy and not a few had shouted to kill him. Luckily, he was fast on his feet, which is why he had survived thus far.

He came to Buddha Country to train, and although he wouldn’t mention other skills, his ability to escape had visibly improved; even his master, at the Mid Integration Stage, was not as fast as him.

But against someone in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, was being fast still useful?

No, no, he shouldn’t think like that. Since the other party was a venerable senior, surely he wouldn’t stoop to quarrel with a junior... right?

"Senior?" Ye Zijin tentatively called out.

"What’s wrong?" Master Ming Huai looked up, his expression normal, showing no sign of peculiarity.

Ye Zijin breathed a sigh of relief. Worthy of being a senior, his temperament was unlike those of the elders.

He calmly stood up and picked up a broom.

Crack.

Master Ming Huai hadn’t controlled his strength well and had broken the broom that had been used for over a thousand years.

Upon seeing this, Ye Zijin turned and fled. If he didn’t run now, it would be too late!

Watching Ye Zijin flee into the distance, Master Ming Huai took two deep breaths. He was a dignified Great Cultivator in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage. It wasn’t worth it to quarrel over such a trivial matter with a junior; he was a dignified Great Cultivator in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage. It wasn’t worth it to quarrel over such a trivial matter with a junior...

"There, chase him!"

Upon hearing the news about Ye Zijin, numerous elders appeared, some even foregoing their meditation. The commotion was much bigger than when they had invited Lu Yang to Western Paradise Temple on New Year’s Eve.

The entire Western Paradise Temple was brightly lit and engulfed by the aura of Integration. Maintaining his dignity, Master Ming Huai, having called out, did not make a move.

Abbot Master Ming Yu was revisiting a chess game: "So it was this move that was wrong. I was too eager to win at chess, made my move too hastily. It seems that what Master Ming Huai said was right, my Mind State still needs polishing."

Both of them had unbelievably casted the exact same Demon Suppression Seal!

The Elders surged forward, and Elder Kong Xing took the opportunity to sneak away from behind.

Suddenly realizing they had apprehended the wrong person as the one holding the Ruyi Buddha Beads ran away, the Elders finally understood they had caught the wrong one.

The more important the vow is for the Buddhist teachings, the more power of Incense and Fire they will receive."

Regarding the Grand Aspiration Practice Method, Lu Yang had learned some from Master Duanchen of Kaihuang Temple, but it wasn’t as detailed as what his second senior brother was explaining.

Like how Master Duanchen made a grand vow for the prosperity of the Kaihuang Temple’s Incense, which had precedents, and upon fulfillment, enabled him to reach the Void Refinement Stage—Ye Zijin had no such precedent for his grand vow, so he could only make a rough estimate.

Is there no restriction on this Grand Aspiration Practice Method?

Time Immortal’s magic artifact might be hidden there. Tonight, I secretly infiltrated the Scripture Pavilion to find out, but before I could find anything, I got caught by an Elder who was sweeping the floor!"

Lu Yang had heard Immortal Fairy describe the Enlightenment Vision Diagram before; it was just a vague image of Buddha under the Bodhi Tree, nothing special, and not as useful as directly contemplating the Yingtian Immortal. As for the other stuff, although it may count as a chance encounter, it’s not necessarily linked to Time Immortal.

Eldest Senior Sister’s judgment of character is as accurate as ever.

Senior Brother’s Shapeshifting Technique had reached the realm of utter believability, surely he could have deceived those Elders, which would have made gathering information much easier?

Speaking of this, Ye Zijin sighed, "Do you think I haven’t tried that? Initially, I lowered my realm successfully and blended in as a Dining Hall monk. Aside from the moments when I secretly used my cultivation to show off and put others in their place, I always kept a low profile and the monks in the Dining Hall never found out."

"One day, though, the Hall Master cooked too little food, and just as it was the Martial Monk Institute Head’s turn, there was no rice left. He was the only one in the whole temple who didn’t get to eat, and the atmosphere got really awkward."

"In an attempt to ease the tension, I went up there, smiling apologetically. I said to the Institute Head, ’It’s lucky that it’s only the rice that’s missing, not you.’

"Then I was discovered."

"I didn’t want to say it, but as the words came to my lips, they changed."

With a troubled expression, Ye Zijin shook his head and sighed as he explained to Lu Yang, "This is the lingering affliction from the Golden Core Stage. I didn’t expect it to persist into the Body Integration Realm. That’s why I sometimes say things that are inappropriate for the situation."

"You’re so understanding of human nature; you understand what I mean, right, Junior Brother?"

"...I can’t really say."

Seeing that the junior brother didn’t go to the brothel, Ye Zijin brought Lu Yang to a hot pot restaurant instead.

"This is a specialty of Buddha Country. You definitely can’t find this anywhere else. This is the most authentic ’HUHU’ hot pot in the entire Buddha Country."

The hot pot had spread from Great Xia and, once it reached Buddha Country, the hardworking and wise people there modified it.

The result of their modifications was so successful that people in Great Xia didn’t acknowledge it originated from their land.

Lu Yang looked at the murky yellow-brown pot bubbling away and couldn’t muster any appetite.

But not eating would mean not giving face to his senior brother.

Lu Yang didn’t dare to go first, so he only observed his surroundings and was surprised to discover that everyone eating here was a cultivator.

"Senior brother, is this place specifically for cultivators to eat..." ƒгeewebnovёl.com

Before he could finish his question, Lu Yang saw his second senior brother scoop up slices of meat from the boiling pot with his hand, looking up in confusion at his junior brother, "What did you just ask?"

"Nothing."

Lu Yang’s eyelids twitched as he watched; no wonder only cultivators came here to eat—without cultivation level, one couldn’t even manage to eat.

With many deserts and scarce vegetation, the people of Buddha Country had become accustomed to eating with their hands.

Seeing that his second senior brother was eating, Lu Yang had no choice but to stiffen his neck and mimic others in fishing out food from the hot pot.

After overcoming the psychological hurdle, Lu Yang was shocked to discover that he now had to overcome the challenge of taste.

It tasted terrible.

"Shall this Immortal give it a try?" This sparked Fairy Eternity’s curiosity, leading her to attempt fishing food out of the hot pot after possessing Lu Yang.

"Indeed, it’s really bad."

After struggling through an unpleasant meal, Lu Yang, worried that his second senior brother might lead him on another bizarre experience, left his contact information and looked for an excuse to leave.

"Senior brother, I’ll be returning to the Sect in a couple of months. Do you want to come back with me?"

If not even the Secret Realm had any clues left by the Time Immortal, Lu Yang felt there was no need to stay in Buddha Country any longer—it was time to go back.

Being away for so long, the Eldest Senior Sister was sure to worry about him.

Ye Zijin thought for a moment, "That sounds good. I haven’t been back to the Sect for a long time. By the way, is Master still not at the Sect as usual?"

"He’s not. I haven’t seen him for two years now. I heard he’s always busy dealing with enemies in the outside world, with no time to return."

"That’s good." Ye Zijin heaved a sigh of relief, "In Buddha Country, I accidentally provoked a few at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, and had to divert this trouble to Master."

"...No wonder the number of Master’s enemies hasn’t decreased."

Lu Yang returned to the Martial Monk Institute and slept soundly as Xin Ding.

Previously, when his second senior brother and the Elders were battling in the sky above Western Paradise Temple, Xin Ding was woken by the noise, set up a soundproofing Array Method, and continued to sleep.

To Xin Ding, the outcome of Ye Zijin’s and the Elders’ battle was not important, so there was no need to specifically wake up to watch.

Upon entering the Green Blade Sword Small World, he was surprised to find a small wooden house that appeared quite elegant, evidently a lot of hard work had gone into it.

Qing Yan, with hands rubbing together and a sheepish smile, said, "We saw there was nowhere to live here, and we were worried it would be beneath you. So, taking the initiative, we built this little wooden house. If you’re satisfied with this small house, we’re relieved, but if there’s any design you’re displeased with, the three of us will rebuild it anew."

Elder Qing Yan had reached the stage of Transcendence Tribulation not solely because of his terrifying talent, amazing strategic mind, relentless perseverance, and luck.

At critical moments, he knew when to cave in.

"Not bad," Lu Yang said as he strolled with his hands behind his back, inspecting the small cabin with a refined air.

After all, it was a Great Power from the stage of Transcendence Tribulation that had constructed it, making it extraordinary. The workmanship of the small cabin was exquisite, devoid of even a single splinter.

The cabin contained everything, including tables, chairs, benches, beds, and wardrobes.

"Wait, why is there only one bed?" Lu Yang frowned. If he was to sleep here, where would Fairy sleep?

Elder Qing Yan was surprised, "Given your relationship with Great Immortal, aren’t you supposed to share the same bed?"

"Hm?"

"Hm?"

Realizing his mistake and having a disagreement with the leader, Elder Qing Yan knew the fault was his and quickly corrected himself, "It was my oversight. I’ll make another bed right away."

"One bed is just fine," Immortal Fairy floated out and thought the small cabin was acceptable. Although it was nowhere close to Zhu Tian, it was still decent; even the Great Xia Palace was made by someone at the stage of Transcendence Tribulation.

"This..." Elder Qing Yan’s gaze wandered uncertainly, not sure whom to listen to. Logically, he should heed Great Immortal’s words, but offending Great Immortal’s favored one also seemed to promise no good ending.

"Fairy, if there’s only one bed, where would I sleep?"

"Isn’t this bed quite large, too large for us both?" Immortal Fairy gestured, indicating the bed was even larger than those in the Spiritual Space.

"As the Emperor of the Great Bean Dynasty, with a body worth thousands in gold, it would be presumptuous and terrifying for me to share a bed with Your Majesty. That’s what male consorts do."

Lu Yang replied seriously, "No."

"Well, alright then, let’s have two beds."

Seeing this, Elder Qing Yan thought it might be better to follow Lu Yang’s lead in the future.

After one night, the Elders of the Western Paradise Temple were still tirelessly searching for any trace of Ye Zijin, having turned Western Heaven City upside down without success.

Xin Ding’s life became more interesting due to Yu Youlan’s one-sided flirtation, leading to frequent challenges from Cultivators, not few of whom held enmity towards Yu Youlan. They were all at the Consummation of Qi Refinement level, and to fight Xin Ding at their level would be seen as bullying the weak, so they sent subordinates equivalent to Xin Ding’s seven layers of Qi Cultivation.

With the Yinglong Visualization, having learned the Arhat Fist and Lion Roar Skill, Xin Ding was invincible at his level.

Cultivators of the seventh layer of Qi would be defeated, then those of the eighth, followed by the ninth, until the ones at the Consummation of Qi Refinement themselves stepped into the fray.

Xin Ding fought like a force of nature, growing stronger with each battle, nurturing his combat skills and understanding of the Arhat Fist and Lion Roar Skill, which was awe-inspiring.

"With such talent, he surely has a place in the Upper Temple of Martial Monks in the future," someone commented.

"It’s hard to say; he has the lowest tier, the Five Spirits Root. Although he excels in the Qi Cultivation Stage, that is just because of the limited techniques available in this stage, and he just happens to have learned the Lion Roar Skill, which isn’t typically accessible during the Qi Cultivation Stage."

"Once he reaches the Foundation Establishment Stage, he will falter. It’s only a matter of time before the glory fades."

"True, did you think a mere Servant Monk could strut around indefinitely?"

"Even if he has a relative at the Divinity Transformation Stage, what of it? He is still just a Five Spirits Root. Can he really surpass our Four Spirit Roots in cultivation talent?"

Xin Ding faced various gossip about him indifferently, disregarding it and focusing on his cultivation.

Two months later, Master Mingyu summoned all monks at the Qi Cultivation Stage to enter the Western Heaven Secret Realm, from the Servant Monk Institute, Martial Monk Institute, Dining Hall, Precepts Court... It was an annual summoning by Master Mingyu, but no one in the Western Paradise Temple knew what was inside the Western Heaven Secret Realm, and even if they questioned the monks afterward, it was futile, for they had all forgotten.

All monks of the Qi Cultivation Stage entered the secret realm, leaving the Western Paradise Temple eerily empty, prompting two managers of the Martial Monk Institute to start a casual conversation.

"Is there some sort of realm restriction for this Western Heaven Secret Realm, otherwise why only allow cultivators in the Qi Cultivation Stage and not let us enter?"

"Is it possible that we entered when we were at the Qi Cultivation Stage?"

"Ah, you have a point."

For many, it was their first time seeing Master Mingyu. The monks could hardly hide their excitement, although they had no idea where Master Mingyu was leading them.

It was also Lu Yang’s first encounter with the ruler of Buddha Country.

The Western Heaven Secret Realm was hidden somewhere within this chaotic mist, making its exact location unknown to all.

"The realm is open, right within the mouth of a stone lion," said Fairy Eternity, and apart from Master Mingyu, only the Immortal Fairy could discern what was happening in the entire chaotic forbidden area.

Master Mingyu tweaked a tooth of the stone lion and the entrance to the Western Heaven Secret Realm opened, with all the monks entering in succession.

"Such a thick Buddha Breath." Upon entering the secret realm, through his Green Blade Sword Small World, Lu Yang could feel the Buddha Breath from the outside world, leaving him astounded.

This was Buddha Breath used for purification and deliverance, but Lu Yang had never encountered such intense Buddha Breath before.

All the monks stood blankly with empty eyes.

"Are they under the influence of Buddha Breath, entering an illusion?" Lu Yang speculated as his cultivation technique was highly sensitive to illusions; it seemed that facing illusions was the test of the Western Heaven Secret Realm.

"I wonder if anyone from this batch will pass the test," Master Mingyu was uncertain, as it had been a long time since any monk had passed the secret realm test, not even he had passed, tracing back 12,000 years when his own master was at the Qi Cultivation Stage.

"Perhaps Xin Zhen of the Precepts Court holds some hope," Master Mingyu looked towards a monk with large ears, whose face resembled a Buddha statue. He had heard from the head of the Precepts Court that this Xin Zhen was a rare and admirable seedling, naturally resembling a Buddha, proficient in Buddhist doctrine, and a person of integrity, praised by all who knew him.

As for Xin Ding, he had also heard of him, but Xin Ding was famous for his combat power rather than for Buddhist teachings.

To pass the test of the secret realm, one’s cultivation level wasn’t important—it was the understanding of Buddhist teachings that mattered.

"Let’s see their choices in the illusion," Master Mingyu chanted a Buddhist invocation, merged with the Buddha Breath, and entered the illusion.

In the illusion, Xin Zhen was baking in the harsh sun, shirtless, bearing heavy rocks to construct a deity statue. Accidentally, a rock fell and broke a corner. Seeing this, the overseer was furious and began whipping him. Xin Zhen pressed his palms together, chanted sutras, and entered a state of self-transcendence, oblivious to the physical pain.

"To endure such pain without a change in expression—impressive," Master Mingyu praised.

"Have I heard that Xin Ding is also a promising seedling from the Martial Monk Institute?" Master Mingyu remembered Xin Ding and entered his illusion.

As soon as he entered the illusion, he heard a series of agonizing screams, distressingly acute.

Master Mingyu frowned. How could Xin Ding have such a disposition, unable to bear even a bit of pain?

Then he saw Xin Ding whipping the overseer with a lash.

Master Mingyu was stunned by this scene. The requirement for this stage was that the monk had to endure the whipping without shouting in pain to pass the test.

Of course, the secret realm wouldn’t allow the overseer to keep on whipping forever. Eventually, a stone would fall from the statue and kill the overseer. freёnovelkiss.com

The overseer had done much evil, and his death by the falling stone aligned with Buddhism’s principle that good is rewarded with good and evil with evil.

Having presided over thousands of Western Heaven Secret Realms, Master Mingyu had seen countless monks make decisions in the secret realm. The greatest challenge of this stage was to endure the pain. Ninety percent of the monks couldn’t withstand it until the overseer received his retribution and would cry out in pain. Only the ones who struggled and gritted their teeth could hold on.

That’s why he had high hopes for Xin Zhen, who had entered a state of ’forgetting both self and objects.’

Buddhism advocates understanding pain through mindful contemplation, thereby achieving a state beyond suffering.

However, seeing Xin Ding strike first was unprecedented, and judging from the overseer’s screams, Xin Ding was extraordinarily forceful.

"Wait, why are you hitting him?" Master Mingyu couldn’t help but reveal himself. He could control the Western Heaven Secret Realm to an extent, and soon Xin Ding would forget he had appeared.

"He was going to hit me," said Xin Ding calmly; in fact, his expression had remained unchanged even as he struck.

In the Western Heaven Secret Realm, monks naturally display their most instinctual reactions and cannot fake or lie.

"Don’t you know that our Buddhist ways promote observing pain without changing expression?"

"Yes, but if it were my fault, I would have admitted it if I were beaten. But now, it’s these overseers overworking us beyond limits; I grew too weak to carry the stones, and thus they fell. If it’s the overseer’s fault, why should I be beaten?" Xin Ding argued forcefully, insisting on reason even to the abbot.

"Do you know that our Buddhist teachings emphasize that good deeds are rewarded with good and evil with evil, and this overseer who wantonly whipped others will receive his due karma?"

"Isn’t he receiving his karma now, by being beaten by me?"

"I..."

Master Mingyu was at a loss for words, unable to find a rebuttal.

This stage tested "endurance," and since Xin Ding had not cried out in pain throughout, he had successfully passed.

In front of Xin Chen, who entered the Martial Monk Institute with Xin Ding, was a wide river with two people beside it: his elderly monk master and a beautiful but timid woman.

The woman was afraid to cross the river.

After crossing the river and parting with the woman, Xin Chen furrowed his brow, extremely puzzled, and after holding in his confusion for a long time, he finally could not help but ask, "Master, wouldn’t this be a violation of the precept of lust?"

The old monk, with loving care, patted Xin Ding’s head, "Xin Ding, I have already let go, but you have not."

Xin Zhen of the Precepts Court witnessed the whole event without speaking. Following the moment the old monk let go of the woman, he too let go, harboring no doubts in his heart.

Xin Chen failed, Xin Zhen passed.

Master Mingyu smiled, quite satisfied with Xin Zhen; he passed two consecutive tests in a manner that pleased him greatly.

The theme of this round was "letting go."

Buddhism advocates that feminine allure is like a pretty skeleton; a true monk should view it as nothing, and being able to do that means no questions would be asked.

Under the influence of Buddha Breath, which makes hiding the truth impossible, and having witnessed the process of carrying the woman across the river, if testers harbored doubts, they would surely ask, and asking meant that they had not let go of the issue, thus failing the test.

"How did Xin Ding do?" Master Mingyu, recalling Xin Ding’s unique performance in the previous round, became somewhat curious about him.

He entered Xin Ding’s Illusionary Realm, and Xin Ding’s choice surprised him yet again.

Xin Ding rushed ahead, carrying the woman across the river before the old monk, and because Xin Ding was still a minor and not quite tall enough, carrying the woman would get her shoes wet, so he simply picked her up, in a quite indecent posture.

Never in thousands of times in the Secret Realm had anyone ever done this!

Master Mingyu was especially puzzled and once Xin Ding crossed the river and appeared again, he wanted to ask for clarification.

"Xin Ding, why did you carry that woman across the river?"

Seeing Master Mingyu appear, Xin Ding was extremely surprised.

"Abbot, how come you have not let go of this matter?"

Master Mingyu’s eyelids twitched uncontrollably, grateful that he was now in charge of the Secret Realm and not the one being tested by it. Otherwise, the words "Xin Ding" would have been enough to kick him out.

With Master Mingyu’s appearance, Xin Ding regained his memory and remembered he was in the midst of the second trial.

However, he didn’t quite understand why the task of ferrying someone across a river would cause the Abbot to appear again.

Could this be a matter of great significance?

It must be that the Abbot’s actions held some profound meaning. It’s just that his own perception was mediocre, unable to penetrate the Abbot’s profound intent.

Not knowing is nothing to be ashamed of, it’s better to ask for guidance.

"May I ask, Abbot, if there is a problem with how I ferried the person?"

The initially eager to speak Master Mingyu was stunned into silence by Xin Ding’s question.

Indeed, what could be wrong with ferrying someone?

"There’s nothing wrong. You did well," said Master Mingyu with a complex expression as he gazed at Xin Ding, unsure if Xin Ding’s response was a mere coincidence or a genuine insight. Regardless of which it was, Xin Ding might have a chance to pass the trial of the Secret Realm.

It seems that Xin Zhen isn’t the only promising candidate in this trial.

Having said this, Master Mingyu turned and left, leaving Xin Ding standing there, utterly bewildered.

Why would the Abbot leave directly without giving an answer after he’d asked his question?

The pass rate for the second round of trials is even lower than the first, with ninety percent of the young monks unable to surpass this challenge.

After the two rounds of trials, only a handful of young monks remain, besides Xin Ding, the rest are renowned for their profound Buddha Nature.

The thick Buddha Breath once again enveloped the area, signaling the onset of the third trial. ƒгeewebnovёl.com

Xin Zhen found himself in an Illusionary Realm recalling his identity within the realm — a Zen Master. Someone who took great displeasure at him was cursing him.

"You uncultured beast, born without manners..."

The person’s words were incredibly vile and offensive to the ears.

Xin Zhen brought his palms together and closed his eyes, entering a Meditative Trance, as if he hadn’t heard the other person’s insults at all.

Eventually, the person grew tired of cursing and looked at Xin Zhen with confusion: "I’ve been cursing you for so long, why haven’t you reacted at all?"

Xin Zhen opened his eyes, his gaze as calm as the surface of a still pond, and with a faint smile, observed, "If someone gives you a gift, but you refuse to accept it, to whom does the gift belong?"

The person replied: "It belongs to the person who was giving the gift."

Xin Zhen smiled and said, "Exactly. If I don’t accept your insults, you’re essentially cursing yourself."

Xin Zhen passed the trial.

This round tested "Jie Chen," the ability to remain calm in the face of others’ insults.

"Not harboring anger or hatred, well done," Master Mingyu silently assessed Xin Zhen, who was neither arrogant nor rash, standing out among the monks. He made the same choices as Master Mingyu in the three trials.

"How is Xin Ding doing?" After two rounds of trials, Master Mingyu had already placed Xin Ding on the same level as Xin Zhen.

No sooner had Master Mingyu entered Xin Ding’s Illusionary Realm than he heard Xin Ding’s forceful retort.

"You’re the uncultured beast, born without manners..."

The two exchanged insults vehemently, a scene so intense that even passing dogs weren’t spared a cursing.

"Stop!"

Unable to hold back, Master Mingyu made his presence known once more, surprised by how this young monk’s choices were continually unexpected.

Those who had made it to the third trial were all Buddhist Cultivators with innate Buddha Nature, who, even if irritated, would at most show anger, but would not stoop to cursing each other.

Xin Ding, on the other hand, engaged in a verbal brawl.
