Looking at Xin Ding’s calm demeanor, he suddenly remembered that Xin Ding had been completely serene while trading insults, not at all resembling someone in a quarrel!

Xin Ding truly believed he was merely "returning a gift"!

The third round of trials ended, and only Xin Zhen and Xin Ding passed, with the other monks being eliminated, a precedent unseen in previous trials.

In the past, either no one passed all three trials, or only one person did.

"Hoo."

With a gentle breath, Master Mingyu cleared away the Buddha Breath, revealing a path that led to an altar at the end. The altar displayed Shariputra, an incense burner, scriptures, and other items for venerating the temple’s treasure.

Lu Yang finally saw the treasure clearly—it was an axe. The blade was damaged, and the surface had an elegant handprint pressed into it.

"The Sky Opening Axe?!"

This was the very Immortal Axe that the Yingtian Immortal boasted of—an unparalleled Immortal Object from Ancient Times.

The Yingtian Immortal had forged the axe from countless pieces of Immortal Gold, after a thousand hammerings and a hundred refinings. The axe’s handle was a segment of the Time Immortal’s main stem, containing the power of time, enabling it to cleave the heavens with the capacity to open the sky.

The Yingtian Immortal had once said that he was ambushed by Ashy Bean during the Great Qian Period, and after that battle, the Sky Opening Axe went missing. So, it had ended up in the possession of the Western Paradise Temple?

Lu Yang understood that the battle between the Yingtian Immortal and Ashy Bean must have been a fierce one. During the fight, the Sky Opening Axe had endured the power of Yingtian Immortal’s tribulation as well as Ashy Bean’s annihilating force.

The handprint on the axe’s surface must have been left by Ashy Bean.

"This object is very likely the legendary Sky Opening Axe, accidentally acquired by our temple in the early days of Great Qian," explained Master Mingyu. "Upon obtaining the Sky Opening Axe, it contained a force that could destroy everything, and no one could approach it. A mere fraction of its released power could lead to utter devastation."

"In order to purify this force, generations of our eminent monks worked tirelessly, finally purifying the axe completely while also imbuing it with Buddha Breath."

"However, an Immortal Object is no ordinary item. Not just anyone is worthy of it. To earn its recognition, one must first pass through the three trials of Buddha Breath, be able to withstand the Buddha Breath within the axe, and then the Immortal Axe chooses its owner, granting only those it selects the right to wield it."

During the Qi Cultivation Stage, Master Mingyu had passed the three trials of Buddha Breath but did not gain the Sky Opening Axe’s recognition. It was uncertain whether either of the two who had passed the trials this time would earn that recognition.

"So, the treasure of the Western Heaven Temple is the Sky Opening Axe," a proud voice suddenly emitted from Xin Zhen’s body.

A cultivator with patterns of hourglasses and coronae on his clothes flew out from Xin Zhen’s Storage Ring, stretching his limbs.

"After lying in wait so many times, I finally found a little monk capable of passing through the three trials of Buddha Breath."

"Who are you?" Master Mingyu’s expression changed drastically as he realized the intruder had entered the Western Heaven Secret Realm undetected on multiple occasions.

The fact that the stranger had made such a brazen appearance meant he must have come prepared!

"The Divine Monarch of Great Qian, Sichen. I wonder, Master, have you heard of him?"

"The God of Time, Suiyue? The one who governed time during the Great Qian Period?!"

Master Mingyu immediately remembered the legend of the God of Time, a great figure from 300,000 years ago.

His concern for the Western Paradise Temple facing a crisis, had it finally come to pass?

"It seems the Master is well-read and knowledgeable," the God of Time said with a grin, his attitude disdainful as he didn’t take Master Mingyu seriously.

"You deceived me!" Xin Zhen realized and laughed at himself for thinking that finding the Storage Ring was a stroke of luck, and that the other party demanded him to be cultivated to the standards of a high-ranking monk.

It was all a scam, just to make sure he could pass the three trials of Buddha Breath!

"When have I deceived you? I have given you everything you wanted, haven’t I?" the God of Time said with a smile, looking at Xin Zhen with eyes that did not see a person but a tool, this kid was no longer of any use to him.

The sacred treasure of the Western Paradise Temple had caused quite a bit of trouble for the Great Qian Dynasty during the Great Qian Period, their armies had set out several times but to no avail.

After awakening in the Great Xia Era, the God of Time quickly set his sights on this sacred treasure.

He discovered that Master Mingyu had not gained the recognition of the sacred treasure and could not use it, a golden opportunity presented itself.

The sacred treasure of the Western Paradise Temple was enveloped in Buddha Breath; taking it by force was impossible, one must pass the three trials of Buddha Breath, for which he had hidden himself within the Immortal Artifact Level Storage Ring, allowing the Qi Cultivation Stage monk to find the ring.

The Western Heaven Secret Realm had the ability to discern realms, only an Immortal Artifact capable of concealment could deceive the Secret Realm, even Immortal Treasures of the next level down could not fool it. freewebnovel.com

After a hundred years and hundreds of attempts, he finally passed the three trials this time and beheld the Sky Opening Axe.

The three trials had consumed a vast amount of Buddha Breath; it was at its weakest moment, and the perfect time for him to take the Sky Opening Axe!

"It’s time for the Sky Opening Axe to have an owner."

The God of Time had governed time during the Great Qian Period and had condensed the outline of the Time Dao Fruit; the handle of the Sky Opening Axe was part of the Time Immortal’s body, so there was some connection between him and the Sky Opening Axe. Even if he couldn’t become the owner of the Sky Opening Axe, taking it away was no problem.

"You dare!"

Master Mingyu roared in fury, and the Buddha bearing fierce flames and wielding a sharp sword appeared behind him.

It was the Unmoving Ming King of Buddhist legend!

With the appearance of the Unmoving Ming King Dharma Aspect, both movement and stillness could destroy heaven and earth.

"Why shouldn’t I dare?" The God of Time’s palm revealed an hourglass, the sands flowing slowly, time becoming incredibly sluggish!

He directly seized the Sky Opening Axe placed on the altar, and with a light swing, he could shatter space and carve out a path to the outside world.

He had not fully gained the recognition of the Sky Opening Axe, merely using a part of its power.

"Stop!"

The God of Time couldn’t keep time slow forever; as soon as time returned to normal, Master Mingyu immediately gave chase!

"Who dares run wild in my Western Paradise Temple!"

The commotion of breaking through the Western Heaven Secret Realm was too great, and the monks of the Western Heaven Temple noticed the disturbance.

Two figures flew out from two corners of the temple, blocking the God of Time.

"Ming Huai, Ming Tian?" The God of Time looked at the two old monks with a smile that was not quite a smile; one in the Late Tribulation Stage, the other in the Middle Tribulation Stage.

"My fellow Junior Brothers, stop him!" Master Mingyu shouted from behind, his face full of rage, as if the true Unmoving Ming King had descended to earth!

"Vajra Demon Suppression!"

To fulfill the supreme vow, Master of Righteous Virtue established the Suspension Temple, which became the source of Great Xia’s Buddhist teachings. From that time, countless temples rose from the ground, appearing in Great Xia and forming a force alongside the sects.

When Master of Righteous Virtue fulfilled the supreme vow, the Buddha Country shook, and it was recorded in the annals of history.

Fortunate to witness this scene in his lifetime.

The Time Immortal, seeing Immortal Fairy, was also extremely excited, "Immortal, you have really resurrected?"

"Yes, it was Little Yang... Lu Yang who resurrected me!"

Little Yang? The Time Immortal paused for a moment, what sort of strange appellation was this?

Then the Time Immortal looked solemnly at Lu Yang and expressed his heartfelt gratitude with two words, "Thank you."

"No, it’s nothing, just a coincidence."

Although every first meeting with Jiang Lianyi, Ao Ling, and Yingtian Immortal resulted in heavy thanks when they learned he had resurrected the Immortal Fairy, such treatment still made Lu Yang slightly uncomfortable.

"A mere coincidence is quite enough." They had strived for a hundred thousand years to achieve what Lu Yang had, and whether it was a fluke or not, it remained a tremendous favor.

Time Immortal glanced at the wooden plaque hanging from Lu Yang’s chest, and recalling the past, he sighed internally. Initially, through the time channel, he saw a part of himself on Lu Yang and speculated whether his future self would meet with disaster.

He was extremely cautious, yet his predictions still came to pass—he truly had met with disaster.

"By the way, Time, how are you still alive?"

The Time Immortal looked strangely at them. Was this a question one should ask upon first meeting?

However, considering Immortal Eternity’s personality, asking such a direct question did seem reasonable.

"How much do you know about the Fire Dynasty?"

"The Fire Dynasty? We’ve met Lianyi, Xiao Ling, and Ying Tian. We know quite a bit about the affairs of the Fire Dynasty now."

"You’ve met Ying Tian? Where is he now?"

"He lives inside an Ancient Ring Small World. The Ancient Ring is in the hands of a disciple from the Laurel Fairy Palace."

"I see. When I obtained the Sky Opening Axe, I thought something had happened to him. It’s good that he’s alive."

"Since you’ve met Ying Tian, then you probably know almost as much as I do about the affairs of the Fire Dynasty. He knows as much as I do, so there’s not much to talk about."

"I heard from Ying Tian that you were secretly attacked at the end of the Fire Dynasty era. Who did it?"

The Time Immortal shook his head lightly. "I don’t know. But it’s definitely one of the three of them. One among them was possessed by someone pulling the strings from behind the scenes!"

"You can use the Time Dao Fruit for time retrospection. How could someone secretly attack you?"

Like a scene from thirty thousand years ago, the Time Immortal slowly exhaled, his expression grave. "My Dao Fruit was tampered with, preventing me from performing time retrospection. I suspect that the hidden manipulator’s Dao Fruit is also related to time."

Immortal Fairy Eternity puzzled, "Also related to time? How is that possible? You possess a time-related Dao Fruit. How could they have one too?"

"That is unknown. It’s just a hunch. Perhaps other Dao Fruits could also have an effect on time retrospection."

"What happened afterward?"

"After the sneak attack, I was severely wounded. The Firmament Tree body was beyond recovery, so I had no choice but to abandon it. My soul performed astral projection, leaping thousands of years into the Great Qian Period. However, I didn’t stay in the Great Qian but chose to go to the Western regions instead."

The Nian Beast can leap through time, and naturally, the Time Immortal could as well.

"Without a physical body and only my soul remaining, if I encountered Silent Extermination Immortal or the hidden manipulator, I wouldn’t have the strength to fight back."

"To construct a true form, I established the Buddha Country in the Western regions and hid inside this Buddha statue in the Mahavira Hall of Western Paradise Temple. Only the abbots of successive generations knew of my existence."

"This Mahavira Hall was constructed using the Power of Incense and Fire, creating a Small World inside, capable of evading the perception of Silent Extermination Immortal."

The Mahavira Hall being brimming with incense is not unusual and wouldn’t raise suspicion.

"In the Buddha Country, I promoted that Buddhist cultivators should transform alms into building a Golden Body for the Buddha. Gradually, this became one of the methods for Buddhist cultivation."

"The act of Buddhist cultivators building a Golden Body for the Buddha would generate the Power of Incense and Fire. As the Buddha, I absorbed part of this incense power."

"At one point, I incidentally found the Sky Opening Axe belonging to Yingtian Immortal, which I used as the treasure of the Western Paradise Temple to conceal my existence."

"Whenever the Western Paradise Temple faced danger, I would predict the future and advise them to use the Sky Opening Axe at the most opportune time to overcome crises."

"I’ve observed that this Lu Yang’s Immortal’s Body is formed by the Power of Incense and Fire, but it cannot be maintained for long and cannot leave the Buddha Country."

"Such a body can’t withstand intense combat." Saying this, the Time Immortal paused for a moment, looking at Lu Yang with evident envy.

"Of course, that is assuming Lu Yang doesn’t possess the Initial Form of the Immortal Dao Fruit."

"I’ve been accumulating strength to shape a permanent Immortal Body."

"The accumulation of incense power is a lengthy process, and the waiting is rather dull. So, I randomly performed time leaps. It could be a few years, a dozen, or dozens of years. At each time node I leaped to, I had the abbot of Western Paradise Temple tell me about the events that had occurred over those years."

"Until just now, during a time leap, I sensed Master Ming Yu calling out to me, saying that the Western Paradise Temple was in grave danger. I also sensed fluctuations from the Time Dao Fruit Outline and the Initial Form of the Immortal Dao Fruit, which prompted me to jump to the current time node."

"Has your immortal body been fully shaped?" Lu Yang asked, aware that the immortal body the Time Immortal had been condensing for three hundred thousand years felt much stronger than the one he temporarily condensed.

"It was completed over a decade ago," replied the Time Immortal with a smile, indicating his current peak state.

"Do you know Tang Chuanwu?"

"Tang Chuanwu? Oh, he’s the kid to whom I granted the ability of Time Retrospection after foreseeing the possibility of him encountering a deadly calamity in the future."

"To test the reaction of the hidden enemy behind the scenes?" Lu Yang asked again.

The Time Immortal looked at Lu Yang with surprise and revealed a smile, "Exactly."

"Although I wasn’t able to clearly see who ambushed me back then, the hidden enemy also isn’t sure whether I saw them or not. So, I gave Tang Chuanwu the ability of Time Retrospection to inform the hidden enemy that I am still alive. They will surely want to find me and might reveal their flaws in their haste."

Lu Yang thought to himself that it indeed was as he suspected. When he had previously speculated about the user of the Time Dao Fruit, he wondered if the user was using Tang Chuanwu to send a message to the hidden enemy.

What message to shout? It was the Time Immortal informing the hidden enemy, "I am still alive."

Later on, Lu Yang also learned the origin of the Time Seeking Immortal Order, which used the oppression of a Dao Fruit over an immature Dao Fruit to locate the Time Immortal.

The suppression of a Dao Fruit over its immature form is not something you can simply escape by hiding in a Small World; otherwise, the Qilin Immortal would have long ago hidden in a Small World, allowing the outsiders Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi to become immortals.

The fact that the Great Qian Dynasty was able to create the Time Seeking Immortal Order indicates that the user of the Time Dao Fruit existed during the Great Qian Period.

Both of these facts imply the possibility that the Time Immortal is still alive.

Thus, when Lu Yang saw the Time Immortal in the Mahavira Hall, he wasn’t too surprised.

But this gives rise to another question—just who is the reincarnation of Li Haoran?

If Li Haoran is not the reincarnation of the Time Immortal, then could he be the reincarnation of the immortal who was possessed by the hidden enemy?!

As long as Li Haoran continues to improve his cultivation level, he will be able to revive his memories and thus learn who he was in his first life.

If that’s the case, then the fact that Junior Brother Li is a reincarnation must not become known to others.

If the hidden enemy finds out about Junior Brother Li’s existence, they will certainly stop at nothing to kill him!

"Young friend Lu Yang, since you’ve brought up Tang Chuanwu, does that mean you’ve met him?"

"I have. The hidden enemy has made a move, but they didn’t act directly, leaving few clues," Lu Yang replied.

"I see," sighed the Time Immortal with a hint of regret. The hidden enemy indeed is very cautious.

Suddenly, a knocking sound came from outside the door of the Mahavira Hall.

"Junior Brother, are you in there?"

"Who is it?!" The Time Immortal was startled.

"Hey, just a little girl," the Immortal Fairy said casually, waving her hand, "Little Yang, go open the door."

While Lu Yang went to open the door, Immortal Fairy quietly sent a message to the Time Immortal.

"Hey Time, did you say before that the future is not set in stone?"

The Time Immortal paused for a moment, then nodded, "I did say that, what about it?"

"The Nian Beast carried us here to Buddha Country, and on the way, we entered the Time Torrent. We saw things from the past, as well as a glimpse of the future."

"So what did you see?" The Time Immortal’s expression turned curious; he had never seen the Immortal Fairy acting so hesitantly before.

"What I saw, it was me reluctantly saying goodbye to Little Yang, saying ’I really can’t bear to leave you.’"

The Time Immortal was immediately taken aback.

"What?"

"That’s why I’m asking you, can the future I saw be changed?"

Time Immortal’s expression became serious, as he realized this was an extremely important matter, "What time in the future did you see?"

Lu Yang pushed open the door of the Mahavira Hall, where outside stood a swordswoman in a long white robe, wearing a bamboo hat covered with white cloth, concealing her face.

Upon seeing Lu Yang, the swordswoman took off her hat, revealing her delicate face, it was the Eldest Senior Sister.

"Eldest Senior Sister, why did you come?" Lu Yang was pleasantly surprised as he clearly hadn’t called for her.

"Your Second Senior Brother contacted me with a relay paper, saying something happened at the Western Paradise Temple."

Lu Yang felt he had everything under control, and indeed it was so, but clearly Ye Zijin didn’t think the same.

"Then why don’t I have it?"

"I was worried about the safety of the Second Disciple and the Third Junior Sister, so I gave them relay papers. Of course, you don’t need such a thing."

Yun Zhi studied her junior brother, whom she hadn’t seen for months, and rarely showed a hint of a smile.

"After the Nian Beast took you away, Mengmeng was quite worried about you. It seems you did well in Buddha Country, even condensing an Immortal Body," she said.

Touching the back of his head, Lu Yang smiled sheepishly, "I just took a shortcut. Please come in, Senior Sister. Fairy and Time Immortal are inside."

"Oh, you found Time Immortal too?" Yun Zhi knew that her junior brother could take care of himself. He could handle situations on his own while traveling and even encounter such fortunate adventures afterward.

He seemed to have heard the name Yun Zhi from Ming Yu, describing her as the true Sect Leader of the Seek Dao Sect.

Fairy Eternity stood proudly between Lu Yang and Yun Zhi, pointing at herself: "I am the strongest from Ancient Times."

Then she pointed to Yun Zhi on her right: "Miss Yun is the strongest of the present day."

"Little Yang is the strongest of the future."

Embracing both to her left and right, Fairy Eternity chuckled happily, "We three are the strongest cultivators of the past, present, and future!"

"Isn’t there something in Buddhism about a Past Buddha, Present Buddha, and Future Buddha? Time, when you look back, you should include the three of us," she suggested.

"The strongest of the present?" Time Immortal was startled. It wasn’t easy to earn such high praise from someone as proud as Eternity.

But given that Lu Yang was dubbed "the strongest of the future," he couldn’t help but feel that the "strongest of the present" title was somewhat inflated.

"What, you don’t believe it? If you don’t believe it, why don’t you spar with her?" Fairy Eternity egged on.

Time Immortal truly didn’t believe it, as if not for an accident along the way, he would have been the first to become an immortal. And afterwards, he came into possession of the mysterious Time Dao Fruit; besides Fairy Eternity, he really feared no one.

"Then, let’s try!" Having not had the chance to flex his muscles since condensing the Incense Immortal Body, this was the perfect opportunity!

Yun Zhi and Time Immortal faced each other, the atmosphere tense. Time Immortal used the Time Dao Fruit to examine all future possibilities!

"Please enlighten me, senior," Yun Zhi said calmly.

"Wait a moment." Just before the battle started, Time Immortal suddenly spoke, "Immortal, what did you say just now?"

"Spar with her?"

"The sentence before that."

"What, you don’t believe it?"

"I believe it."

In ancient times, the Time Immortal seldom faced defeat, primarily because he could foresee the future, knowing whether his chances of winning or losing a battle were higher.

This ability was praised by Fairy Eternity as the "Great Invincible Pill"!

After viewing all possible futures, the Time Immortal burst into a cold sweat and cursed Ming Yu for being unreliable under his breath.

"The true Sect Leader of Seek Dao Sect? With such an astonishing cultivation level, saying she is the real ruler of Great Xia would be more like it!"

Thinking this, a smile piled upon the Time Immortal’s face, which already bore a Buddha-like serenity, becoming even more benevolent.

"I have known Fairy Eternity for a very long time, how could I not believe her words?"

"She said you are the strongest in the world, you definitely are the strongest in the world!"

The Time Immortal altered the future merely through his words without anyone noticing, a testament to his formidable power!

"So you’re saying I am truly the strongest in the future?" Lu Yang pointed at himself, rather excited, though the future was elusive, if it were evaluated by the Time Immortal who controlled time, then that future seemed quite credible.

"Of course, Lu Yang, my young friend, you are indeed the strongest in the future," the Time Immortal affirmed, now ready to dispute with anyone who denied Lu Yang’s supremacy.

"You possess the Initial Form of Immortal Dao Fruit, and possess an Immortal’s Body; thus, you are no longer merely at the Divinity Transformation Stage, but have created a completely new realm—Immortal Transformation Stage!"

"Creating something out of nothing, crafting realms, these are acts only the ancient sages could achieve!"

Lu Yang gasped, was he really that strong?

Eldest Senior Sister was very curious about the experiences of the Time Immortal over the past three hundred thousand years, so the Time Immortal had no choice but to recount once again how he had jumped through time over the years.

"The techniques of Elder Time Immortal are truly wonderful."

In case of another unforeseen event at Western Paradise Temple, this Sky Opening Axe could still mask his presence.

"Lu Yang sure did a thorough job blowing it up; I wonder when Western Paradise Temple will be repaired."

"Won’t the Heavenly Venerate return again?" During the quiet of deep night, Xin Ding tossed and turned on his bed, his mind full of the day’s battle.

During the chaos of the battle, no one noticed that the Green Peak Sword had flown out from behind him.

After that battle, Heavenly Venerate disappeared and never showed up again.

Suddenly, his tent lit up with specks of golden light, which converged to form a golden silhouette.

"Little monk, still not asleep at this hour?"

"Heavenly Venerate!"

Tofu Heavenly Venerable stood with his hands behind his back, gazing at the sky, his eyes filled with the vicissitudes of life, "Ultimately, Western Paradise Temple turned into ruins because of my emergence, but through this battle, my causality is dissolved, and I no longer have a reason to stay."

"Heavenly Venerate, may I go with you?" Xin Ding looked at Tofu Heavenly Venerate reluctantly. Although they had been together for only a few months, Xin Ding had already come to regard Tofu Heavenly Venerable as his master.

Tofu Heavenly Venerable shook his head: "Little monk, you are naturally attuned to Buddhism. If you were to follow my Taoist sect, it would only hold you back. Staying at Western Paradise Temple is the best choice for you."

"If you diligently cultivate, there may yet be a time when you see me again."

With that, Tofu Heavenly Venerable turned again into specks of golden light and disappeared.

Lu Yang arrived at the gates of Western Heaven City and met up with Eldest Senior Sister and Second Senior Brother.

"All set?"

"All set, let’s head back."

Ye Zijin curiously circled around Lu Yang, "Junior Brother, have you really become an immortal?"

He still hadn’t figured out how his junior brother had changed like this.

"Only in the Buddha Country, and even then, it’s not truly becoming an immortal," Lu Yang said modestly.

When Lu Yang left Buddha Country, he left both the Immortal’s Body and the Eternity Dao Fruit Outline behind. If he returned to Buddha Country, he could become an immortal again at any time.

Although somewhat reluctant, he could not stay in Buddha Country forever.

"Back to the sect!"

Lu Yang spoke with his chest puffed out and his head held high, displaying great vigor. This trip to Buddha Country had been fertile; he had found the Sky Opening Axe and Time Immortal, gained the Immortal’s Body, and captured Si Chen God Lord. It was not an exaggeration to call him a great hero who had saved Buddha Country.

Then Lu Yang stealthily crossed the border and returned to Great Xia.

He had been taken out of Great Xia by the Nian Beast, with no exit records.

Lu Yang returned to the familiar Seek Dao Sect and relaxed.

Though Buddha Country was delightful, Seek Dao Sect felt more comfortable.

"Eldest Senior Sister, see you in a bit!" Lu Yang briefly turned around for a farewell and headed straight for the Task Hall.

With such significant events happening in Buddha Country, including capturing Si Chen God Lord, how many contribution points could he gain?

In the room, Dai Bufan held some intelligence and rubbed his chin thoughtfully, hearing the familiar knock at the door.

"Elder Brother Dai, are you in?"

"It’s Junior Brother Lu, come in."

Lu Yang entered, beaming with a spring-like demeanor, in stark contrast to the thoughtful Dai Bufan.

"I do."

"You really know?" Dai Bufan was surprised; he had asked without much hope, but Junior Brother actually had an answer?

"Who is it?"

Proudly pointing at himself, Lu Yang said, "It’s me."

"Huh?" Dai Bufan was full of question marks, failing to understand the meaning of Lu Yang’s statement, or rather, with his comprehension, he could not grasp what Lu Yang meant.

Seeing Elder Brother Dai’s disbelief, Lu Yang produced a Recording Orb, showing the first-person perspective of his battle with Si Chen God Lord.

With a broad smile, Lu Yang shared the joyful news with his respected Elder Brother Dai:

"Elder Brother Dai, I’ve become an immortal."

Dai Bufan had a lengthy dream, where he envisioned his birth accompanied by unusual celestial phenomena, marking him as a prodigy. After joining the Seek Dao Sect, which was filled with talents, he, except for Yun Zhi, was still able to dominate his peers and sweep through all challenges.

He was measured in his actions and deeply cherished by his junior brothers and sisters. After entering the Body Integration Realm, he took charge of various affairs in the Task Hall, earning the heartfelt admiration from all sides...

"Elder Brother Dai, Elder Brother Dai, wake up!"

Lu Yang shook Elder Brother Dai, who was lying on the ground, and pinched him forcefully on the philtrum. Elder Brother Dai immediately sat up stiffly, his eyes clouded and memory jumbled.

Had he just experienced a life flashing before his eyes?

"Elder Brother Dai, you finally woke up; you scared me to death just now," Lu Yang wiped his sweat, affirming the old saying that both great joy and great sorrow are harmful to the body; the ancients truly did not deceive me.

"What happened to me just now?"

Lu Yang looked at Elder Brother Dai, his eyes bright and sincere, "Just now I said I had become an Immortal, and you, Elder Brother Dai, stood up happily, but you staggered and fainted."

"You became an Immortal?" Elder Brother Dai thought for a moment, then immediately pulled out a crimson Auspicious Cloud Banner from his storage ring, making a gesture to smash it towards Lu Yang.

"You’re only at the Mid-stage of Transforming Spirit now, you dare to fool even me?"

Lu Yang hurriedly covered his head, "Ay, ay, ay, don’t hit, don’t hit, I’m telling the truth."

"I even have a witness."

"A witness?"

Lu Yang touched his forehead lightly, and a comatose Soul Body floated out.

"This person is the Si Chen God Lord of Great Qian."

After experiencing several self-detonations, Si Chen God Lord had luckily survived but had not woken up ever since.

Seeing the half-dead witness, Elder Brother Dai withdrew the Auspicious Cloud Banner, smilingly brought Lu Yang to the main seat, and began to massage his shoulders.

Lu Yang tried to get up several times but was firmly pressed down by Elder Brother Dai.

Elder Brother Dai leaned in close and whispered in Lu Yang’s ear, making Lu Yang shiver involuntarily, "Immortal Lu, what exactly is going on? What have you been doing in the Buddha Country?"

"Oh, nothing much, just that I’ve done many good deeds as usual, which are considered great merits to the Buddha Country. The Power of Incense and Fire from the Buddha Country just kept rushing towards me non-stop. I couldn’t even refuse it or block it, so I used the Power of Incense and Fire to condense an Immortal Body."

"However, this Immortal Body was temporarily condensed and can’t leave the Buddha Country. Once I returned to our Great Xia, my realm reverted back to normal."

Lu Yang grinned and gave Elder Brother Dai a thumbs-up, "They don’t say Elder Brother Dai is the backbone of Seek Dao Sect for nothing; accurate to a tee."

Elder Brother Dai took Lu Yang’s banter as mere jest, and waved him off impatiently, his mind relieved from not seeing and worrying, "Go, go, go, if you refuse to explain, just leave it be. Quickly send Si Chen God Lord to Captive Peak."

"Alright."

Lu Yang briskly left the Task Hall, making his way familiarly into Captive Peak.

The inmates in Captive Peak who had been chatting, quieted down immediately upon seeing Lu Yang. They hastily bowed their heads, not daring to meet Lu Yang’s gaze, afraid of making eye contact.

Lu Yang moved Si Chen God Lord out from the Spiritual Space, not worried about Si Chen God Lord waking up and causing trouble with the initial form of Time Dao Fruit, as the Time Immortal had already used the Time Dao Fruit to lock down the capabilities of Si Chen God Lord’s Dao Fruit Outline.

Now, Si Chen God Lord seemed no different from one who was at the Transcendence Tribulation Stage.

In the Mysterious Land, a silhouette sat on a throne built of dry bones, pondering the freshly received intelligence, eyes gradually brightening; the hidden affairs behind this intelligence were no small matter.

The breathtakingly beautiful female immortal carried her basket of vegetables down the bustling street; oddly enough, bystanders looked the other way, as if they couldn’t see the stunning immortal at all.

"This is bad, Qinghe..."

With that thought, Ashy Bean no longer mimicked the life of mortals, twisted space, and instantly arrived at the small and unpopular restaurant.

Ashy Bean carried her basket of vegetables into the kitchen and, seeing that Qinghe was still flipping through the recipe book, breathed a sigh of relief.

Seeing Ashy Bean hurry back in a rush, Qinghe closed the recipe book and with a calm and collected voice, said the words Ashy Bean least wanted to hear.

Qinghe looked directly into Ashy Bean’s bright and angry immortal eyes and said, word by word, "I, must, go!"

Eldest Senior Sister looked helplessly at her good sister and good Junior Brother, "Which one of you conjured up such a huge piece of clothing that it’s covering half of Sky Gate Mountain?"

She was peaceably sitting on the Emperor’s Chair drinking tea when suddenly it darkened, leading her to think someone had invaded.

Lu Yang: "..."

Yun Mengmeng looked up to Second-in-command with admiration, "I get it now, if the sleeve becomes bigger it can hold everything, so this is the true Universe within the Sleeve!"

...

"Old Meng, can you show me your Dharma Aspect?"

"For what?"

Meng Jingzhou looked puzzled at Lu Yang, especially baffled, yet still he displayed the Supreme Pure Yang Dharma Image, immense and awe-inspiring, simply standing there was enough to deter any petty criminals.

"Does your Dharma Aspect lack clothing?"

Meng Jingzhou saw Lu Yang taking out a set of huge clothes, full of question marks.

"Where on earth did you get this set of clothes from, kid?"

"Cough cough, this is the Supreme Treasure Clothing that I’ve diligently cultivated for many days, exhausting countless efforts to refine. Your Dharma Aspect looks indecent, bare-assed, so I specially refined it for your Dharma Aspect to wear."

Actually, it was because Lu Yang found out that the result of ’Universe within the Sleeve’ made the clothes grow bigger, so he kept practicing magic skills to revert the clothes, aiming to master the true ’Universe within the Sleeve’.

However, he didn’t master the true ’Universe within the Sleeve’, and in the end, he found that his clothes, which had grown repeatedly bigger, could no longer shrink back.

Having such a large piece of clothing was of no use to Lu Yang, so he might as well offer a bargain to his good brother.

Meng Jingzhou rolled his eyes, "I’d have to see a ghost to believe your nonsense."

But wearing the clothes wouldn’t hurt.

Meng Jingzhou had the Dharma Aspect wear the clothes, and truth be told, it fit quite well.

Originally imposing, wielding a shield in one hand and a spear in the other, the Dharma Aspect, upon wearing the clothes, gained a refined scholarly air, like a well-read scholar heading into battle.

The Supreme Pure Yang Dharma Image surged with terrifying Pure Yang Light Flame on its body, a single strand of which could burn a host of little demons to death, its power terrifying. Ordinary clothes that touched the Dharma Aspect would turn to ash in an instant.

But how could the clothes worn by Lu Yang be ordinary? These garments were impervious to knife and fire, water and flame, unafraid of the Pure Yang Light Flame.

Turns out this was a free gift from Lu Yang, and he was at a loss.

"Not bad," Meng Jingzhou was very satisfied with the current appearance of the Dharma Aspect, much more refined. His previous Dharma Aspect looked like a butcher, which didn’t suit the identity of Young Master Meng at all.

On the way back, the more Lu Yang thought about it, the more something felt off. He had spent so much time learning ’Universe within the Sleeve’, but ended up gaining nothing, instead letting Old Meng benefit.

"Should I also make myself bigger? Fairy, do you know how to enlarge one’s body?"

Recalling his encounters with High-Level Cultivators in battle, they usually moved mountains and seas, and fought by enlarging themselves. Learning how to enlarge his own body would be useful for future battles.

"Then learn ’Law of Heaven and Earth’."

’Law of Heaven and Earth’, a Divine Ability even more renowned than ’Universe within the Sleeve’. Not many Integration Period Cultivators could learn it. Lu Yang, only at the Spirit Transformation Late Stage, was even less likely to learn it, but considering Lu Yang’s exceptional talent, the Immortal Fairy thought it wouldn’t hurt to try.

Anyway, if he practiced it incorrectly, it had nothing to do with her.

"Then let’s learn this!"

Lu Yang returned to the place where he had previously learned ’Universe within the Sleeve’, with the Immortal Fairy personally instructing him.

"’Law of Heaven and Earth,’ as the name suggests, is about imitating the power of ’Heaven’ and ’Earth’, achieving a state of integration with the natural laws of heaven and earth, thereby making the body immensely gigantic, grand like heaven and earth!"

"You need to form the Heaven-Earth seal in your heart, the hand gesture is like this..."

"Little Yang, calm your mind, feel the heaven and the earth."

The reason ’Law of Heaven and Earth’ is difficult to learn is crucially because there are no shortcuts; it relies solely on enlightenment.

Great Cultivators who mastered ’Law of Heaven and Earth’ usually specially refine a huge set of clothes to wear after enlarging. Lu Yang had no such concerns.

Night fell, cold silvery rays scattered over the lawn, reflecting a peaceful and tranquil scene.

Lu Yang sat cross-legged on the ground, assuming the Five Centers Toward Heaven position, took a deep breath, and exhaled slowly, as if at that moment, all distractions were excluded, leaving only a dialogue with heaven and earth.

A breeze passed by, mixed with Spiritual Energy, bringing a fresh scent from distant mountains and forests, as if the Spiritual Energy was responding to his call.

Lu Yang also felt the pulse of the earth, as if synchronizing with his own heartbeat, solid and powerful, containing endless strength.

Three days went by in a blink, Lu Yang neither ate nor drank nor slept, completely merging with heaven and earth.

Noon sunlight streamed through the clouds onto Lu Yang’s cheeks; he opened his eyes and stood up, completely rejuvenated, the blend with heaven and earth was an unprecedented experience that left him deeply moved.

Lu Yang pointed at the sky, trying to imitate the Worldly Venerable’s posture of ’above all under heaven, I alone am honored’.

"Law of Heaven and Earth!"

Lu Yang disappeared, leaving only his clothes on the ground.

He felt like a Heavenly God high above, looking down on all creatures, who seemed like mere ants in his eyes.

"Is this what becoming a giant feels like? Indeed, it’s a completely different sensation."

Immortal Fairy flew up to the sky to find Lu Yang.

"Fairy, I succeeded!" Lu Yang said excitedly, "It wasn’t easy, after studying magic for so long, I’ve finally gotten it right once."

Immortal Fairy scratched her head, unsure how to describe Little Yang’s condition.

Immortal Fairy conjured a mirror with a spell, Lu Yang looked into the mirror, but could not see himself.

Immortal Fairy finally knew how to describe Little Yang’s condition, "Second-in-command, you seem to have turned into spiritual energy."

"!"

A cluster of spiritual energy was floating in the sky, and it was Lu Yang who had transformed.

Frightened, Lu Yang hastily dispelled the magic skill, reverted to his naked human form, and quickly flew back to get dressed.

"I was scared to death, I thought I was going to die," Lu Yang broke out in cold sweat, as if he had just taken a walk past the gates of hell.

For a cultivator to turn into spiritual energy, that’s called transforming the path and it happens only after one dies.

"It must have been a mistake in the steps of the magic skill I used just now. I’ll try it again."

Cultivating magic skills is never absolutely safe, but as a cultivator, as a seeker of the path, Lu Yang would not let this minor incident stop him.

"Law of Heaven and Earth!"

Unlike the last time, Lu Yang felt as if he had merged with the earth, which was very reassuring.

Immortal Fairy watched from the side, she saw Little Yang disappear and in his place, a heap of soil appeared.

"So, was it Law of Heaven just now, and now it’s Earth?"

Immortal Fairy hissed, Little Yang really imitated heaven and earth thoroughly.

Upon learning the truth, Lu Yang tried several times, only to find that he either turned into the sky or the earth, but never back into a human.

Lu Yang lay on the ground, spread-eagled, staring blankly at the sky, wondering if becoming a giant was really that difficult.

Just as Immortal Fairy was about to step forward and comfort Lu Yang, he suddenly sat up.

"Hey, I’ve got an idea for a solution!"

Lu Yang went ahead and executed the Law of Heaven and Earth, transforming into a cluster of spiritual energy just like before. freёweɓnovel.com

Then, using the Taotie Clan’s innate divine ability "Devour the Sky and Swallow the Earth," Lu Yang crazily absorbed spiritual energy, expanding his own size.

"Release!"

Lu Yang dispelled the magic, reverting to his human shape; this time, he had transformed into a giant!

"Haha, I knew this would work!"

Thrilled, Lu Yang jumped up. His idea was right, using Devour the Sky and Swallow the Earth to absorb spiritual energy would transform him, consuming soil when he became soil, till transforming back into a giant human form!

Atop Sky Gate Mountain, a naked giant hopped around, completely unbothered by his condition.

"Old Meng, show your Dharma Aspect, let’s have a one-on-one duel."

"Devour the Sky and Swallow the Earth!"

Lu Yang frenziedly devoured the soil at the entrance to Meng Jingzhou’s abode.

Lu Yang dispelled the Law of Heaven and Earth.

"Universe within the Sleeve!"

Lu Yang made his clothes grow larger.

"Why are there so many steps for you to get big?"

"It’s just you who talks too much!"

Lu Yang, enraged, thought what was wrong with having more steps, even additional steps were part of the Law of Heaven and Earth!

After he transformed into a several-hundred-foot-tall giant, his voice also changed, booming like thunder, echoing in the mountain ravine.

Lu Yang drew out the Green Peak Sword, an Immortal Sword, which could change size along with Lu Yang.

Meng Jingzhou didn’t hesitate either, his Dharma Aspect’s shields and spears collided, creating ripples through space, while the Green Peak Sword emitted a sharp, resonating hum.

The two starkly different sounds collided in the middle of the battlefield, causing a massive explosion, shaking the entire space!

The Dharma Aspect’s eyes shot out foot-thick beams of red light, akin to magma; even before approaching Lu Yang, he could feel the raging power within the beams.

"Open!"

With a swing of the Green Peak Sword, he split the red beams in two, which skimmed past on either side of him, instantly reducing the white sandalwood forest next to Meng Jingzhou’s abode to ashes, carving two deep trenches in the ground that glowed with molten glass.

The Dharma Aspect strode forward, each step leaving a ball of flame on the ground. With a forceful stomp, the earth cracked, and its massive form leaped into the air.

With the sky above its head and the earth beneath its feet, the Pure Yang Flames swept across the sky, staining it crimson as if the heavens were bleeding.

The spear tore through the sky, carrying a torrent of fire as it collided with the Green Peak Sword, the sound of metal clashing like sudden thunder, followed by another shield whistling towards Lu Yang’s ribs.

Lu Yang flicked his left hand, and the pitch-black Inheriting Shadow Sword appeared, blocking the fierce blow.

With a flick of his wrist, he sent out a barrage of sword shadows, each strong enough to level mountains, forcing Meng Jingzhou to pay close attention.

Meng Jingzhou’s method of using the shield and spear was no longer chaotic as before; it had become rhythmic.

The Cease War Skill was a combat technique created for Meng Jingzhou by Meng Junzi.

Meng Junzi emerged as a renowned fighter at the end of the Great Yu Late Period, with countless battles both large and small, his combat experience immensely rich. He developed the Cease War Skill for Meng Jingzhou’s Dharma Aspect, a technique to stop fighting with fighting, to cease bloodshed with bloodshed!

A raging storm of spiritual essence swept through, and the actions of the two giants at the center of the battlefield could reshape the terrain. The entrance to Meng Jingzhou’s abode had been disfigured beyond recognition; no one coming here would be able to tell it was Meng Jingzhou’s abode!

Countless blades suddenly sprouted beneath Lu Yang’s feet, sticking out from the ground haphazardly like small hills, restricting Meng Jingzhou’s movements.

"Big Sun Magma Arrow!"

The massive form of the Dharma Aspect oozed boiling magma that bubbled, steamed the land, scorched the space, and was so hot in temperature that cultivators of the same level dare not refine such heated spiritual essence for fear of burning their meridians.

This magma hovered in the air, spinning, transforming into a barrage of arrows, shooting out violently!

Blades gathered in front of Lu Yang, forming a shield that sliced through the molten arrow feathers as they made contact, shattering them with the released Sword Qi.

Meng Jingzhou seized the opportunity to charge with his shield raised; the two shields collided and both were shattered by the impact.

The Dharma Aspect leaned in, pushing past Lu Yang’s guards; the two were so close that Lu Yang was forced to abandon using his sword and engage in a physical duel.

Lu Yang’s punch landed on Meng Jingzhou’s Dharma Aspect, finding it much harder than his own flesh and unable to break its defense. When the Dharma Aspect hit Lu Yang, it caused him acute pain.

Lu Yang used Law of Heaven and Earth to simply enlarge his body, whereas Meng Jingzhou’s Dharma Aspect was based on his own flesh, further enhanced. Meng Jingzhou’s physical body was already slightly stronger than Lu Yang’s, and now, augmented by the Dharma Aspect, this led to Lu Yang being at a disadvantage when it came purely to strength and defense.

"How about that, Old Lu? You’re better than me with weapons, but in close combat, you’re no match for me," Meng Jingzhou laughed heartily, knowing that Old Lu had yet to use the devious Extinguishing Immortal Sword Array, signifying that Lu Yang was testing for flaws in the Law of Heaven and Earth.

The flaw had been exposed, and it was time to finish this!

"Earth-Shaking Eight Styles!"

The Dharma Aspect exhibited the Earth-Shaking Eight Styles that could be described as capable of destroying heaven and earth, causing Lu Yang to retreat step by step. Even if Lu Yang could block it, his physical strength was insufficient, so blocking was futile.

A sixteen-foot golden body suddenly materialized, bringing a sudden silence to the fierce battle between the two.

Lu Yang’s eye twitched. He had transformed to several hundred feet tall using the Law of Heaven and Earth, and the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body was not even the size of his palm, making its high defensive power seemingly useless.

"I’ve got an idea!" A flash of brilliance struck Lu Yang.

"Sixteen-Foot Golden Body, Sixteen-Foot Golden Body, Sixteen-Foot Golden Body..."

In one go, Lu Yang created a multitude of Sixteen-Foot Golden Bodies, sticking them onto his body as armor, covering him from head to toe, securely guarded.

Lu Yang had grown large by swallowing the earth and Spiritual Energy. The enormous size of his Spiritual Energy Pool had increased several times over, allowing him to repeatedly cast the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body.

"How’s that?" Lu Yang flaunted his suit of armor. This time, his defense was definitely strong enough.

Meng Jingzhou’s eye twitched. Old Lu was covered in little figures, looking stranger by the minute. Even he felt it was excessively weird, to the point where calling Old Lu a giant figure of the Demon Path wouldn’t seem out of place.

"Earth-Shaking Eight Styles!"

Despite the ridiculous appearance, the defense was genuinely solid. As Meng Jingzhou struck Lu Yang with the Earth-Shaking Eight Styles, the Sixteen-Foot Golden Bodies absorbed most of the force, and Lu Yang himself was unharmed.

"Hiss, it really does seem to work." Meng Jingzhou hadn’t expected the defense provided by the Sixteen-Foot Golden Bodies used as armor to be so strong; it was almost outrageous.

"With this, the Law of Heaven and Earth is now the complete version," Lu Yang he-he’d with a smile, finding that testing out techniques with Old Meng was indeed a way to identify and address shortcomings.

"My White Sandalwood Forest! What are you two brats doing, is this a place for you to duel?"

The Third Elder noticed the commotion and flew into a rage. The power of the two young cultivators’ clash was comparable to a Body Integration Realm duel, leaving the land and forest completely devastated!

The ground, scorched by intense heat, had even turned into glass, not to mention the trees, which had long become charcoal ash.

Our Sect has so many open spaces, and you two just had to duel here, didn’t you?

Especially this forest; it was his favorite White Sandalwood Forest, which he had carefully tended for many years, and now it was all destroyed in a blaze!

True, this was Meng Jingzhou’s Abode, but this mountain also belonged to the Third Elder.

In his furious state, the Third Elder didn’t hold back and sent one punch each their way, hammering giant Lu Yang and the Dharma Aspect Meng Jingzhou into the ground, leaving only their heads exposed.

The Third Elder glared menacingly at Meng Jingzhou: "I need to teach you a lesson, or are you trying to rebel against the heavens? You go do volunteer work at the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect for two months before coming back!"

The Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect in Great Xia was specifically responsible for dealing with the aftermath of cultivators’ duels and restoring the landscape.

Meng Jingzhou nodded repeatedly.

Lu Yang was a disciple of Daoist Buyu, so the Third Elder couldn’t do much about him.

After the Third Elder left, the two crawled out of the dirt, looking disheveled and dusty.

"It’s all your fault for coming over and challenging me for no reason."

"It’s not such a big deal, it’s just two months of learning at the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect. I’ll go with you."

Lu Yang’s conscience was not yet lost. He knew that Old Meng was punished because he had proposed a duel, and that he bore some responsibility for the destruction of the White Sandalwood Forest.

Therefore, he actively offered to also go to the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect to perform two months of voluntary labor.

"That sounds more like it."

Before going to the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect, the two had to first restore the ruins at the entrance of Meng Jingzhou’s abode back to their original state.

From afar, the area around Body Refining Peak looked like it had been chewed up by a dog, completely bare, and indeed quite an eyesore.

Lu Yang had never thought about using Tang Chuanwu’s ability to reverse time. He had asked Tang Chuanwu to reverse time during the murder case in order to save people and catch the murderer.

This time was different. Lu Yang certainly couldn’t ask Tang Chuanwu to sacrifice himself just because he had made a mistake. Even if Tang Chuanwu could be revived, dying once was not a pleasant experience.

Lu Yang had realized early on that if he resorted to asking Tang Chuanwu to sacrifice himself whenever he faced an issue, he would easily become indifferent to Tang Chuanwu’s life, treating him as nothing more than a tool.

The two of them got to work together. After shaving off several layers of the ground, they finally cleared away all of the scorched earth and glass. Then they shoveled some soil from the sect’s grasslands, filling in the large pits.

"What about the White Sandalwood Forest, do we use the Tree Planting Spell?"

Lu Yang was also somewhat troubled. After pondering for a moment, he suggested, "Since the White Sandalwood Forest was cultivated by the Third Elder, if you simply use the Tree Planting Spell to restore it, that would effectively erase all traces of the Third Elder’s efforts. It would be best for us to plant White Sandalwood tree seeds and let the forest grow naturally."

"That’s true."

The two bought a large bag of White Sandalwood tree seeds from the Task Hall. Lu Yang used his sword to dig holes, and Meng Jingzhou dug with his hands. Huffing and puffing, they finally finished the job.

I have to say, doing this does bring a sense of accomplishment.

"We’ve finally arrived at the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect." Lu Yang stretched out mightily. This journey had been exhausting, but fortunately, it had been safe and without any alarming incidents.

Initially, he and Old Meng thought it made sense for them, as cultivators in the Spirit Transformation Late Stage, not to need a flying boat—they could simply fly directly to the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect.

Then, on their way, they happened upon a Secret Realm that only opened once a century. The Secret Realm specified that only Divine Transformation Stage Cultivators could enter. Going with the thought that since they had already come this far, they entered and consecutively passed through three trials. Finally, at the end of the third trial, they encountered the Secret Realm Spirit.

Dissatisfied with their method of passing the trials, it battled with them for hundreds of rounds. After realizing it couldn’t defeat the two, it resorted to telling them the origin of the Secret Realm to distract them and used its authority over the Secret Realm to expel them, forbidding them from ever entering this Secret Realm again.

After being randomly transported out by the Secret Realm Spirit, they found themselves in the forbidden area of a hermit family, who had settled there for generations to suppress an Evil Demon. To maintain the seal, the hermit family had been sacrificing young men and women every hundred years for over a hundred thousand years to extend the life of the Array Method with their blood.

The Evil Demon was the malevolent spirit of a Transcendance Tribulation Stage being from long ago. The hermit family were descendants of this Transcendance Tribulation Stage individual.

After Lu Yang and his companion saved the young men and women who were about to be sacrificed, and after battling the Evil Demon for hundreds of rounds, they decided to report it to the government office, allowing the Governor of Youzhou to send people to deal with it.

In Chunjiang City, after dealing with the Void Venerate and the Nightmare Supreme, Lu Yang had given the Fu Ling sisters a small wooden sword for protection. Now, they had encountered troublemakers and had been forced to use the small wooden sword to fend off the aggressors.

They claimed that the sword was a gift from Lu Yang, but the evildoers, while afraid of Lu Yang’s reputation, were somewhat skeptical of the sword’s origin. The Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect is nestled deep within the mountains, beside a river, surrounded by a beautiful environment... that is, if the mountains stay still.

The existence of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect is quite special; as a sect under the rule of the Dynasty, it doesn’t have a hierarchical classification.

They are mainly responsible for the aftermath of cultivator battles, restoring maps, organizing mountain ranges, planting trees, and so forth. Therefore, to join this sect, one must at least have Earth Attribute or Wood Attribute in their Spirit Root.

From outside the sect, the two saw mountains moving to and fro, which was the sect disciples practicing the Mountain Shifting Skill.

"Did you also destroy the landscape in battle and seek our help to restore it?"

That’s why everyone comes to their sect.

The sect leader of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect was named Kong Liansheng, a middle-aged man with a long beard and a scholarly demeanor.

Sect Master Kong sat in a grandmaster’s chair, with the introduction letter placed to the side.

"We greet Sect Master Kong."

Sect Master Kong stood up, stroking his beard and smiling warmly as he looked at the two, his eyes full of appreciation.
