Meng Jingzhou owned up to their mistake honestly, "In a fight between us, we accidentally destroyed his White Sandalwood Forest."

Upon hearing this, Sect Master Kong laughed heartily, "So, it was the destruction of the White Sandalwood Forest that got you sent here. Everyone has their youthful impetuosity, understandable, understandable."

Sect Master Kong seemed to recall something and waved the introductory letter, "Speaking of which, the letter mentioned you should have arrived in early July. Why did it take until mid-August for you to get here?"

"We were delayed by some minor issues on the way."

Although Sect Master Kong wanted to know what the "few small matters" mentioned by the two were, he was not a cultivator with a heavy sense of curiosity, and he did not inquire further.

"So are you two planning to stay in our sect for two months, and after two months, I just send a letter back with Third Zhang saying you two have been doing quite well here, or do you want to do something else?"

Sect Master Kong wanted to know the real thoughts of Lu Yang and his companion. They were not the first batch of disciples sent to their sect. Besides the Seek Dao Sect, the other Four Great Immortal Sects, as well as Super-grade and First-Grade sects, all had a custom of sending disciples who had made mistakes to undertake obligatory labor here.

Among them, some disciples accepted their punishment willingly, while others worked reluctantly. For the latter, Sect Master Kong found it troublesome to make arrangements and simply let them stay at the sect until their time was up and then return on their own.

Meng Jingzhou bowed respectfully and said earnestly, "Since we have made mistakes, we should be punished, and this is also a rare experience. My brother and I are willing to make some contributions to the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect."

"Not bad," Sect Master Kong nodded, appreciating that the two not only had extraordinary cultivation talents but also demonstrated commendable character. They were indeed rare good seeds.

At such a young age, they had already cultivated to the Spirit Transformation Late Stage, unmatched in the world.

"How much do you two know about our sect?"

At this point, Lu Yang and his companion exchanged glances, their eyes revealing some embarrassment—they knew very little about the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect.

Seeing their expressions, Sect Master Kong understood what they were thinking and smiled, easing the awkward atmosphere: "Very few cultivators know about our sect, so it’s normal not to be familiar with it."

"Despite our sect’s lack of fame, it’s actually very useful for cultivators. Let me tell you a few things, and then you’ll understand the importance of our sect."

"During the celebration in Qingzhou, it was unfortunately disrupted by the Heavenly Calamity Sovereign, and several mountains were flattened or even vanished during the battle. It took our sect a great deal of effort to restore those mountains to their original forms."

"When the sixth Emperor Yu, Wu Youdao, attacked Hanshui City in the Wild State and faced Heavenly Venerate Dou from the Ancient Heavenly Court, he was defeated and retreated. Some houses in Hanshui City were damaged, and the area outside the city was destroyed beyond recognition. Today, Hanshui City has been restored to its original state, which is the result of our sect’s hard work."

"There’s also Chunjiang City, which was pulled into the Void Realm by the Void Venerate. Although the city itself was unharmed, the citizens who witnessed the battle between the Semi-Immortals were terrified, and it was our sect that provided psychological counseling to comfort them."

"Take the Immortal Battle in the Imperial City as another example. When Meng Junzi fought the Great Yu National Preceptor, many landmark buildings in the Imperial City were reduced to ruins, riddled with scars. It was still our sect that acted to give the Imperial City a new lease of life, restoring it to its original condition."

"Then there’s the Western Paradise Temple that was destroyed by an avatar of the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord and still has not been restored. If our sect took on the task, the temple would have been fixed long ago."

Sect Master Kong listed the major events that the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect had handled over the years, with a tone inevitably filled with some pride.

As Lu Yang and his companion listened to the introduction, they nodded and gained a new understanding of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect. They were eyewitnesses to these great battles and knew how difficult it was to deal with the aftermath. The sect truly had its own unique strengths.

In the midst of their conversation, a young man walked in and, seeing Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, showed a slightly surprised expression but did not say much. Instead, he focused on the matter at hand: "Master, a task commission has arrived."

"What’s the content?"

"It’s a duel arranged by two Divine Transformation Late Stage cultivators in three days at the Qingniu Mountain Range. They hope that our sect will restore the appearance of the Qingniu Mountains after the battle is over."

The Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect, in addition to fulfilling tasks assigned by the dynasty, also took responsibility for the cleanup after battles between ordinary cultivators.

The latter was divided into two scenarios: either the sect would be commissioned after the battle, or it would be commissioned before the battle. The fee for the second scenario was lower than the first.

After all, the first scenario required the sect to find the pre-battle state through other channels, while in the second, they could survey the area in advance, saving a lot of trouble.

"In three days, then," Sect Master Kong looked at Lu Yang and his companion. "That would be a good opportunity to familiarize you two with our sect’s workflow."

"Master, are these two Fellow Daoist Lu Yang and Fellow Daoist Meng Jingzhou?" the young man asked.

Nowadays, besides those cultivators who are in constant seclusion, there’s no one under heaven who doesn’t recognize Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

"Right, I haven’t introduced you two to each other yet."

"This is my eldest disciple Fang Jin, who has just entered the Body Integration Realm and has already mastered the Law of Heaven and Earth."

Sect Master Kong stroked his beard with a smile, very satisfied with his big disciple. It was important to know that a divine ability like the Law of Heaven and Earth couldn’t be learned by ninety percent of cultivators in the late Body Integration stage, yet Fang Jin had mastered it in the early stage of Body Integration, which spoke volumes about his talent.

In the future, there would be no objections to him taking over the position of Sect Leader.

"Greetings to Elder Brother Fang Jin."

"Junior Brother Lu, Junior Brother Meng, I’ve heard about you from Elder Brother Dai. He always praises you for your upright character, courage, and righteousness, and for punishing the evil and promoting the good. He often thinks of handing over the position of Task Hall Master to you both right now!"

Lu Yang’s eyes twitched. Was Elder Brother Dai praising them? It didn’t quite feel like it.

"Fang Jin, take these two around our sect. They will be staying with us and helping out for the next two months."

"Yes."

The Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect was vast, encompassing various terrains. It was a land specially designated by the dynasty to facilitate the disciples’ practice of the art of mountain moving and sea filling. The sect also featured a variety of architectural styles, and repairing these structures was likewise one of their tasks.

Walking through the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect felt like travelling across all of Great Xia, witnessing all sorts of cultures and customs.

Three days later, to show his importance, Sect Master Kong personally led a team, including Lu Yang and the others, to the Qingniu Mountain Range.

Along the way, all the disciples were curiously whispering about Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou standing to the left and right of Sect Master Kong. They couldn’t believe they were witnessing these two legendary figures in person.

What was even more significant was that these two would be staying in the sect for two months, so in the future, they could proudly tell their peers that they had met Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Once the group arrived at the Qingniu Mountain Range and the two Divine Transformation Stage cultivators had yet to arrive, everyone followed the predetermined arrangements, dividing the tasks and cooperating in an organized manner, and started their investigation, taking out Recording Orbs to map the scene.

"With the Qiongqi Clan’s Recording Orbs, this job is so much easier."

"Yeah, it’s said that the Recording Orb comes from an ancestor of the Qiongqi Clan, quite remarkable indeed."

The disciples of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect couldn’t stop praising the Recording Orb; mapping the scene used to be a very arduous task.

Fairy Immortality looked at the bustling scene with some emotion, "You all are drawing maps based on the scene now, aren’t you? Back in our day, we used to alter the landscape according to the map."

"...Altering the landscape according to the map?" Lu Yang found this concept strange.

"Back then, the Yingtian Immortal said he felt the terrain wasn’t rugged and imposing enough for them. The five of us became immortals, and with countless Semi-Immortals and Transcendance Tribulation cultivators, it was surely a vibrant era to come."

"But the current terrain didn’t match their Cultivation Levels. The mountains were too low, the seas too shallow, the trees too short."

"The Time Immortal and the other two agreed with the Yingtian Immortal’s view. The four of them devised a brand new map and, according to it, moved various races to habitable areas and then used swords and axes to change the landscape."

"Fairy, what you mean is ’radical reform.’"

"Oh, and then they used great swords and broad axes to change the terrain, creating mountains that reached into the universe and oceans that delved deep into the earth’s heart."

"They even moved several veins of top-grade spirit stones to a planet, claiming that it could give birth to life forms composed of top-grade spirit stones."

"The Twenty-Eight Constellations, the Beidou Seven Stars, were also shaped by the Yingtian Immortal and the others moving the stars into formation."

Originally, Lu Yang felt the starry sky was vast and the universe mysterious, and he lamented that cultivators of the box world could not use the power of the stars.

Now, after listening to Fairy Eternity’s description, he suddenly felt that the Beidou Seven Stars were nothing special.

"Are the Yingtian Immortals just idling?" Lu Yang couldn’t help but speak his mind, "If you four really have nothing better to do, why not ponder on how to ascend to transcendence?"

"Not at all, they are very busy. Every day, if they aren’t giving lectures, they are altering the landscape. I’ve invited them to my home for dinner, and they never come, unlike Little Ling Lianyi and her company, who are quiet and always make time to attend,"

Lu Yang felt it was understandable that Ying Tian and his fellows were busy.

"Once the landscape is all set up, cultivators in duels will be extremely cautious, fearing they might ruin the hard work of the four Yingtian Immortals."

In reality, Sect Master Kong, looking over his bustling disciples shaping mountains and rivers, couldn’t help but remark emotionally.

"Little Lu, Little Meng, look at this mountain range, how beautiful it is. This mountain resembles a bull’s head, here is the body, and that one resembles its tail, hence it’s called Qingniu Mountain Range."

"Every time I see such scenes, I marvel at nature’s incomparable craftsmanship, capable of creating such bizarre and beautiful landscapes."

"This is also why I chose to join the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect in the first place. I don’t want to see cultivators destroying nature’s masterpieces with their own hands."

Lu Yang, standing behind Sect Master Kong, hesitated to speak. He wanted to say that these were not the works of nature but those of the Four Ancient Immortals, yet he worried that the truth would break Sect Master Kong’s heart.

Even Elder Brother Dai, under a thousand years old, couldn’t bear a few words of exaggeration, so what about Sect Master Kong who was over two thousand years old? Perhaps he was also somewhat sensitive?

"It’s not nature’s craftsmanship; it’s the craftsmanship of immortals. It was all carved out by Yingtian Immortal with his axe,"

Immortal Fairy thought Sect Master Kong was really uneducated, even misusing idioms; at least, Little Yang was literate.

For example, she just mentioned an axe and didn’t specify which kind, yet Little Yang knew it was a broad axe.

In contrast, this Mr. Kong, who appeared scholarly and full of ink, showed his ignorance the moment he spoke. Compared to Little Yang, the difference was clear.

The preparation work was completed, and two cultivators in the Spirit Transformation Late Stage finally arrived at the Qingniu Mountain Range.

On seeing Sect Master Kong, they were stunned first at why such a high-level cultivator would come here, but then, realizing the reason, they were elated.

To think that their reputation was so great that even Sect Master Kong came specially to watch their battle!

"Xiao Jin, what’s the background of the two fighters in this battle?" Sect Master Kong called over his chief disciple, Fang Jin, to ask.

"These two are old ancestors from a nearby influential family of a thousand years, one named Song Junhao, the other named Ning Zihao. When they were young, they teamed up and made a name for themselves, known as the ’Twin Talents.’

"Now, people respectfully call them `Twin Senior Talents`."

Sect Master Kong hesitated for a moment, "Are you sure that’s a term of respect?"

"At least it is locally."

"Alright then."

Sect Master Kong didn’t say much else. He waved his hand, signaling everyone to stand back. They were here to tidy up after the battle and didn’t want to interfere with the Twin Senior Talents’ fight.

Knowing that Sect Master Kong was present, the Twin Senior Talents seemed to revert back to their youthful, spirited selves, their cultivation techniques operating faster than usual.

"Old Song, make your move!"

"Then I won’t hold back—Hidden Dragon Do Not Use!"

"Green Wave Technique!"

Two veteran Cultivators at the late stage of Spirit Transformation took action in an extraordinary manner, as a earth Dragon burrowed out from below the ground, issuing bursts of dragon roars while the lake water churned endlessly.

Perhaps it was due to the stimulating presence of Sect Master Kong, both felt an unprecedentedly good condition, their minds more active than before, producing moves that effortlessly countered the opponent’s, each move concealing layers of deep calculations, strategically poised for victory, fully revealing their cunning!

The magic artifacts they brought out each had their wondrous uses, capable of producing unexpected effects at critical moments.

The two battled for a hundred rounds, fighting vigorously and passionately, yet still no victor was decided!

As spectators, Lu Yang and another stealthily yawned— the duel of the Twin Senior Talents had nothing new to offer, lacking enough power; even their battles at the Nascent Soul Late Stage were more impressive.

Finally, during the three-hundredth round, Song Junhao had a breakthrough in his mind state at a critical moment, touched the threshold of the Divinity Transformation Stage, reaching the Half-step Spirit Transformation Stage.

"I lost," Ning Zihao admitted defeat despondently.

Song Junhao said coldly, "According to the agreement, your Ning Family will cover the repair costs of this battle."

"Ah—" Ning Zihao sighed heavily. This would be a heavy financial blow.

The Twin Senior Talents wanted to ask Sect Master Kong for his comments on the battle, but after looking around, they found no one from the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect and had to give up and return to their respective families. freewebnσvel.cøm

After the battle, the members of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect emerged from the shadows, having hidden to avoid interfering with the fight.

The Qingniu Mountain Range was a sight of devastation, mountaintops shaved flat, lake water flowing backward, countless trees toppled—if anyone familiar with Qingniu Mountain Range were here, they wouldn’t recognize it.

This highlighted the importance of the disciples from the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect. They took out Recording Orbs, reconstructing the mountain range to its state before the battle.

Some disciples lifted up the lake water that had seeped into the soil with their hands and returned it to the lake, placing back fish and shrimp affected by the battle into the water as well, replenishing with fry where necessary as some were killed during the fight.

Another disciples, carrying shovels, dug up broken tree roots, then pinched tree seeds, flicking them into the prepared holes. Under the influence of the "Tree-Planting Sutra," the seeds grew swiftly into towering trees, the authentic Tree Planting Spell filling Lu Yang with envy.

Such proficiency clearly showed mastery of the Tree Planting Spell.

Sect Master Kong, noticing the unusual look in Lu Yang’s eyes, asked with a smile, "What, would you like to give it a try?"

"What would I need to do?"

Sect Master Kong pointed to a mountain that had moved more than ten meters and said, "Sword Cultivators excel at Sword Flight and are noted for object control; you can try controlling that mountain and move it back to its original place."

"Actually, the best way would be to use the Law of Heaven and Earth or Dharma Aspect, but you are only at the late stage of Spirit Transformation, not yet time to master these Supreme Great Divine Abilities..."

Then, Sect Master Kong witnessed an unbelievable scene, he saw Lu Yang transform into a wisp of clear gas and drift into the sky, an image full of divinity, akin to the legendary Feather Transformation Ascension!

Suddenly, Sect Master Kong felt the Spiritual Energy around him disappear completely, and the heavens and earth came alive, using the Cycle Power to sustain Lu Yang!

Then, with a thunderous sound, Lu Yang, hundreds of feet tall and dressed impeccably, landed!

The giant Lu Yang grinned at Sect Master Kong, "I just happen to know the Law of Heaven and Earth."

Lu Yang’s landing made such a commotion, it was hard not to notice him, causing all disciples of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect to stare open-mouthed at the giant Lu Yang, half-believing they were seeing an illusion.

"Isn’t it said that only a few in the Body Integration Realm can learn the Law of Heaven and Earth? Elder Brother Lu Yang is only in the Spirit Transformation Stage!"

"Yes, and Senior Brother Fang learned the Law of Heaven and Earth at the Early Integration Stage, already hailed as a genius that appears once in a thousand years."

Fang Jin looked at Lu Yang incredulously. Knowing the Law of Heaven and Earth was surprising enough, but what stunned him even more was how Lu Yang managed to grow while simultaneously enlarging his clothes as well.

He couldn’t help but doubt his own knowledge: "Could it be the Law of Heaven and Earth I learned is incomplete, and Junior Brother Lu has mastered the complete version?"

It was no wonder Fang Jin doubted his own learning, as the process of Lu Yang growing larger was indeed easy to deceive from an outsider’s perspective. Only Meng Jingzhou, who knew the ins and outs, understood how preposterous the process of Lu Yang’s growth was.

He still remembered when Lu Yang had to eat the soil from half an acre of land at the entrance to his abode to grow larger.

Meng Jingzhou couldn’t stand seeing Lu Yang steal the spotlight and stamped his foot with a cold snort, "Who can’t grow larger just the same."

The Supreme Dharma Form that reached heaven stood erect, holding a spear, clad in white robes, appearing like a scholar who had abandoned his pen for the military life, drawing gasps from the crowd.

"It’s a Dharma Aspect!"

"A Dharma Aspect never seen before!"

The disciples of Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect had seen many high-level cultivators battle with magic, and had seen or heard of various Dharma Aspects, but they had never seen the Dharma Aspect displayed by Meng Jingzhou.

The Supreme Pure Yang Dharma Image evolved from the Pure Yang Dharma Aspect into an even more extreme form, a Dharma Aspect uniquely mastered by Meng Jingzhou alone.

Two giants appeared in the Qingniu Mountain Range, and just by standing there, they emanated a pressure far greater than that of the Twin Senior Talents by dozens of times.

The two giants stared at each other, the atmosphere deadly, poised on a knife-edge.

Suddenly, the huge figure of Lu Yang moved. He fiercely collided with the mountains, pushing them back to their original positions.

Meng Jingzhou’s Dharma Aspect, on the other hand, scooped up a mound of dirt and piled it onto the flattened mountain top.

With two giants intervening, the restoration process was much faster than anticipated.

Upon seeing this scene, Sect Master Kong showed an expression as if deep in thought.

"These two haven’t reached the Body Integration Realm yet, but have already mastered the Law of Heaven and Earth and Dharma Aspects; they really are suitable for our Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect."

"It seems Third Zhang sending these two youngsters to me was not solely for punishment, but also to practice their Law of Heaven and Earth and Dharma Aspects."

"It looks like Elder Brother Dai wasn’t exaggerating when he praised these two junior brothers’ exceptional talents, unrivaled since ancient times," Fang Jin inwardly marveled, remembering that no cultivator he knew of had ever managed to successfully practice the Law of Heaven and Earth during the Divinity Transformation Stage.

Even Master of All Laws, famed as peerless genius, couldn’t achieve this.

"It’s just that I always feel there’s something off about Elder Brother Dai’s tone when he praises them, or am I overthinking it?"

As the disciples of Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect were already highly efficient, with the help of Lu Yang and the other, they restored Qingniu Mountain Range to its original state in less than two hours.

After returning to the sect, Fang Jin pondered for a while, wrote a letter, and sent it to Dai Bufan to inquire about the exact situation of the two Lu Yangs.

Sect Master Kong called the two Lu Yangs to the back mountain. Stroking his beard, the more he looked at the two, the more fitting he found them for their Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect, it was a pity they had joined the Seek Dao Sect.

"I didn’t expect you two to be capable of the Law of Heaven and Earth and Dharma Aspects, that really was beyond my expectations."

"Earlier, I noticed your movements while moving the mountain were a bit unpolished, which suggests you are not very familiar with these two grand divine abilities."

Sect Master Kong, valuing talent, was willing to teach Lu Yang and the other some skills.

"These two grand divine abilities are fundamentally the same, both involve enlargement, enhancing oneself in all aspects, it’s just that one can inevitably feel uneasy after such enlargement," he explained.

The two Lu Yangs nodded in agreement, as they had felt it themselves.

"It just so happens that I have dabbled in these two aspects of Great Divine Skill, and I can teach you a few tricks,"

"However, ultimately, the best way is to use your Dharma Aspects more and complete large-scale restoration tasks. It’s just that such tasks are rare—you might wait two months and still encounter none if you’re unlucky. But it’s not a big problem; our sect has many different terrains, you can practice here..."

At this moment, Fang Jin approached, "Master, I’ve just received a mission from the Dynasty. Two cultivators in the early stages of the Integration Realm fought using their magical powers, and it’s said the battle was fierce. Mountains turned into plains and rivers changed their courses. The Dynasty wants our sect to handle the aftermath."

Sect Master Kong was slightly surprised, "This is exactly the kind of large-scale restoration task I was talking about. Little Lu and Little Meng, go give it a try."

"Yes."

On the way following Fang Jin, Lu Yang and his companion came to understand the situation.

The cause was one of the Integration Period Cultivators who had obtained a mysterious Jade Scroll at an auction, unaware of the scroll’s origin, contents, and how to activate it. The other cultivator realized that this Jade Scroll was the legendary one containing heritage from a Pass Tribulation Cultivator, and after the auction concluded, he developed a desire to seize it.

After the battle had erupted, the Dynasty arrested the latter cultivator for robbery.

This act of legitimate defense meant that the government would fund the cleanup, which in practice meant the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect would step in.

Under Fang Jin’s guidance, they used the Law of Heaven and Earth and Dharma Aspect Mountain Shifting to alter the river’s course and perfect the restoration.

"Sect Master Kong, we have handled it," Lu Yang and his companion returned to the sect to continue their studies.

"Well done, your speed was fast. Where did I stop last time? Oh right, I was saying there is a trick to magnification..."

"Master, a Void Refinement Stage Cultivator has successfully passed his tribulation, rising to the rank of Unification True Monarch, but during the Thunder Tribulation, what was supposed to be a six-stage tribulation turned into nine stages. The added stages of the tribulation destroyed the protective Array Method, ruining the landscape for hundreds of miles, turning pasture into desert, and they’ve requested our intervention."

Sect Master Kong clicked his tongue, "Alright then, you two go there again, and when you come back, I’ll continue with the tricks."

Lu Yang and his companion smoothly completed the task. Just as they arrived at the gates of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect, they saw Sect Master Kong waiting with a piece of paper for the two of them.

"I just received another mission, saying that two Void Refinement Stage Cultivators have started fighting."

"These two Void Refinement Stage cultivators are half-brothers, both geniuses bearing unique talents. They were born with anomalies; the elder brother was born with an Immortal Bone in his finger, naturally containing Divine Abilities. The younger brother possessed an innate physique. Their father and the younger brother’s mother were true loves, hence he favored the younger brother, transplanted the elder brother’s Immortal Bone into the younger, giving him both the innate physique and the Immortal Bone."

Lu Yang roughly guessed what happened next, "Did the elder brother, even without the Immortal Bone, still rise to challenge his younger brother to prove he was the strongest?"

"No, instead, the elder brother pressed charges, and the government office transplanted the Immortal Bone back, arresting their parents. I estimate their parents won’t leave prison in their lifetimes."

"Feeling that his brother went too far, the brothers bore grudges, and their conflicts intensified, culminating in a life-and-death duel during their Void Refinement Stage, despite the inherent risks of their cultivation stage,"

"Who wins or loses is not our concern. You two go clean up the scene."

"All right."

Watching their departing figures, Sect Master Kong stroked his beard, his eyes flashing with a peculiar light.

"Strange, there weren’t so many high-level cultivator fights or large-scale restoration tasks before. How come there have been so many lately?"

He had always wanted the opportunity to teach the tricks, but never had the chance.

Meanwhile, Elder Brother Dai’s reply also arrived for Fang Jin, who opened the envelope, finding it contained only a sincere and urgent piece of advice which confused Fang Jin.

"Hurry up and buy insurance for your sect!"

"Buy insurance?" Fang Jin lifted the letter, tilting his head as he stared at it for a long time, trying to discern something else from the contents.

He found nothing.

"What does Elder Brother Dai mean? Is it some kind of code? But that shouldn’t be right, this isn’t some secret operation, why would there be a code?"

Fang Jin curbed the urge to soak the letter in water or roast it with fire. It was a regular letter, Elder Brother Dai probably wasn’t using a code.

"So he really wants me to buy insurance for the sect?"

Fang Jin was still baffled—he merely asked Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou what was going on, and somehow Dai Bufan just responded with "buy insurance."

With such a large sheet of paper, couldn’t you write a bit more? Is writing expensive for you?

Although confused, out of trust for Dai Bufan, Fang Jin dutifully headed to the Jingzhou Branch of the Land Money Trade Association.

The Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect was a Dynasty sect, and Fang Jin, holding the rank of Third Grade in official status, represented the sect externally. Additionally, being in the early stages of the Body Integration Realm, his visit to the Jingzhou branch warranted personal reception by the branch president.

"Brother Fang means your esteemed sect wants to purchase insurance?" The branch president was rather taken aback when he understood Fang Jin’s intention.

He had never heard of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect encountering any accidents. Why would they suddenly want to buy insurance?

"Brother Fang, what level of compensation are you considering for the sect insurance? We have five tiers here—Alpha, Beta, Gamma, Delta, and Epsilon. Normally, Gamma, which compensates sixty percent, is sufficient. If you’re determined, Beta compensating eighty percent is also an option, although very few opt for Alpha..."

"I’ll take Alpha, for a year first. How many spirit stones?"

Branch president grew more doubtful at Fang Jin’s decisiveness, and replied with a forced smile, "Brother Fang, you know the rules—we need to evaluate your sect’s risk over the past year before we can set the price."

"Don’t worry, brother, it’ll just take two days to get the results."

"Alright then."

After Fang Jin left, the branch president dispatched seven of the most professional evaluators to the Mountain and Sea Filling Sect. These seven evaluators were the veterans of the Jingzhou branch, abundantly experienced, and would have moved to the headquarters long ago if not for their attachment to the branch.

The dispatch of these seven cultivators illustrated the branch president’s consideration for the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect.

Two days later, the risk assessment results were ready.

The branch president grabbed a thick report, flipping directly to the conclusion on the last page:

"...The establishment of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect began twenty thousand years ago when an ancestor of the Dao Seeking Sect, acting as the governor of Qingzhou, ostensibly moved a flourishing nearby city into Qingzhou under the pretense of combat. This led the Dynasty to establish policies for terrain restoration and the founding of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect..."

"...Over the twenty thousand years, the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect faced no external invasions nor internal power struggles..."

"...The recent significant change in the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect is that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou from the Dao Seeking Sect are currently staying there."

"There are countless stories about Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou in the martial world, with hundreds of storytelling scripts available. However, according to investigations, most of these tales are fabricated by the Dao Seeking Sect Master, Daoist Buyu, for promotional purposes, and the real Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou did not experience these stories."

"Although Lu Yang participated in the Shu State Sword Tower’s Sword Inquiry Convention, during which the Sword Tower was destroyed by an attack from the Yingtian Immortal—a compensation claim that became a classic example of insurance failure for the Shu State Branch in the last hundred years—Lu Yang’s presence was merely coincidental and unrelated to the attack on the Sword Tower."

"Therefore, the appearance of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou does not increase the risk for the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect."

"The conclusion is... extremely low risk?"

The branch president frowned—this didn’t make sense. If there was no risk, why would Fang Jin buy insurance?

However, the risk assessment report could not be falsified. Since all seven elders unanimously agreed on the extremely low risk, there must be no risk.

Fang Jin managed to buy a first-class Sect insurance at the lowest price.

...

These days, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had been on their feet nonstop; each time they returned to the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect, they received new tasks, hurrying off in haste, unaware that the risk assessment cultivators had visited or that Elder Brother Fang had heedfully purchased insurance.

The two brothers initially enjoyed their efforts immensely, but gradually, the non-stop work wore them out both physically and mentally.

"This Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect is really that busy."

"The Dynasty is so stingy, not even sending extra help here."

Lu Yang shook his head, deeply disappointed with Prime Minister Emperor Xia’s management style of the Great Bean Dynasty; luckily, they were here as volunteers. If they hadn’t come, who knows how busy the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect would have been.

"Let it go, think positively; maybe Great Xia is just as short of people as our Great Bean Dynasty." Lu Yang consoled himself, his words expressing staunch loyalty to the Great Bean Dynasty, witnessed by heaven and earth, illuminated by the sun and moon.

However, Lu Yang had a special status, holding dual nationality; when Fairy Eternity was around, he was with the Great Bean Dynasty, and when Eldest Senior Sister was around, he was with the Great Xia Dynasty.

At this moment, Lu Yang transformed into a giant and began transplanting seedlings with a bent posture, as if he were arranging a mini landscape.

He first poked a hole in the ground with a finger, then cautiously planted a sapling into the hole, covering it with soil and watering it, being very careful to control his strength throughout the process, as a single mistake could ruin everything.

"Sect Master Kong is really right, practicing more is more effective than any technique."

Initially, Lu Yang couldn’t control his strength well and snapped the saplings, but now, as long as he was attentive, the saplings remained unharmed. freewebnøvel.coɱ

But that wasn’t enough; he aimed to plant trees effortlessly, with complete control over his strength.

Meng Jingzhou’s progress was similar to Lu Yang’s; as long as they were careful, there were no issues, but distractions led to failure.

After planting the trees, both of them had to move the mountains back to their original locations, which was also a meticulous task.

With their current strength, simply pushing the mountains back was no problem, but doing so would cause irreparable damage to the mountains, thus they also needed to control their strength when moving mountains.

"Finally done. Where’s our next stop?" Lu Yang wiped off his sweat, deflating like a balloon, spiritual essence leaking out, gradually shrinking back to his normal size.

Meng Jingzhou first helped his Dharma Aspect to take off clothes and fold them neatly before retracting the Dharma Aspect and picking up the clothes.

"Why is it so troublesome to dress and undress this Dharma Aspect?" Meng Jingzhou felt it was really inconvenient.

Lu Yang sighed, "What does this tell you? It shows that although those cultivators using Law of Heaven and Earth appear majestic in battle, once they revert, they have to sneakily and honestly fold their clothes."

This highlighted the advantage of Universe within the Sleeve, where clothes could be resized directly.

"Next stop is quite far, probably about twenty thousand miles from here."

As they spoke, intense fluctuations of spiritual energy came from above their heads.

Looking up, there were two Integration Period Cultivators battling, having flown from somewhere and stopping right there above them.

The might of Integration Period Cultivators was immense; to ordinary people, it might seem like the end of the world had come, causing them to tremble with fear.

These two Integration Period Cultivators battled fiercely, each move capable of tearing through the sky, crushing mountains, and evaporating lakes!

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were immediately anxious; after all the hard work they had put into organizing the terrain, letting it be destroyed by continued fighting was unacceptable!

"Liu Tianyang, today you and I must determine a victor!"

"Ye Zheng, do you think I am afraid of you?"

The two Integration Period Cultivators faced off with relentless ferocity, each move merciless, stirring ripples in the fabric of space that radiated outward in expanding circles.

They fought as they flew, eventually arriving at a location of pristine mountains and clear waters, where they simultaneously stopped flying and chose this place for their battle.

"Please wait a moment, esteemed seniors, might we change the location of our fight?" Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou hurriedly intervened.

Being Integration Period Cultivators was a rarity. Moreover, as a disciple of Daoist Buyu, Lu Yang had early on come to recognize the faces of almost all Integration Period Cultivators in Great Xia, these two included, known as Liu Tianyang and Ye Zheng, both at the Integration Mid-Stage, one specializing in Earth Magic and the other in Water Based Magic.

The two also recognized Lu Yang and his companion.

The disciple of Daoist Buyu, Lu Yang, and Meng Family’s Young Master, Meng Jingzhou.

Although Liu Tianyang and Ye Zheng recognized their identities, they still had no intention of stopping. They were locked in an intense magical duel, and one misstep could mean total defeat. Whoever paused first would surely lose.

Moreover, even though Lu Yang and his companion had big reputations as geniuses, they were ultimately juniors. What right did they have to interfere in their matters?

"Earth Dragon Roll..." Liu Tianyang uttered lightly, drawing talismans with one hand and forming seals with the other. The ground roared and shook violently, splitting open to reveal an Earth Dragon burrowing up from below.

Lu Yang watched, his eyes wide as the carefully tended landscape was destroyed. Merging Three Flavored True Fire with Golden Bird True Flame into the ultimate True Flame, he flew to the middle of Liu Tianyang and Ye Zheng and detonated it.

The casting process was interrupted, and the Earth Dragon, barely poking its head out of the ground, crumbled to dust.

Liu Tianyang and Ye Zheng, who were thoroughly enjoying their duel, were suddenly disrupted by the explosion of True Flame, their expressions instantly darkening.

"Lu Yang, I recognize you, Old Buyu’s little disciple. You just verbally intervened in the battle of your elders. Out of respect for Seek Dao Sect, I won’t hold it against you, but you have directly intervened, and this matter won’t be so simple!"

"Junior has no wish to interfere with the duel of the two seniors, but may I suggest that you take your fight into space?"

"You’re meddling too much," frowned Liu Tianyang. Why should he be ordered around by Old Buyu’s disciple?

Even if the storytelling blew Lu Yang’s reputation sky-high, Liu Tianyang knew it was all Buyu’s making—the old liar didn’t have a single truthful word, and with Lu Yang being his disciple, there was surely exaggeration. Lu Yang indeed had some skill, but he was not nearly as powerful as described in the stories, certainly not stronger than himself!

"Earth Dragon Flipping Sky!" Liu Tianyang shouted again, resuming the magic he had been using earlier. The scattered Earth Dragon reassembled, tearing through the terrain and erupting from the ground, charging towards Lu Yang.

Fang Jin took out fifty thousand Spirit Stones and handed them to Chen Yachong as the price for the map, eager to get this matter settled quickly.

In recent years, Fang Jin had made a significant profit from several big events organized by the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect, like the Qingzhou Festival and Hanshui City affairs. To him, fifty thousand Spirit Stones were just a drop in the bucket.

All debts cleared, Duan Qinghe’s beast skin IOU was no longer useful, so he simply gave it to Fang Jin, the final financier.

After wrapping up, Fang Jin, Lu Yang, and Meng Jingzhou returned to the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect. Fang Jin was somewhat caught between laughter and tears over this ridiculous situation.

"Senior Brother Fang, sometimes luck can solve problems," Lu Yang comforted.

Fang Jin thought about it and realized it was true, and his trip wasn’t entirely fruitless. He took out the Jade Silk Map, deciding to regard it as reclaiming an old map, just unsure when he would find the remaining old maps.

Suddenly, the Jade Silk Map, the box, and the beast skin all vibrated, as if triggering a resonance.

The box opened, and inside was a Jade Silk Map.

The beast skin tore, and out flew a Jade Silk Map.

The three Jade Silk Maps overlapped, revealing the true appearance of the real map.

Fang Jin: "..."

What was going on? Wasn’t it said that Chen Yachong had spent hundreds of years without being able to collect them all?

When had his luck become so good?

"This means that you, Senior Brother Fang, possess enormous good fortune."

Lu Yang stepped forward to congratulate him very tactfully, even happier than when he had gathered the map himself.

"Chen Yachong spent hundreds of years without obtaining the other two pieces of the map, yet Senior Brother Fang, you collected all of them in just one trip. What does this tell us? It shows that this map is fated to be yours!"

"Precisely, indeed, this must be an extremely auspicious sign." Meng Jingzhou also stepped forward to offer his congratulations; the two of them were so eloquent in their praise, lauding Fang Jin as if he were the chosen one.

The three pieces of the Jade Silk Map overlaid together revealed the true appearance of the map.

The map displayed a place called the Qinglian Mountain Range, with a circle drawn in the middle of the mountain range, which probably indicated something of significance there.

"Where is Qinglian Mountain Range?" Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou looked at each other in confusion. They were not familiar with the names of various mountain ranges. Where was it located in Great Xia?

"Qinglian Mountain Range..." Fang Jin furrowed his brows, vaguely recognizing the name.

"If I remember correctly, the Qinglian Mountain Range was a name from the Great Qian Period."

"During the Great Yu Era, it was called the Jiangbei Hills."

"During the Great Xia Period, it was called the Tianhe Plain."

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou wore odd expressions; it seemed like the changes involved more than just the name.

"That’s quite normal. Have you not considered? During the Great Qian and Great Yu periods, there were many cultivators, and their battles were even more chaotic, often altering the landscape," explained Fang Jin.

"Over three hundred thousand years driven by human forces, seas turned into mulberry fields; the maps of those times have long since changed."

Fang Jin was well-versed in ancient maps; he remembered clearly all the changes in geography from the Great Qian to the Great Xia periods.

This ancient map was useful only in the hands of Fang Jin; other cultivators who obtained it could only stare at it helplessly.

"Let’s go check out the Tianhe Plain." With the ancient map in hand, Fang Jin was enthused.

Since he had gathered the ancient map through incredible coincidences, perhaps as Junior Brother Lu had said, the treasures were destined to be his.

The Tianhe Plain was abundant with water and grass, with cattle and sheep everywhere. When the three of them landed, they even startled a flock of sheep that scattered, leaving behind a field covered with droppings.

Some of the lambs unafraid, bleating as they charged towards the three men, were quickly snatched away by the ewes.

Fang Jin gestured; the site marked on the ancient map was rather large: "It should be around here."

He released his Spiritual Sense, scanning every inch of land within the range and discovered clues beneath the ground.

"It seems there is a Secret Realm underground; let’s dig and have a look," he suggested.

"Why bother digging? Just have Old Lu consume the dirt," proposed Meng Jingzhou.

Lu Yang kicked over; this place was full of sheep droppings, I’ll eat your grandpa.

Fang Jin and Lu Yang both employed the Law of Heaven and Earth while Meng Jingzhou deployed his Dharma Aspect; the three giants squatted down to dig the earth.

After digging about two thousand meters deep, the three of them encountered a stone that seemed embedded into the space itself, static even when the earth below was removed. They tried moving the stone but to no avail.

Fang Jin channeled spiritual essence into the stone, and the stone revealed complex patterns, ancient and mysterious. The stone exerted a powerful suction force, pulling all three of them in.

When the three regained their senses, all was pitch black around them.

"It seems that this place suppresses Spiritual Sense; we can’t utilize it here."

Meng Jingzhou looked up and ignited the Pure Yang Fire to illuminate the space.

"A cave?"

The three discovered they were in a damp and closed cavern, with no hint of a breeze, indicating the cavern was sealed.

"Is there a treasure in here?"

Just as Fang Jin was about to take a step forward, he suddenly heard Lu Yang’s voice.

"Senior Brother Fang, don’t move forward!"

Fang Jin abruptly stopped in his tracks, "What’s wrong?"

"There’s a restriction in front of you, if you continue, it will trigger the restriction, and it’s very dangerous!" Lu Yang warned solemnly.

Fang Jin jumped in fright and quickly retracted his left foot, crouching down to inspect the ground, he indeed found some incomprehensible runes, although they were fragmented.

"It seems this cave is filled with restrictions, but someone forced their way in and destroyed these runes," Lu Yang said, passing off the words of Immortal Fairy as his own speculation.

Even the runes that had been damaged contained an extremely terrifying power that was beyond their capability to touch.

"This method of setting up restrictions is like that of the Time Immortal," Immortal Fairy pondered, stroking her chin, "Since his true form is a tree, he always likes to bury things underground, making them very troublesome to find."

"Little Yang, you go ahead and walk. An idiot has already explored the way for you, and the obstructive restrictions have been destroyed. Just avoid touching the restrictions, and you’ll be fine."

"The trinket at the end of the cave should be created by the Time Immortal."

Lu Yang carefully bypassed the restrictions, leading Fang Jin and Meng Jingzhou to the deepest part of the cave, finding a small metal box roughly the size of a fist, placed on a high plinth.

Fang Jin used spiritual essence to form a large hand, taking the metal box from a distance. The box felt heavy in his hands.

"Is this made of Immortal Gold?!"

Fang Jin was astonished, for if it was made of Immortal Gold, then the metal box was at least a half-immortal crafted Immortal Treasure, and there was even a tiny chance it was crafted by an Immortal!

"Fairy, what is the purpose of this metal box crafted by the Time Immortal?"

Immortal Fairy pondered with frustration, "The little gadgets made by the Time Immortal look quite similar, and I always get them mixed up."

"However, judging by the style of this metal box, it seems to be an artifact that can slow down time."

Lu Yang was startled; an artifact that could slow down time sounded extraordinary. As expected of the Time Immortal, the effects of his crafted artifacts were so powerful.

"To use this box, there is an incantation, ’Immortal as Supreme, Time as King’, no, that’s not right. It’s ’Stars revolve as I command, the four seasons change in the blink of an eye.’ Also not right, what was it?"

"Why not just ask the Time Immortal?" suggested Lu Yang, thinking that if remembering was difficult, why not ask the person himself.

"No need, that’s too much trouble. Just open the ’Immortal’s Quotations’, pick out the words the Time Immortal has said, and read them one by one; the incantation will definitely be in there."

"...Alright then."

Fang Jin flipped through it for a long time, not knowing how to use the metal box, "Forget it, the master and the Supreme Elder have seen much and know much, let’s take it back for them to see."

The metal box belonged to the Time Immortal, and logically should be returned to its owner, but with Lu Yang’s status, it wasn’t appropriate for him to keep the box; it needed the Sect’s high-level members to step forward.

Lu Yang thought that he would have to speak to the Eldest Senior Sister and have her figure out a way to return it to the Time Immortal.

"Old Lu, there’s nothing dangerous about this metal box, is there?" Meng Jingzhou asked, uneasy.

"There shouldn’t be any danger. This is a great item left behind by the Time Immortal."

"That’s good then."

...

"Xiao Tian, do you think I was too harsh by making Little Meng and Little Lu do two months of pointless work at the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect as a punishment?" The Third Elder had been troubled recently, wanting to discuss it with Yun Zhi, but since she couldn’t be found, she instead went to consult with the Third Senior Sister, Gan Tian.

Gan Tian thought to herself that she had assumed the Elder was using this opportunity to send them to learn the Law of Heaven and Earth and Dharma Aspect at the sect, but in reality, was it just a punishment?

"Should I call the Second-in-command back? I’ll go call her!" Yun Mengmeng volunteered eagerly.

Recently, Si Lei God Lord has been rather restless, and it’s not because his good friend Si Chen God Lord has disappeared without a trace, nor is it a big deal that the treasure map he drew was lost.

The biggest problem he faces now is that he doesn’t know the location of the Ancient Secret Realm.

Thirty thousand years ago, he came across a secret realm left by Fairy Eternity from ancient times, but the realm was so heavily restricted that he dared not touch it, yet he couldn’t bear to give up on such an opportunity.

Due to the long duration of his slumber, coupled with the influence of the Power of Faith, there was a possibility of partial memory loss upon awakening.

Therefore, he drew a map before his deep sleep and split it into three parts, scattering it among the common folk to ensure that even if someone got their hands on one part, they wouldn’t be able to piece together the complete map.

Naturally, he also had a secret method to know the whereabouts of the map.

Upon awakening, he remembered the location of that Ancient Secret Realm, situated in Lotus Mountain; thus, the map became something he could take or leave.

"Where is Qinglian Mountain rage?"

After waking up from a long sleep, not only had dynasties changed twice, but the very landscape had undergone drastic transformations — without any landmarks, remembering the location of Qinglian Mountain was utterly useless.

"Can’t those cultivators restore the original geography after their battles!" Si Lei God Lord was furious; he didn’t revert the landscape himself because he was a Semi-Immortal, but why couldn’t those cultivators beneath the level of Semi-Immortal restore it!

The secret realm left by the Time Immortal ah, it’s very likely to contain Immortal Artifacts related to time! If he were to possess a Time Immortal Artifact, who among the Semi-Immortals could be his match?

He had recently heard some good news that might lead him to find Qinglian Mountain.

"It is said that the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect houses historical maps of the Central Continent from all dynasties; they surely have the location of Qinglian Mountain!"

Si Lei God Lord left the Fairy Palace and headed straight for the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect.

"Is this the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect? They sure picked a nice place." Si Lei God Lord saw that the sect was situated by a mountain and water, in a beautiful environment, and he even felt like living there.

As a Semi-Immortal, his whereabouts were a mystery; the sect had no idea he had arrived.

He walked into the Scripture Pavilion, where books were piled up like mountains; it would be impossible to find anything about Qinglian Mountain quickly.

The cultivator guarding the Scripture Pavilion was a bit interesting to watch, but that was about it.

"Just at the Early Tribulation Stage." Si Lei God Lord casually laughed, and even as he walked past the old guardian of the Scripture Pavilion, the elder didn’t notice him.

In the Great Qian Period, the Early Tribulation Stage would barely qualify to be his subordinate.

However, since it was still the Transcendence Tribulation Stage, Si Lei God Lord didn’t dare to make a big commotion and, not willing to search with his Spiritual Sense, had to flip through the books one by one.

When he reached the fourth floor, he noticed some commotion below.

"Master, do you recognize this iron lump?" Sect Master Kong, holding an Immortal Gold Box, went to the old man guarding the Scripture Pavilion, Jin Wenzhang, the Supreme Elder of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect.

Fang Jin, Lu Yang, and Meng Jingzhou followed behind him.

"What is this thing?" The Supreme Elder examined the Immortal Gold Box, knocking and tapping it, and even when he injected spiritual essence into the box, he got repelled.

"You don’t recognize it either?" Sect Master Kong could not identify or figure out how to use the Immortal Gold Box and had sought the Supreme Elder; he hadn’t expected that even the Supreme Elder would not recognize it.

"This iron lump, together with Lu Martial Nephew, and Meng Martial Nephew, was accidentally found on an ancient map from the Great Qian Period. The map indicated that something was buried in Qinglian Mountain Range. It was Xiao Jin, who reads a lot, who recognized that the Qinglian Mountain of the Great Qian Period is the current Tianhe Plain, and that’s how they found this Immortal Gold Box."

"It seems you’ve not wasted your time soaking up knowledge in the Scripture Pavilion, you little guy." The Supreme Elder chuckled, stroking his beard. He had a very favorable impression of this junior.

Qinglian Mountain!

Upon hearing the familiar term, Si Lei God Lord immediately became agitated and inadvertently leaked his presence.

"Who’s there!" The Supreme Elder raised his head and roared like an enraged old lion, unable to believe that someone had dared to sneak into the Scripture Pavilion right under his watch!

Roar—

Buddhist Lion Roar!

"This object should be mine by right!"

Si Lei God Lord was equally furious; after searching for years and failing to find the location, to think that a junior had found it and even taken the Time Immortal Artifact that was meant for him!

Unforgivable!

Si Lei God Lord transformed his hand into golden thunder, reaching out to grab the Immortal Gold Box; the Supreme Elder, however, had no intention of letting him have his way.

"Tianqing!"

The Supreme Elder bellowed in anger, and a metallic dragon with a gleaming luster burst forth from the ground. The dragon raised its head high and directly topped the Si Lei God Lord out of the Scripture Pavilion!

If they were to fight in the Scripture Pavilion, no matter who won, the Scripture Pavilion would be destroyed in an instant!

"Everyone, retreat!" Sect Master Kong knew that a battle at the Tribulation-Passing Level was not something he could handle. All he could do now was to have his disciples quickly leave the sect to avoid being affected!

Si Lei God Lord didn’t regard the Supreme Elder as a concern at all.

"Thunder as heavy as mountains!"

Thunder roared and lightning flashed, and in an instant, the entire Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect was engulfed in thunder, with thick as water jars thunderbolts rampaging through the sect, leaving huge pits upon striking the ground and even causing the land to crack, the intermittent flashes lighting up Si Lei God Lord’s countenance in an especially daunting way.

He possessed the outline of a Tribulation Dao Fruit. As long as the Yingtian Immortal remained absent, he was the embodiment of thunder, the nemesis of all cultivators!

"A Semi-Immortal?!" The Supreme Elder instantly recognized that this kind of thunder could not be unleashed by someone at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage; it must be the power of a Dao Fruit Outline.

"So what if it’s a Semi-Immortal? Even the Half-Immortals of Great Qian don’t dare to run wild within the bounds of Great Xia!" The Supreme Elder, despite knowing the gap between them, showed no fear at all. He too had a fierce temper when he was young and would often get into fights with those who gave assignments.

The Supreme Elder grew taller against the wind, transforming into a giant nine thousand zhang high, with the metallic dragon entwined around his arms.

The giant’s feet stomped on the earth, his head towered into the thunder, holding a massive hammer, he charged at Si Lei God Lord to bring it smashing down!

"Law of Heaven and Earth, Heaven and Earth Flipping!"

This one strike would flatten even a hundred thousand mountains!

"Ignorant youngster, you do not recognize the might of heaven!" Si Lei God Lord looked on coldly at the Supreme Elder. What use was increasing one’s size? Without sufficient realm, no technique could compensate.

In front of the outline of a Tribulation Dao Fruit, before the might of heaven, everything was useless.

"Nine Heavens Demon Sweeping Divine Thunder."

Nine layers of the vast sky appeared, each layer higher than the last, with the Demon Sweeping Divine Thunder sweeping mightily across, cleansing the world of its filth and demons.

And who was deemed a demon, was decided solely by the Si Lei God Lord.

"You are the demon."

Thus he decreed, as if he had ordained the identity of the Supreme Elder, with the Nine Heavens Demon Sweeping Divine Thunder locking onto the Supreme Elder, nine different types of Divine Thunders fell one after another!

Lu Yang was reciting nervously from the "Immortal’s Quotations," the words of the Time Immortal.

According to Fairy Eternity, as long as one could recite the incantation correctly, one could use the Immortal Gold Box. If the Supreme Elder had the help of the Immortal Gold Box, he would certainly be able to contend with Si Lei God Lord.

With the second to last Divine Thunder falling and the Supreme Elder seemingly unable to resist, Lu Yang gritted his teeth and directly threw the Immortal Gold Box over, blocking the Divine Thunder.

He recited the final phrase of the Time Immortal from the "Immortal’s Quotations" in the Ancient Language.

"The Great Dao is boundless, but time alone is supreme."

The Immortal Gold Box surface instantly lit up with various mystical patterns, imbued with the power of time, drawing in anyone who glanced at it, unable to extricate themselves.

A burly figure emerged from the Immortal Gold Box.

"Finally able to come out."

The last Divine Thunder fell, striking the burly man.

"Who the hell is striking me!"

The burly figure roared angrily, and with just one shout, its power matched the Buddhist Lion Roar of the Supreme Elder! ƒreewebɳovel.com

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, upon seeing the burly figure, were stunned in unison, rubbing their eyes, almost thinking it was an illusion.

"Celestial Master Guiyuan?"

Fairy Eternity, upon seeing the patterns lighting up on the Immortal Gold Box, finally remembered the purpose of this box.

"This is a box made by the Time Immortal while studying the Time Dao Fruit. The flow of time inside the box is different from the outside; one day of Cultivation inside it is equivalent to a year in the outside world."

Just as Lu Yang was about to nod in admiration of how incredible the box was, he suddenly realized something was amiss.

What’s the use of this damn box!
